详细信息
────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
第一篇　使徒的教训─神在新约中的整个说话，关于神新约的经纶
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　在五旬节那天得救的三千信徒，坚定持续在使徒的教训和交通里，持续擘饼和祷告─徒二41～42。
一　教训和交通成为一组，是使徒的教训和交通，与神的经纶有直接的关系，乃是为着保守召会，就是基督身体的一；二者都是惟一的：
１　使徒的教训是维持同心合意的因素─徒二42上，46上。
２　我们若将自己限制于使徒的教训之内，就是限制在关于神新约经纶的教训之内，我们就会被保守在一里，也会有一条道路，为着一个目标。
３　在召会中应当只有一个惟一的教训─使徒的教训；不仅如此，也应当只有一个惟一的交通，而这交通是由使徒的教训所产生的。
４　任何在使徒的交通之外的交通，都是分裂的；我们的交通必须在使徒的交通之内。
二　擘饼和祷告成为第二组，是信徒之基督徒生活的实行。
贰　新约的整个教训，就是使徒的教训，乃是神在子里向祂新约子民的说话，神的谕言─来一1～2。
一　宇宙中有一件美妙的事，就是神的说话─来一2：
１　在新约时代，神不是多分多方，或借着申言者，向祂的子民说话。
２　在新约时代，神只在子这一个人位里说话。
二　神首先在为人的子里，在四福音里说话─约十四10，五24，十六12，十30。
三　其次，神借着使徒们，在那成为灵的子里，在使徒行传和二十一卷书信（罗马书到犹大书）里说话─约十六12～15，太二十八19～20，来二3～4，彼后三15～16，西一25～27。
四　第三，神借着使徒约翰，在那成为七灵的子里，在启示录里说话─启一2，4，二1，7。
五　神在新约教训里的说话，是借着保罗和约翰完成的：
１　神的话作为启示出来的奥秘，是借着保罗得到完成的─西一25～27。
２　全部新约是借着约翰的著作完成的─启二十二18～19。
六　在子里的这个说话，就是使徒的教训，并不强调诸如洗脚、受浸、蒙头等类的事；这些都不包含在关于神永远经纶之新约启示中，那些基本、内在、中心和基础的事里面。
叁　使徒的教训是神新约经纶的惟一神圣启示，从神的成为肉体到新耶路撒冷的终极完成，由基督在三个神圣奥秘的时期里丰满的职事所完成，为着成就神永远的经纶：
一　第一个时期，成肉体的时期，乃是为使基督将神带到人里，在人性里彰显神，并完成祂法理的的救赎。
二　第二个时期，总括的时期，乃是为使基督生为神的长子，成为赐生命的灵，并为着祂的身体重生信徒。
三　第三个时期，加强的时期，乃是为使基督加强祂生机的救恩，产生得胜者，并终极完成新耶路撒冷。
肆　使徒的教训是完满福音的内容，不是仅仅包含新约的一部分，乃是包含整个新约─罗一1～4。
伍　使徒的教训是召会的宪法：召会必须持守，并完全在其管制之下：
一　使徒的教训是基督徒信仰的宪法─犹3，提前一19，六12，提后四7。
二　使徒的教训是召会的宪法，应当普遍的在各处各召会中，同样的教导─林前四17，七17：
１　使徒的教训是为着神的经纶，而这教训是主耶稣健康的话─提前一3～4，六3。
２　一切教训都必须受使徒教训之界限和范围的限制。
３　基督教因为使徒教训界限之外的许多教训，而有许多的路。
４　今天基督徒中间一切的难处、分裂和混乱，都是由于一件事─不是只注重使徒教训的惟一启示。
三　在召会中，应当只有一个惟一的教训，就是使徒的教训，而没有不同的教训。
四　这个宪法，就像每个宪法一样，必须正确的加以解释。
陆　使徒不许可任何与使徒教训不同的教训：
一　使徒不许可在惟一信仰之外的其它信仰─加一7～9。
二　使徒不许可那些越过基督之教训的教训─约贰9～11。
三　使徒不许可不同的教训，包括旧约时代中那些与神经纶不同的教训─提前一3～4。
四　使徒把一切与神新约经纶的惟一启示不同的教训，看作是教训之风─弗四14。
五　任何人都不可任意曲解神的圣别著作，而该正确、正直、毫不曲解的解开─彼后三16，提后二15。
柒　召会的蒙恩，在于召会坚定持续在使徒的教训和交通里─徒二42，46，六7。
捌　断定正确的职事，就是神新约经纶的职事，决定的因素乃是使徒的教训：
一　一个人若教导使徒的教训，他的工作就是在新约的职事里。
二　惟一的职事乃是神所命定，照着使徒教训的职事。
参读　使徒的教训；使徒的教训与新约中的领导；长老训练，第七册；同心合意为着主的行动，第五、八章；神命定实行新约经纶的路，第十六至十九章；如何作同工与长老，并如何履行同工与长老的义务，第一至三篇；使徒行传生命读经，第十二篇；新约的职事以及使徒的教训和交通(中文尚未出书)。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message One
The Apostles' Teaching— the Entire Speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament Economy
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　The three thousand believers who were saved on the day of Pentecost continued steadfastly in the teaching and the fellowship of the apostles, in the breaking of bread and the prayers—Acts 2:41-42:
A.　The teaching and the fellowship form one group which is of the apostles and related directly to God's economy for the keeping of the oneness of the church, the Body of Christ; both are unique:
1.　The teaching of the apostles was the holding factor of the one accord—Acts 2:42a, 46a.
2.　If we limit ourselves to the apostles' teaching, the teaching concerning God's New Testament economy, we will be kept in oneness and will have one way for one goal.
3.　In the church there should be only one unique teaching—the teaching of the apostles; furthermore, there should be one unique fellowship, which is produced by the apostles' teaching.
4.　Any fellowship outside the fellowship of the apostles is divisive; our fellowship must be inside the fellowship of the apostles.
B.　The breaking of bread and the prayers form a second group and are practices of the believers' Christian life.
II.　The entire teaching of the New Testament, which is the apostles' teaching, is God's speaking, God's oracle, in the Son to His New Testament people—Heb. 1:1-2:
A.　In the universe there is a marvelous matter, God's speaking—Heb. 1:2:
1.　In the age of the New Testament God does not speak to His people in many portions and in many ways or through the prophets.
2.　In the New Testament age God only speaks in one person, the Son.
B.　God firstly spoke in the Son as a man in the four Gospels—John 14:10; 5:24; 16:12; 10:30.
C.　God secondly spoke in the Son as the Spirit through the apostles in Acts and the twenty-one Epistles (Romans through Jude)—John 16:12-15; Matt. 28:19-20; Heb. 2:3-4; 2 Pet. 3:15-16; Col. 1:25-27.
D.　God thirdly spoke in the Son as the seven Spirits through the apostle John in Revelation—Rev. 1:2, 4; 2:1, 7.
E.　God's speaking in the teaching of the New Testament was completed through Paul and John:
1.　The word of God as the revealed mystery was completed through Paul—Col. 1:25-2b.
2.　The entire New Testament was completed by John's writings—Rev. 22:18-19.
F.　This speaking in the Son, the apostles' teaching, does not stress matters such as foot-washing, baptism, head covering, etc.; these are not the basic, intrinsic, central, and elementary things contained in the New Testament revelation concerning God's eternal economy.
III.　The teaching of the apostles is the unique divine revelation of God's New Testament economy from the incarnation of God to the consummation of the New Jerusalem, carried out by the full ministry of Christ in three divine and mystical stages for the fulfillment of God's eternal economy:
A.　The first stage, the stage of incarnation, is for Christ to bring God into man, to express God in humanity, and to accomplish His judicial redemption.
B.　The second stage, the stage of inclusion, is for Christ to be begotten as God's firstborn Son, to become the life-giving Spirit, and to regenerate the believers for His Body.
C.　The third stage, the stage of intensification, is for Christ to intensify His organic salvation, to produce the overcomers, and to consummate the New Jerusalem.
IV.The apostles' teaching is the contents of the full gospel of God, comprising not merely a part of the New Testament, but the entire New Testament.
V.　The apostles' teaching is the church's constitution; the church must hold it and be under it absolutely:
A.　The apostles' teaching is the constitution of the Christian faith—Jude 3; 1 Tim. 1:19; 6:12; 2 Tim. 4:7.
B.　The apostles' teaching, as the church's constitution, should be universally taught everywhere in every church in the same way—1 Cor. 4:17; 7:17:
1.　The teaching of the apostles is for God's economy, and the teaching is the healthy words of the Lord Jesus—1 Tim. 1:3-4; 6:3.
2.　All teachings must be restricted by the limit and sphere of the apostles' teaching.
3.　Christianity has many ways because of the many teachings outside the limit of the apostles' teaching.
4.　All the problems, divisions, and confusion among Christians today are due to one thing—not caring only for the unique revelation of the apostles' teaching.
C.　In the church there should be one unique teaching, the apostles' teaching, not different teachings.
D.　This constitution, like every constitution, must be properly interpreted.
VI.　Any teaching that was different from the apostles' teaching was not allowed by the apostles:
A.　No other belief besides the unique faith was allowed by the apostles—Gal. 1:7-9.
B.　Teachings that went beyond the teaching of Christ were not allowed by the apostles—2 John 9-11.
C.　The different teachings, including those from the Old Testament dispensation that were different from God's economy, were not allowed by the apostles—1 Tim. 1:3-4.
D.　All teachings that were different from the unique revelation of God's New Testament economy were considered by the apostles to be winds of teaching—Eph. 4:14.
E.　God's holy writing should not be twisted by anyone in any way but rather unfolded rightly and straightly without any distortion—2 Pet. 3:16; 2 Tim. 2:15.
VII.　The blessing of the church is dependent upon the church's continuing steadfastly in the teaching and fellowship of the apostles—Acts 2:42, 46; 6:7.
VIII.　The deciding factor in determining the right ministry, which is the ministry of God's New Testament economy, is the teaching of the apostles:
A.　A person's work is in the New Testament ministry if he teaches the teaching of the apostles.
B.　The unique ministry is the ministry ordained by God according to the apostles' teaching.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第一篇　使徒的教训─神在新约中的整个说话，关于神新约的经纶
The Apostles' Teaching— the Entire Speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament Economy
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
壹　在五旬节那天得救的三千信徒，坚定持续在使徒的教训和交通里，持续擘饼和祷告─徒二41～42。
I.　The three thousand believers who were saved on the day of Pentecost continued steadfastly in the teaching and the fellowship of the apostles, in the breaking of bread and the prayers—Acts 2:41-42:
一　教训和交通成为一组，是使徒的教训和交通，与神的经纶有直接的关系，乃是为着保守召会，就是基督身体的一；二者都是惟一的：
A.　The teaching and the fellowship form one group which is of the apostles and related directly to God's economy for the keeping of the oneness of the church, the Body of Christ; both are unique:
１　使徒的教训是维持同心合意的因素─徒二42上，46上。
1.　The teaching of the apostles was the holding factor of the one accord—Acts 2:42a, 46a.
２　我们若将自己限制于使徒的教训之内，就是限制在关于神新约经纶的教训之内，我们就会被保守在一里，也会有一条道路，为着一个目标。
2.　If we limit ourselves to the apostles' teaching, the teaching concerning God's New Testament economy, we will be kept in oneness and will have one way for one goal.
３　在召会中应当只有一个惟一的教训─使徒的教训；不仅如此，也应当只有一个惟一的交通，而这交通是由使徒的教训所产生的。
3.　In the church there should be only one unique teaching—the teaching of the apostles; furthermore, there should be one unique fellowship, which is produced by the apostles' teaching.
４　任何在使徒的交通之外的交通，都是分裂的；我们的交通必须在使徒的交通之内。
4.　Any fellowship outside the fellowship of the apostles is divisive; our fellowship must be inside the fellowship of the apostles.
二　擘饼和祷告成为第二组，是信徒之基督徒生活的实行。
B.　The breaking of bread and the prayers form a second group and are practices of the believers' Christian life.
贰　新约的整个教训，就是使徒的教训，乃是神在子里向祂新约子民的说话，神的谕言─来一1～2。
II.　The entire teaching of the New Testament, which is the apostles' teaching, is God's speaking, God's oracle, in the Son to His New Testament people—Heb. 1:1-2:
一　宇宙中有一件美妙的事，就是神的说话─来一2：
A.　In the universe there is a marvelous matter, God's speaking—Heb. 1:2:
１　在新约时代，神不是多分多方，或借着申言者，向祂的子民说话。
1.　In the age of the New Testament God does not speak to His people in many portions and in many ways or through the prophets.
２　在新约时代，神只在子这一个人位里说话。
2.　In the New Testament age God only speaks in one person, the Son.
二　神首先在为人的子里，在四福音里说话─约十四10，五24，十六12，十30。
B.　God firstly spoke in the Son as a man in the four Gospels—John 14:10; 5:24; 16:12; 10:30.
三　其次，神借着使徒们，在那成为灵的子里，在使徒行传和二十一卷书信（罗马书到犹大书）里说话─约十六12～15，太二十八19～20，来二3～4，彼后三15～16，西一25～27。
C.　God secondly spoke in the Son as the Spirit through the apostles in Acts and the twenty-one Epistles (Romans through Jude)—John 16:12-15; Matt. 28:19-20; Heb. 2:3-4; 2 Pet. 3:15-16; Col. 1:25-27.
四　第三，神借着使徒约翰，在那成为七灵的子里，在启示录里说话─启一2，4，二1，7。
D.　God thirdly spoke in the Son as the seven Spirits through the apostle John in Revelation—Rev. 1:2, 4; 2:1, 7.
五　神在新约教训里的说话，是借着保罗和约翰完成的：
E.　God's speaking in the teaching of the New Testament was completed through Paul and John:
１　神的话作为启示出来的奥秘，是借着保罗得到完成的─西一25～27。
1.　The word of God as the revealed mystery was completed through Paul—Col. 1:25-2b.
２　全部新约是借着约翰的著作完成的─启二十二18～19。
2.　The entire New Testament was completed by John's writings—Rev. 22:18-19.
六　在子里的这个说话，就是使徒的教训，并不强调诸如洗脚、受浸、蒙头等类的事；这些都不包含在关于神永远经纶之新约启示中，那些基本、内在、中心和基础的事里面。
F.　This speaking in the Son, the apostles' teaching, does not stress matters such as foot-washing, baptism, head covering, etc.; these are not the basic, intrinsic, central, and elementary things contained in the New Testament revelation concerning God's eternal economy.
叁　使徒的教训是神新约经纶的惟一神圣启示，从神的成为肉体到新耶路撒冷的终极完成，由基督在三个神圣奥秘的时期里丰满的职事所完成，为着成就神永远的经纶：
III.　The teaching of the apostles is the unique divine revelation of God's New Testament economy from the incarnation of God to the consummation of the New Jerusalem, carried out by the full ministry of Christ in three divine and mystical stages for the fulfillment of God's eternal economy:
一　第一个时期，成肉体的时期，乃是为使基督将神带到人里，在人性里彰显神，并完成祂法理的的救赎。
A.　The first stage, the stage of incarnation, is for Christ to bring God into man, to express God in humanity, and to accomplish His judicial redemption.
二　第二个时期，总括的时期，乃是为使基督生为神的长子，成为赐生命的灵，并为着祂的身体重生信徒。
B.　The second stage, the stage of inclusion, is for Christ to be begotten as God's firstborn Son, to become the life-giving Spirit, and to regenerate the believers for His Body.
三　第三个时期，加强的时期，乃是为使基督加强祂生机的救恩，产生得胜者，并终极完成新耶路撒冷。
C.　The third stage, the stage of intensification, is for Christ to intensify His organic salvation, to produce the overcomers, and to consummate the New Jerusalem.
肆　使徒的教训是完满福音的内容，不是仅仅包含新约的一部分，乃是包含整个新约─罗一1～4。
IV.The apostles' teaching is the contents of the full gospel of God, comprising not merely a part of the New Testament, but the entire New Testament.
伍　使徒的教训是召会的宪法：召会必须持守，并完全在其管制之下：
V.　The apostles' teaching is the church's constitution; the church must hold it and be under it absolutely:
一　使徒的教训是基督徒信仰的宪法─犹3，提前一19，六12，提后四7。
A.　The apostles' teaching is the constitution of the Christian faith—Jude 3; 1 Tim. 1:19; 6:12; 2 Tim. 4:7.
二　使徒的教训是召会的宪法，应当普遍的在各处各召会中，同样的教导─林前四17，七17：
B.　The apostles' teaching, as the church's constitution, should be universally taught everywhere in every church in the same way—1 Cor. 4:17; 7:17:
１　使徒的教训是为着神的经纶，而这教训是主耶稣健康的话─提前一3～4，六3。
1.　The teaching of the apostles is for God's economy, and the teaching is the healthy words of the Lord Jesus—1 Tim. 1:3-4; 6:3.
２　一切教训都必须受使徒教训之界限和范围的限制。
2.　All teachings must be restricted by the limit and sphere of the apostles' teaching.
３　基督教因为使徒教训界限之外的许多教训，而有许多的路。
3.　Christianity has many ways because of the many teachings outside the limit of the apostles' teaching.
４　今天基督徒中间一切的难处、分裂和混乱，都是由于一件事─不是只注重使徒教训的惟一启示。
4.　All the problems, divisions, and confusion among Christians today are due to one thing—not caring only for the unique revelation of the apostles' teaching.
三　在召会中，应当只有一个惟一的教训，就是使徒的教训，而没有不同的教训。
C.　In the church there should be one unique teaching, the apostles' teaching, not different teachings.
四　这个宪法，就像每个宪法一样，必须正确的加以解释。
D.　This constitution, like every constitution, must be properly interpreted.
陆　使徒不许可任何与使徒教训不同的教训：
VI.　Any teaching that was different from the apostles' teaching was not allowed by the apostles:
一　使徒不许可在惟一信仰之外的其它信仰─加一7～9。
A.　No other belief besides the unique faith was allowed by the apostles—Gal. 1:7-9.
二　使徒不许可那些越过基督之教训的教训─约贰9～11。
B.　Teachings that went beyond the teaching of Christ were not allowed by the apostles—2 John 9-11.
三　使徒不许可不同的教训，包括旧约时代中那些与神经纶不同的教训─提前一3～4。
C.　The different teachings, including those from the Old Testament dispensation that were different from God's economy, were not allowed by the apostles—1 Tim. 1:3-4.
四　使徒把一切与神新约经纶的惟一启示不同的教训，看作是教训之风─弗四14。
D.　All teachings that were different from the unique revelation of God's New Testament economy were considered by the apostles to be winds of teaching—Eph. 4:14.
五　任何人都不可任意曲解神的圣别著作，而该正确、正直、毫不曲解的解开─彼后三16，提后二15。
E.　God's holy writing should not be twisted by anyone in any way but rather unfolded rightly and straightly without any distortion—2 Pet. 3:16; 2 Tim. 2:15.
柒　召会的蒙恩，在于召会坚定持续在使徒的教训和交通里─徒二42，46，六7。
VII.　The blessing of the church is dependent upon the church's continuing steadfastly in the teaching and fellowship of the apostles—Acts 2:42, 46; 6:7.
捌　断定正确的职事，就是神新约经纶的职事，决定的因素乃是使徒的教训：
VIII.　The deciding factor in determining the right ministry, which is the ministry of God's New Testament economy, is the teaching of the apostles:
一　一个人若教导使徒的教训，他的工作就是在新约的职事里。
A.　A person's work is in the New Testament ministry if he teaches the teaching of the apostles.
二　惟一的职事乃是神所命定，照着使徒教训的职事。
B.　The unique ministry is the ministry ordained by God according to the apostles' teaching.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE ONE
THE APOSTLES5 TEACHING—THE ENTIRE SPEAKING OF GOD IN THE NEW TESTAMENT CONCERNING GOD'S NEW TESTAMENT ECONOMY
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
The Lord has led us, through a period of intense exercise, fellowship, and seeking for His leading, to have a thorough review of the rich, crucial contents of God's New Testament ministry. This is fitting for the critical time in which we now find ourselves. In 2 Timothy 3:14 Paul says, "But you, continue in the things which you have learned and have been assured of, knowing from which ones you have learned them," We are here to continue in the things which we have learned, the things of God's New Testament ministry, the things of God's eternal economy. The messages in this series, with their thorough outlines, are a continuation in the things of God's economy. As we continue in these things, there is a deep intrinsic knowing within us, which is the realization that we did not learn these things in our private Bible study. We did not receive these things directly from God in our morning revival. We learned them from certain ones, and we are not ashamed, to present them, in a very real and honorable sense as a tribute to and a reminder of the ones through whom we learned the things in which we will continue. We learned them from Brother Watchman Nee, and we learned them, in particular during the last thirty-five years from Brother Witness Lee. We are not ashamed to bear witness of this fact. This series is a declaration of steadfast continuing. We will continue in these things, but we will continue knowing, remembering, recalling, appreciating, honoring, and respecting the ones from whom we have learned them. Surely it is fitting to follow Paul's pattern, which is to "continue…knowing."
The twelve crucial contents of God's New Testament ministry are the apostles' teaching, the New Testament ministry, God's economy, the Triune God, the all-inclusive Christ, the full ministry of Christ, the all-inclusive Spirit, the eternal life, God's complete salvation, the Body of Christ, the practical expression of the church, and as a climax, the wonderful New Jerusalem, which is the goal and the intrinsic substance of Brother Lee's ministry. In a very real sense, the outlines are the messages. The outlines are exceedingly rich. Each one is a feast of many courses. They are compilations of crystals, gems, and diamonds from our brother's ministry. As much as possible we have retained his utterance, and we unashamedly repeat it with a fresh exercise of our mingled spirit. In our study times and in our morning revivals we hope that all the seeking saints in the Lord's recovery will be able to immerse themselves in the wonderful things we learned at the feet of a faithful slave, our Brother Lee.
The crucial contents of God's New Testament ministry may be summarized by the following statements:
(1) The apostles' teaching is the entire speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament economy.
(2) The New Testament ministry is the unique ministry according to the apostles' teaching, the teaching of God's New Testament economy, for the building up of the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem.
(3) God's economy is His plan to dispense Himself into His chosen people as their life and everything to produce and build up the organic Body of Christ.
(4) The New Jerusalem as the consummation of God's eternal economy is the divine and human incorporation of the processed and consummated God constituted with His regenerated, transformed, and glorified elect.
In the Lord's recovery we would exercise to be as broad as God is broad and as limited as God is limited. He has limited us to one teaching—the apostles' teaching. We are here to continue steadfastly in the apostles' teaching. All the apostles in the New Testament had one teaching. That one teaching is the entire speaking of God concerning God's New Testament economy. We need to be deeply impressed, even to receive a heavenly vision, that in God's economy there is only one teaching revealed by God and recognized by God, which is the teaching of the apostles. We can bear testimony to the fact that everything Brother Lee taught, preached, and practiced was according to the apostles' teaching. We follow his teaching because his teaching is in keeping with the apostles' teaching.
THE THREE THOUSAND BELIEVERS WHO WERE SAVED ON THE DAY OF PENTECOST CONTINUED STEADFASTLY IN THE TEACHING AND THE FELLOWSHIP OF THE APOSTLES, IN THE BREAKING OF BREAD AND THE PRAYERS
The three thousand believers who were saved on the day of Pentecost continued steadfastly in the teaching and the fellowship of the apostles, in the breaking of bread and the prayers (Acts 2:41-42). From the outset of the church, there was a corporate continuation of what had been wrought into the one hundred twenty, who had been charged by the resurrected Christ to disciple the nations, baptizing them into the name of the Father, the Son, and the Spirit, teaching them to observe everything the Lord commanded. When the three thousand were saved and added to the church, they continued steadfastly in the apostles' teaching. We should love these two words, continued steadfastly. We are here to continue, and the way to continue is steadfastly. Steadfast means fixed, unchanging, steady, constant, unswerving, and firmly loyal. We are not here to continue in a burst of energy for one week, one month, one year, or even one decade. We are here giving ourselves to continue steadfastly until we meet the Lord. By the Lord's mercy and grace, this is our covenant, our commitment: to be firmly loyal, constant, and unswerving, come what may, to the apostles' teaching.
The Teaching and the Fellowship Form One Group Which Is of the Apostles and Related Directly to God's Economy for the Keeping of the Oneness of the Church, the Body of Christ
The teaching and the fellowship form one group which is of the apostles and related directly to God's economy for the keeping of the oneness of the church, the Body of Christ. Both the teaching of the apostles and the fellowship of the apostles are unique. This is our one and only teaching and our one and only fellowship. No ministry in the New Testament age has any right to teach anything different from the entire speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament economy. This teaching is unique and the fellowship produced by this teaching is also unique.
The Teaching of the Apostles Was the Holding Factor of the One Accord
The teaching of the apostles was the holding factor of the one accord (Acts 2:42a, 46a). Ephesians 4 charges us to keep the oneness of the Spirit, but we need to go further to also keep the one accord, to think the one thing, to speak the one thing, and to have one intention, goal, way, and purpose. We may have the oneness of the Spirit, but we may not have that much of the one accord. May the Lord show us that the holding factor of the one accord is the apostles' teaching. To teach differently or to handle the apostles' teaching wrongly will eventually bring in discord. We surely are not for this; we are for maintaining the holding factor of the one accord.
If We Limit Ourselves to the Apostles' Teaching, the Teaching concerning God's New Testament Economy, We Will Be Kept in Oneness and Will Have One Way for One Goal
If we limit ourselves to the apostles' teaching, the teaching concerning God's New Testament economy, we will be kept in oneness and will have one way for one goal. This is the way to have a worthy continuation of our brother's faithful ministry and the way to have one way with one goal. For this we all, especially the responsible brothers, need to limit ourselves. The messages in this series are a training for us to limit ourselves. May we all limit ourselves to the apostles' teaching. This will keep us in oneness, and all over the earth there will be one way for one goal. For there to be one way among us for one goal in every city, country, continent, and language will be a glory to the Lord and a vindication of our brother's ministry. No one should have a private goal or a personal agenda. We do not agree that selfish and individualistic things would burst forth anywhere. We only care for the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem. For this we need to be limited to the apostles' teaching.
In the Church There Should Be Only One Unique Teaching— the Teaching of the Apostles—and One Unique Fellowship, Which Is Produced by the Apostles' Teaching
In the church there should be only one unique teaching—the teaching of the apostles. Furthermore, there should be one unique fellowship, which is produced by the apostles' teaching. In all the churches, the elders, the leading brothers, have no authorization from God to teach differently. In the church there should be one unique teaching. Paul used expressions such as, "As I teach everywhere in every church" (1 Cor. 4:17). This is normal. Every church is the same in teaching. This one unique teaching is the teaching of the apostles.
Teaching always creates a fellowship. Fellowship is invariably a product of teaching. The kind of fellowship we enter into corresponds to the kind of teaching we are under. There is one unique fellowship, which is the fellowship of the apostles. Some may say that our fellowship is the fellowship of the Spirit or the fellowship of life. Our fellowship is of the Spirit and of life, but we are brought into this fellowship by the apostles' teaching. The apostles' teaching releases the divine life in which we participate in the apostles' fellowship, and that fellowship is the unique fellowship of the Body of Christ. Wrong teaching produces wrong fellowship. Therefore, Christianity is a confusion; it has wrong fellowship based on wrong teaching. It is a serious matter to be preferential or biased in our teaching of the apostles' teaching. It is also a serious matter to be hasty to modify or expand the apostles' teaching. If we do so, we may teach differently and produce, even in the Lord's recovery, a different kind of fellowship. We absolutely are not for this. We are for the one unique teaching, the teaching of the apostles that produces the one unique fellowship, the fellowship of the apostles. We give ourselves for this.
Any Fellowship outside the Fellowship of the Apostles Is Divisive
Any fellowship outside the fellowship of the apostles is divisive. Our fellowship must be inside the fellowship of the apostles.
The Breaking of Bread and the Prayers Form a Second Group and Are Practices of the Believers' Christian Life
The breaking of bread and the prayers form a second group and are practices of the believers' Christian life. The stress of this message, however, is on the apostles' teaching rather than our practice.
THE ENTIRE TEACHING OF THE NEW TESTAMENT IS GOD'S SPEAKING IN THE SON
In the Universe There Is a Marvelous Matter, God's Speaking
The entire teaching of the New Testament, which is the apostles' teaching, is God's speaking, God's oracle, in the Son to His New Testament people (Heb. 1:1-2). In the universe there is a marvelous matter, God's speaking. Hallelujah, our God is a speaking God, and He is still speaking.
In the Age of the New Testament God Does Not Speak to His People in Many Portions or in Many Ways, or through the Prophets
In the age of the New Testament God does not speak to His people in many portions or in many ways, or through the prophets. We are not here for many portions, many ways, and many prophets. That is the speaking of another dispensation.
In the New Testament Age God Only Speaks in One Person, the Son
In the New Testament age God only speaks in one person, the Son. In the four Gospels God spoke in the Son because the Son, the embodiment and expression of the Triune God, was there speaking. In John 7:46, those who came to arrest Him said, "Never has a man spoken as this man has." That was God speaking in the Son. The apostles' teaching is the entire speaking of God in the New Testament. How can the speaking in the remaining twenty-three books of the New Testament be God's speaking in the Son when the Son had literally and physically ascended? We need to realize that all the apostles were sons of God in the firstborn Son. In their speaking, in their ministry, they were not in themselves speaking from themselves. They were in the Son; they were part of the corporate Christ, the corporate "Me" that Paul was persecuting in Acts 9. The apostles were incorporated into the divine sonship, and according to the principle of incarnation, their speaking became God's speaking in the Son in them as the enlargement of the Son. Therefore, the entire speaking of God in the New Testament is God's speaking in the Son, either in His Son individually or in His Son corporately. Although the canon of revelation is closed, God in His speaking today in His recovery still speaks in the Son. That is why our brother repeatedly prayed before he ministered, "Lord, cause me to be one spirit with You. Make Your speaking my speaking; make my speaking Your speaking." We all need to be in the Son and speak not from ourselves but from within the Son according to the principle of incarnation. Any speaking outside of the Son is not the speaking of the New Testament ministry.
God Spoke in the Son as a Man, in the Son as the Spirit, and in the Son as the Seven Spirits
God firstly spoke in the Son as a man in the four Gospels (John 14:10; 5:24; 16:12; 10:30). God secondly spoke in the Son as the Spirit through the apostles in Acts and the twenty-one Epistles, Romans through Jude (John 16:12-15; Matt. 28:19-20; Heb. 2:3-4; 2 Pet. 3:15-16; Col. 1:25-27). God thirdly spoke in the Son as the seven Spirits through the apostle John in Revelation (1:2, 4; 2:1, 7). God's speaking in the Son as the Spirit through the apostles became the speaking which forms the apostles' teaching as the entire speaking of God in the New Testament.
God's Speaking in the Teaching of the New Testament Was Completed through Paul and John
The Word of God as the Revealed Mystery Was Completed through Paul
God's speaking in the teaching of the New Testament was completed through Paul and John. The word of God as the revealed mystery was completed through Paul (Col. 1:25-27). The mystery of God is Christ (2:2), the mystery of Christ is the church (Eph. 3:4), and the great mystery is Christ and the church (5:32). The speaking concerning this mystery was completed through Paul.
The Entire New Testament Was Completed by John's Writings
The entire New Testament was completed by John's writings (Rev. 22:18-19). Revelation ends with a warning not to add anything to or take away anything from the speaking of God. The ones from whom we have learned these things neither took away from nor added anything to the pure word of God. What a mercy it is that we could be under such a ministry!
This Speaking in the Son, the Apostles' Teaching, Does Not Stress Matters Which Are Not the Basic, Intrinsic, Central, and Elementary Things concerning God's Eternal Economy
This speaking in the Son, the apostles' teaching, does not stress matters such as foot-washing, baptism, head covering, etc. These are not the basic, intrinsic, central, and elementary things contained in the New Testament revelation concerning God's eternal economy. We need to learn which matters are not basic so that we will not emphasize them wrongly. To be sure, they are in the New Testament. We do have a proper teaching concerning baptism, but we do not emphasize baptism by immersion, much less make it a condition of fellowship. Reflecting upon our brother's ministry among us, we realize that it was not only faithful to the whole divine revelation but faithful to the emphasis of the whole revelation, emphasizing the Triune God, the all-inclusive Christ, the all-inclusive Spirit, the Body of Christ, and the New Jerusalem. What a ministry has been passed on to us! What a tremendous grace that we have heard the apostles' teaching! May the Lord be merciful to us that we will continue firmly loyal, steadfast, until we meet the Lord.—R. K.
THE TEACHING OF THE APOSTLES IS THE UNIQUE DIVINE REVELATION OF GOD'S NEW TESTAMENT ECONOMY FROM THE INCARNATION OF GOD TO THE CONSUMMATION OF THE NEW JERUSALEM
The teaching of the apostles is the unique divine revelation of God's New Testament economy from the incarnation of God to the consummation of the New Jerusalem, carried out by the full ministry of Christ in three divine and mystical stages for the fulfillment of God's eternal economy. The apostles' teaching is the speaking of God in the Son in three stages. But what is the speaking of the Son? The teaching of the apostles, as the Son's speaking, is the unique divine revelation of God's New Testament economy from the incarnation of God to the consummation of the New Jerusalem. Our Christ was incarnated to be a man. He lived on this earth for thirty-three and a half years. He went to the cross and died an all-inclusive death, He was raised in an all-conquering resurrection, and He ascended in an all-transcending ascension. Then He breathed the inner life into the church, and He baptized all the members in the Spirit. By these two actions He produced the marvelous church which is the Body of Christ, the house of God, the new man, the kingdom of God, and ultimately the bride of Christ. This glorious church will consummate in the New Jerusalem. This is the apostles' teaching.
The First Stage, the Stage of Incarnation, Is for Christ to Bring God into Man, to Express, God in Humanity, and to Accomplish His Judicial Redemption
God's New Testament economy is carried out by the full ministry of Christ in three divine and mystical stages: the stage of incarnation, the stage of inclusion, and the stage of intensification. The first stage, the stage of incarnation, is for Christ to bring God into man, to express God in humanity, and to accomplish His judicial redemption. The infinite God became a finite man. In His incarnation, the Triune God was united and mingled with the tripartite man. This is a great matter. In this stage, Christ expressed in His humanity the bountiful God in His rich attributes through His aromatic virtues. This was the life that Christ lived in His humanity. He also went to the cross as His last act in the stage of incarnation to accomplish His judicial redemption. In this judicial redemption He forgave us of all our sins, washed us from our sins, justified us, sanctified us positionally, and reconciled us to God. What a marvelous judicial redemption this is! In this redemption He terminated the old creation, and He redeemed back the creation that had been terminated on the cross. He also created the new man, the church, on the cross. In addition, He released the divine life from the shell of His humanity. In His judicial redemption as a procedure, a base, He paved the way for God's organic salvation.
The Second Stage, the Stage of Inclusion, Is for Christ to Be Begotten as God's Firstborn Son, to Become the Life-giving Spirit, and to Regenerate the Believers for His Body
The second stage, the stage of inclusion, is for Christ to be begotten as God's firstborn Son, to become the life-giving Spirit, and to regenerate the believers for His Body. According to His divinity, Christ was the only begotten Son from eternity past, but in time He came, lived on this earth, died, and was resurrected to become the firstborn Son of God. Through crucifixion and resurrection, this One, who was the only begotten Son of God in His divinity, uplifted His humanity and brought it into divinity. Bringing His humanity into divinity produced Christ as the firstborn Son of God with all of His brothers. To be begotten as God's firstborn Son was a great accomplishment. Moreover, when Christ was resurrected He was transformed, transfigured, to become the life-giving Spirit. Today He is the life-giving Spirit in all the believers, and because of this, we enjoy Him as life. Third, in the stage of inclusion He regenerated all the believers to become His Body. In Christ's resurrection we also were raised, and through His resurrection we were also regenerated.
The Third Stage, the Stage of Intensification, Is for Christ to Intensify His Organic Salvation, to Produce the Overcomers, and to Consummate the New Jerusalem
The third stage, the stage of intensification, is for Christ to intensify His organic salvation, to produce the overcomers, and to consummate the New Jerusalem. In the stage of intensification, Christ is not only accomplishing His organic salvation, but He is intensified to carry out His organic salvation in an intensified way in all of His believers in the degraded stage of the church. In His intensified stage He is also producing the overcomers. According to the Bible, the church became degraded, but Christ as the Spirit came in to intensify Himself so that He can produce overcomers out of the pitiful, degraded situation. Today this One who is still the Spirit, even the seven Spirits in His intensification, is carrying out His organic salvation in all of us in a wonderful, intensified way. The final result of the third stage of intensification is to consummate the New Jerusalem.
THE APOSTLES' TEACHING IS THE CONTENTS OF THE FULL GOSPEL OF GOD, COMPRISING NOT MERELY A PART OF THE NEW TESTAMENT, BUT THE ENTIRE NEW TESTAMENT
The apostles' teaching is the contents of the full gospel of God, comprising not merely a part of the New Testament, but the entire New Testament. In Romans 1:1, Paul said that he was separated unto the gospel of God. Paul carried out the full gospel of God, and this full gospel carried out by him is the apostles' teaching. The apostles' teaching is the revelation of God's economy from the Lord's incarnation to the consummation of the New Jerusalem, carried out by the full ministry of Christ in three divine and mystical stages. This is the very center and focal point of the entire New Testament. It is the intrinsic essence of all the teachings that have been brought to us in His Word. Brother Lee came to this country with the intention to bring us the apostles' teaching. All the years that he was with us, he never deviated, never turned away, from the apostles' teaching, but rather he unceasingly presented it to the Lord's children. What a heritage we have!
THE APOSTLES' TEACHING IS THE CHURCH'S CONSTITUTION
The apostles' teaching is the church's constitution; the church must hold it and be under it absolutely. Every proper country has a constitution, and that constitution must be adhered to unreservedly. Each country must hold it and be under it absolutely; otherwise, that country has no way to go on. Today we also have a marvelous constitution, which is the apostles' teaching. If we hold this constitution, the Lord's recovery will have a way to advance year after year, decade after decade, until the Lord comes. Our advancing depends on whether we as the saints and all the churches in the Lord's recovery hold the apostles' teaching with all loyalty.
The Apostles' Teaching Is the Constitution of the Christian Faith
The apostles' teaching is the constitution of the Christian faith (Jude 3; 1 Tim. 1:19; 6:12; 2 Tim. 4:7). The Christian faith is the apostles' teaching, which comprises all the things that we believe in. The things we believe in are many, taken from Genesis to Revelation. This is the Christian faith, the apostles' teaching, which we hold unreservedly.
The Apostles' Teaching, as the Church's Constitution, Should Be Universally Taught Everywhere in Every Church in the Same Way
The apostles' teaching, as the church's constitution, should be universally taught everywhere in every church in the same way (1 Cor. 4:17; 7:17). This means that we cannot add to the apostles' teaching. The apostles' teaching has been adequately defined by the New Testament ministry throughout many years. Now we only need to hold it universally in every church and teach it in the same way in every church without any deviation. If the Lord will be merciful to us to keep us uniquely in the apostles' teaching, the Lord's recovery has a great future. This is the holding factor for all the churches and all the saints in the Lord's recovery throughout the whole earth. Our constitution as the holding factor is nothing other than the apostles' teaching.
The Teaching of the Apostles Is for God's Economy, and the Teaching Is the Healthy Words of the Lord Jesus
The teaching of the apostles is for God's economy, and the teaching is the healthy words of the Lord Jesus. First Timothy 1:3-4 speaks of God's economy, to which we should hold, and 1 Timothy 6:3 speaks of the healthy words of the Lord Jesus. The healthy words of the Lord Jesus are the apostles' teaching. When the Lord was on the earth, He taught the apostles many things. Following this, He continued to speak many things through the apostles; those teachings were still the healthy words of the Lord Jesus. Whatever the apostles spoke was based upon what the Lord Jesus had revealed to them when He was on the earth. According to John 16:12-15, God's speaking in the Son did not stop with His resurrection and ascension. God continued to speak through the apostles, and this speaking is the speaking in the Son, the healthy teachings of the Lord Jesus.
All Teachings Must Be Restricted by the Limit and Sphere of the Apostles' Teaching
All teachings must be restricted by the limit and sphere of the apostles' teaching. If we are limited by this sphere, and all our teaching is within this realm, we will have one way for one goal without any different teachings. It will be a tragedy if certain churches or a region in the work eventually teach differently. This will divide the Lord's recovery because a different teaching produces a different fellowship. Teaching only the apostles' teaching is a great holding factor for our one accord. We expect that the Lord's recovery will go on in this way, not just at this time or in the next year but for as long as necessary. As long as the Lord delays His coming, we will be kept by the apostles' teaching in oneness and in one accord.
Christianity Has Many Ways Because of the Many Teachings outside the Limit of the Apostles' Teaching
Christianity has many ways because of the many teachings outside the limit of the apostles' teaching. May we not repeat the poor, sad history of Christianity.
All the Problems, Divisions, and Confusion among Christians Today Are Due to One Thing— Not Caring Only for the Unique Revelation of the Apostles' Teaching
All the problems, divisions, and confusion among Christians today are due to one thing—not caring only for the unique revelation of the apostles' teaching. However, if we keep and hold to the apostles' teaching, the Lord will keep us blended in harmony and in oneness.
In the Church There Should Be One Unique Teaching
In the church there should be one unique teaching, the apostles' teaching, not different teachings.
This Constitution, like Every Constitution, Must Be Properly Interpreted
This constitution, like every constitution, must be properly interpreted. Every believer has the same constitution, which is the New Testament from Matthew to Revelation, but the interpretation of this constitution has varied greatly. We can bear witness and testimony that we have been under a ministry that has properly interpreted this constitution. There is a balance among the three branches in the American government, but the one with the most practical power is the judicial branch with the Supreme Court, because it is the branch which interprets the Constitution. The constitution of the New Testament has been interpreted in full and interpreted rightly through the ministry of Brother Nee and Brother Lee.
ANY TEACHING THAT WAS DIFFERENT FROM THE APOSTLES' TEACHING WAS NOT ALLOWED BY THE APOSTLES
No Other Belief or Different Teaching Was Allowed by the Apostles
Any teaching that was different from the apostles' teaching was not allowed by the apostles. No other belief besides the unique faith was allowed by the apostles (Gal. 1:7-9). Teachings that went beyond the teaching of Christ were not allowed by the apostles (2 John 9-11). The different teachings, including those from the Old Testament dispensation that were different from God's economy, were not allowed by the apostles (1 Tim. 1:3-4). By reading the verses referenced here, we can see that the apostles spoke strongly against any deviation or any teaching other than the apostles' teaching.
All Teachings That Were Different from the Unique Revelation of God's New Testament Economy Were Considered by the Apostles to Be winds of Teaching
All teachings that were different from the unique revelation of God's New Testament economy were considered by the apostles to be winds of teaching. Ephesians 4:14 says that the different teachings are in the sleight of men. Apparently, many are good, but in actuality they are a cheating by Satan to bring the believers into another way. Paul goes on to say that such teachings are with a view to a system of error. Behind such teachings is Satan himself dividing the Body of Christ. We have to be delivered not only from heretical teachings but even from good teachings which are stressed but are not the intrinsic essence of the apostles' teaching.
God's Holy Writing Should Not Be Twisted by Anyone in Any Way but Rather Unfolded Rightly and Straightly without Any Distortion
God's holy writing should not be twisted by anyone in any way but rather unfolded rightly and straightly without any distortion (2 Pet. 3:16; 2 Tim. 2:15). The New Testament as our constitution has to be interpreted, of course, but it must be expounded, unfolded, and interpreted in a way that is absolutely right. Paul told Timothy to cut straight the word of the truth. The word must be unfolded rightly and straightly without any distortion.
THE BLESSING OF THE CHURCH IS DEPENDENT UPON THE CHURCH'S CONTINUING STEADFASTLY IN THE TEACHING AND FELLOWSHIP OF THE APOSTLES
The blessing of the church is dependent upon the church's continuing steadfastly in the teaching and fellowship of the apostles (Acts 2:42, 46; 6:7). Because the disciples continued steadfastly in the apostles' teaching, there was a great blessing upon the church in Jerusalem. Not only was the blessing upon the church in Jerusalem, but the Lord's new way began to spread throughout many countries. This was the Lord's blessing, and that blessing in life, in fellowship, and in spreading was brought in by the apostles' teaching. If we hold to this same teaching, there will be a great blessing in the Lord's recovery.
THE DECIDING FACTOR IN DETERMINING THE RIGHT MINISTRY, WHICH IS THE MINISTRY OF GOD'S NEW TESTAMENT ECONOMY, IS THE TEACHING OF THE APOSTLES
A Person's Work Is in the New Testament Ministry If He Teaches the Teaching of the Apostles
The deciding factor in determining the right ministry, which is the ministry of God's New Testament economy, is the teaching of the apostles. A persons work is in the New Testament ministry if he teaches the teaching of the apostles. Today many Christians are looking for an apostle. However, we should not look for an apostle to follow but for the right teaching to follow. If we are looking for an apostle, we may eventually be deceived, but if we are following the apostles' teaching, we will be kept in the Lord's recovery until we go to be with the Lord. Any deviation from the apostles' teaching will bring us into the wrong way. Our brothers before us bore the testimony that their speaking and teaching were the apostles' teaching. Therefore, we gladly follow them; that is, we follow their teaching. To follow the apostles' teaching means that we follow the person who is giving the teaching, but the basic matter in our following is not the person but the teaching. Once Brother Lee told Watchman Nee that he followed him not because of who he was but because he had the right teaching; even if Brother Nee were to stray from this teaching, Brother Lee would still continue in it. Today we also have been brought into the apostles' teaching; we must follow it.
The Unique Ministry Is the Ministry Ordained by God according to the Apostles' Teaching
The unique ministry is the ministry ordained by God according to the apostles' teaching. In How to Be a Co-worker and an Elder and How to Fulfill Their Obligations on page 44 Brother Lee says,
In his Epistles, especially in 2 Timothy, Paul spoke thoroughly concerning the degradation of the church. He said that all who were in Asia turned away from him (2 Tim. 1:15). This means that the churches established by Paul in Asia turned away from him. The saints in those churches did not forsake Paul himself; rather, they turned away from his New Testament ministry, the apostles' teaching which he preached. All that Paul had preached to them, all that he had nurtured them with all that he had taught them, and all that he had shown were completely abandoned by them. The first thing that happened in the degradation of the church was the turning away from the apostles' teaching. If all of us today in the Lord's recovery did not care for the apostles' teaching preached by Brother Watchman Nee and me, the church and the Lords recovery would become degraded. To remain in the apostles' teaching is a tremendous grace.
Thank the Lord for the apostles' teaching that has been preached and released to the Lord's recovery through our brothers. May the Lord keep us abiding in this teaching and in this grace.—B. P.

第二篇　新约的职事─照着使徒教训的惟一职事
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　新约的职事，是在宇宙中独一无二的职事─徒一17，25，林后四1，提前一12：
一　那灵的职事和义的职事，也就是新约的职事，与属死和定罪的职事，也就是旧约的职事，是相对的─林后三7～9。
二　新约职事的工作，乃是完成神关于召会的新约经纶，以建造基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷─弗三9～10，四11～12。
贰　新约的职事是独一无二的，但有许多的执事有分于这一个职事─徒二十24，二十一19，提后四5，西四17：
一　新约惟一的职事包括众使徒所有的工作（众职事），而众使徒乃是新约的众执事─林后三6。
二　新约的职事是独一无二的，也是团体的，但因为这职事是基督身体的事奉，又因为基督身体有许多的肢体，所以每一个肢体有其自己个人的职事。
三　因此，就着肢体说，有许多个人的职事；然而，就整个身体说，只有一个职事。
四　虽然执事有许多，但所有这些执事只有一个团体的职事，就是新约的职事。
叁　除了那为着完成神新约经纶的使徒教训以外，其它一切教训的工作（众职事）都不算在这惟一的职事里─徒二42，提前一3～4：
一　正确的职事乃是照着使徒教训，就是神新约经纶教训的职事，为着建造基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷。
二　神在信仰里的经纶，乃是神的家庭行政，要在基督里将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，使祂得着一个家彰显祂自己，这家就是召会，基督的身体。
三　在神经纶惟一之教训以外的其它教训，都被使徒看作是不同的教训─提前一3～4。
肆　分裂都是来自带着不同教训的不同职事：
一　异议者不同的教训，乃是被神仇敌所利用的风，要打岔神的子民，将他们从神的经纶带开─弗四14。
二　分裂的教训为撒但所组织并系统化，造成严重的错谬，因而破坏基督身体生活实行的一。
三　不同的教训乃是召会败落、堕落、并变质的主要根源─提前一3～4，6～7，六3～5，20～21。
伍　分辨真正新约的职事，有两个秘诀：
一　今天“热中犹太教的人”挑起问题，使信徒从主耶稣宝贵的人位岔开，但真正的职事激起我们对主耶稣这位新郎的爱，使我们享受祂作我们的丈夫到极点─林后十一2～3。
二　今天“热中犹太教的人”不为基督的身体受苦，但真正的职事加强我们来跟随基督，为着祂身体的缘故，交通于祂的受苦─林后十一23～33，腓三10，西一24。
陆　新约的职事是借着受苦、消耗的压力，以及十字架杀死的工作，所得对基督之丰富的经历，而在新约执事身上产生的─林后一8，四8～12：
一　新约的执事是在基督凯旋行列中的俘虏，从一处到另一处，散放基督的馨香之气，显出祂凯旋的荣耀─林后二14～15。
二　新约的执事是基督的大使，借着完成两步的和好职事，而成就神的定旨─林后五18～20：
１　第一步是使罪人脱离罪与神和好。
２　第二步是使活在天然生命中的信徒脱离肉体与神和好。
柒　新约的执事借着适应一切的生命，完成新约惟一的职事─林后六1：
一　新约职事的功用，是将生命分赐给别人─林后四12。
二　新约职事的功用，是将恩典供应给圣徒─林后一15，四15，六1。
三　新约职事的功用，是将经过过程并终极完成的三一神，分赐到信徒里面─林后十三14。
四　新约职事的功用，是用赐生命的灵作素质，书写基督的活信─林后三1～6：
１　这些信是用基督为内容所写，以传输并表现基督。
２　使徒将基督这赐生命的灵写在圣徒心上，使他们成为基督的信。
捌　新约职事惟一的目标，是要建造基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷：
一　这惟一的职事使信徒在生命、性情和彰显上与神一式一样─林后三3，6，五21，三18。
二　这惟一的职事将信徒合并到基督里，为着完成宇宙神人二性的合并：
１　信徒得以坚固的联于基督，好经历那灵的膏抹、印涂和作质─林后一21～22。
２　信徒得以与神完全和好，成为新耶路撒冷，就是扩大和终极的至圣所─林后五20，启二一16。
参读　新约的职事以及使徒的教训和交通；真理信息，第四章；神命定实行新约经纶的路，第十八章；哥林多后书生命读经，第五至七篇，三十九篇；基督的人性结晶读经，第二、四篇（中文尚未出书）。

GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message Two
The New Testament Ministry— the Unique Ministry according to the Apostles' Teaching
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　The ministry of the New Testament, which is the ministry of the new covenant, is uniquely one universally—Acts 1:17, 25; 2 Cor. 4:1; 1 Tim. 1:12:
A.　The ministry of the Spirit and of righteousness, which is the ministry of the new covenant, is in contrast with the ministry of death and of condemnation, which is the ministry of the old covenant—2 Cor. 3:7-9.
B.　The work of the New Testament ministry is to accomplish God's New Testament economy concerning the church in the building up of the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem—Eph. 3:9-10; 4:11-12.
II.　The ministry of the New Testament is uniquely one, but there are many ministers who have a part in this one ministry—Acts 20:24; 21:19; 2 Tim. 4:5; Col. 4:17:
A.　The unique ministry of the New Testament comprises all the works (ministries) of all the apostles, the ministers of the new covenant—2 Cor. 3:6.
B.　The New Testament ministry is uniquely one and corporate, but because this ministry is the service of the Body of Christ and because the Body has many members, every member has its own personal ministry.
C.　Thus, according to the members, there are many personal ministries; however, according to the Body as a whole, there is just one ministry.
D.　Although the ministers are many, all these ministers have only one corporate ministry, which is the New Testament ministry.
III.　All the works (the ministries) of the teachings other than the teaching of the apostles for the accomplishment of God's New Testament economy are not counted in this unique ministry—Acts 2:42; 1 Tim. 1:3-4:
A.　The proper ministry is the ministry according to the apostles' teaching, the teaching of God's New Testament economy, for the building up of the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem.
B.　God's economy in faith is His household administration to dispense Himself in Christ into His chosen people that He may have a house to express Himself, which house is the church, the Body of Christ.
C.　Any teaching other than the unique teaching of God's economy is considered by the apostle as a different teaching—1 Tim. 1:3-4.
IV.　Divisions come out of different ministries with different teachings:
A.　The different teachings of the dissenting ones are winds used by God's enemy to distract His people and carry them away from His economy—Eph. 4:14.
B.　The dividing teachings are organized and systematized by Satan to cause serious error and thus damage the practical oneness of the Body life.
C.　The different teachings are the major source of the church's decline, degradation, and deterioration—1 Tim. 1:3-4, 6-7; 6:3-5, 20-21.
V.　There are two secrets of discerning the genuine New Testament ministry:
A.　Today‘s "Judaizers" stir up questions to distract the believers from the precious person of the Lord Jesus, but the genuine ministry stirs up our love for the Lord Jesus as our Bridegroom so that we may enjoy Him to the uttermost as our Husband—2 Cor. 11:2-3.
B.　Today‘s "Judaizers" do not suffer for the Body of Christ, but the genuine ministry strengthens us to follow Christ in the fellowship of His sufferings for the sake of His Body—2 Cor. 11:23-33; Phil. 3:10; Col. 1:24.
VI.　The ministry of the new covenant is produced in the new covenant ministers by the experiences of the riches of Christ gained through sufferings, consuming pressures, and the killing work of the cross—2 Cor. 1:8; 4:8-12:
A.　The ministers of the new covenant are the captives of Christ in the train of His triumph, scattering the fragrance of Christ from place to place for His triumphant glory—2 Cor. 2:14-15.
B.　The ministers of the new covenant are the ambassadors of Christ to accomplish God's purpose by carrying out the ministry of reconciliation in two steps—2 Cor. 5:18-20:
1.　The first step is to reconcile sinners to God from sin.
2.　The second step is to reconcile the believers living in the natural life to God from the flesh.
VII.　The ministers of the new covenant carry out the unique ministry of the new covenant by an all-fitting life—2 Cor. 6:1:
A.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to impart life to others—2 Cor. 4:12.
B.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to supply grace to the saints—2 Cor. 1:15; 4:15; 6:1.
C.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to dispense the processed and consummated Triune God into the believers—2 Cor. 13:14.
D.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to write living letters of Christ with the life-giving Spirit as the essence—2 Cor. 3:1-6:
1.　The letters are composed of Christ as the content to convey and express Christ.
2.　The apostles inscribe Christ as the life-giving Spirit in the hearts of the saints to make them letters of Christ.
VIII.　The unique goal of the ministry of the new covenant is to build up the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem:
A.　The unique ministry makes the believers the same as God in life, nature, and expression—2 Cor. 3:3, 6; 5:21; 3:18.
B.　The unique ministry incorporates the believers into Christ for the consummation of the universal divine-human incorporation:
1.　The believers are firmly attached unto Christ to experience the Spirit's anointing, sealing, and pledging—2 Cor. 1:21-22.
2.　The believers are fully reconciled to God to become the New Jerusalem, the enlarged and consummate Holy of Holies—2 Cor. 5:20; Rev. 21:16.

纲目|outline-听抄-目录

三　在神经纶惟一之教训以外的其它教训，都被使徒看作是不同的教训─提前一3～4。
C.　Any teaching other than the unique teaching of God's economy is considered by the apostle as a different teaching—1 Tim. 1:3-4.
肆　分裂都是来自带着不同教训的不同职事：

C.　The different teachings are the major source of the church's decline, degradation, and deterioration—1 Tim. 1:3-4, 6-7; 6:3-5, 20-21.

V.　There are two secrets of discerning the genuine New Testament ministry:

A.　Today‘s "Judaizers" stir up questions to distract the believers from the precious person of the Lord Jesus, but the genuine ministry stirs up our love for the Lord Jesus as our Bridegroom so that we may enjoy Him to the uttermost as our Husband—2 Cor. 11:2-3.

B.　Today‘s "Judaizers" do not suffer for the Body of Christ, but the genuine ministry strengthens us to follow Christ in the fellowship of His sufferings for the sake of His Body—2 Cor. 11:23-33; Phil. 3:10; Col. 1:24.

VI.　The ministry of the new covenant is produced in the new covenant ministers by the experiences of the riches of Christ gained through sufferings, consuming pressures, and the killing work of the cross—2 Cor. 1:8; 4:8-12:

A.　The ministers of the new covenant are the captives of Christ in the train of His triumph, scattering the fragrance of Christ from place to place for His triumphant glory—2 Cor. 2:14-15.
二　新约的执事是基督的大使，借着完成两步的和好职事，而成就神的定旨─林后五18～20：
B.　The ministers of the new covenant are the ambassadors of Christ to accomplish God's purpose by carrying out the ministry of reconciliation in two steps—2 Cor. 5:18-20:
１　第一步是使罪人脱离罪与神和好。
1.　The first step is to reconcile sinners to God from sin.
２　第二步是使活在天然生命中的信徒脱离肉体与神和好。
2.　The second step is to reconcile the believers living in the natural life to God from the flesh.
柒　新约的执事借着适应一切的生命，完成新约惟一的职事─林后六1：
VII.　The ministers of the new covenant carry out the unique ministry of the new covenant by an all-fitting life—2 Cor. 6:1:
一　新约职事的功用，是将生命分赐给别人─林后四12。
A.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to impart life to others—2 Cor. 4:12.
二　新约职事的功用，是将恩典供应给圣徒─林后一15，四15，六1。
B.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to supply grace to the saints—2 Cor. 1:15; 4:15; 6:1.
三　新约职事的功用，是将经过过程并终极完成的三一神，分赐到信徒里面─林后十三14。
C.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to dispense the processed and consummated Triune God into the believers—2 Cor. 13:14.
四　新约职事的功用，是用赐生命的灵作素质，书写基督的活信─林后三1～6：
D.　The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to write living letters of Christ with the life-giving Spirit as the essence—2 Cor. 3:1-6:
１　这些信是用基督为内容所写，以传输并表现基督。
1.　The letters are composed of Christ as the content to convey and express Christ.
２　使徒将基督这赐生命的灵写在圣徒心上，使他们成为基督的信。
2.　The apostles inscribe Christ as the life-giving Spirit in the hearts of the saints to make them letters of Christ.
捌　新约职事惟一的目标，是要建造基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷：
VIII.　The unique goal of the ministry of the new covenant is to build up the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem:
一　这惟一的职事使信徒在生命、性情和彰显上与神一式一样─林后三3，6，五21，三18。
A.　The unique ministry makes the believers the same as God in life, nature, and expression—2 Cor. 3:3, 6; 5:21; 3:18.
二　这惟一的职事将信徒合并到基督里，为着完成宇宙神人二性的合并：
B.　The unique ministry incorporates the believers into Christ for the consummation of the universal divine-human incorporation:
１　信徒得以坚固的联于基督，好经历那灵的膏抹、印涂和作质─林后一21～22。
1.　The believers are firmly attached unto Christ to experience the Spirit's anointing, sealing, and pledging—2 Cor. 1:21-22.
２　信徒得以与神完全和好，成为新耶路撒冷，就是扩大和终极的至圣所─林后五20，启二一16。
2.　The believers are fully reconciled to God to become the New Jerusalem, the enlarged and consummate Holy of Holies—2 Cor. 5:20; Rev. 21:16.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE TWO
THE NEW TESTAMENT MINISTRY—THE UNIQUE MINISTRY ACCORDING TO THE APOSTLES' TEACHING
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
Our God is a God of purpose, and His eternal purpose, His heart's desire, is to gain a corporate man, the built-up Body of Christ, to be His corporate expression. God's New Testament economy is His household arrangement to fulfill His eternal purpose. The only way God's purpose can be fulfilled is by His economy, which is to dispense Himself into His redeemed people to be our life and everything. By Christ as our life, we are built up together to be the Body of Christ, the church, as God's corporate expression. The apostles' teaching is the entire speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament economy, and the New Testament ministry is the unique ministry according to the apostles' teaching for the building up of the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem.
THE MINISTRY OF THE NEW TESTAMENT, WHICH IS THE MINISTRY OF THE NEW COVENANT, IS UNIQUELY ONE UNIVERSALLY
The ministry of the New Testament, which is the ministry of the new covenant, is uniquely one universally (Acts 1:17,25; 2 Cor. 4:1; 1 Tim. 1:12). Today in Christianity many people talk about ministry, but regrettably, very few know what the ministry is. The Ministry of the New Testament and the Teaching and Fellowship of the Apostles helps us to clearly see what the ministry is. A ministry is based upon a covenant (2 Cor. 3:6, 14). A ministry carries out what God has covenanted with His people. Therefore, without God's covenant it is not possible to have His ministry. Moreover, if there is one covenant, there is one ministry, and for two covenants there are two ministries. In the Old Testament the most important covenant God made with His people was the covenant of the law, which 2 Corinthians 3:14 calls the old covenant. In the New Testament, however, God only made one covenant with His people, which is the new covenant, the covenant of grace. God did not make more than one covenant with His New Testament people. Therefore, there is only one ministry. If there is only one new covenant, it is impossible to have more than One New Testament ministry. The ministry is the service rendered to God to carry out His covenant. If we see this, the matter of the ministry will be very clear to us. Since in the New Testament there is only one covenant, the covenant of grace, there can only be one unique New Testament ministry.
The Ministry of the Spirit and of Righteousness,
Which Is the Ministry of the New Covenant, Is in Contrast with the Ministry of Death and of Condemnation,
Which Is the Ministry of the Old Covenant
The ministry of the Spirit and of righteousness, which is the ministry of the new covenant, is in contrast with the ministry of death and of condemnation, which is the ministry of the old covenant (2 Cor. 3:7-9). The old covenant is the covenant of the law. The letter of the law cannot give us life. It requires us to practice the law, but it does not supply life to us. None of us can practice the law; therefore, this law condemns us and kills us. Therefore, the Old Testament ministry, which is based on the old covenant, becomes the ministry of death and the ministry of condemnation. However, since the New Testament ministry is basedon the new covenant, which is the covenant of grace, it is the ministry of righteousness, that is, of justification.
The covenant of grace, the new covenant, is for us to receive God, experience God, enjoy God, and have God as our life and everything. The God whom we have in the new covenant, who is the supply to us, is the pneumatic Christ, the life-giving Spirit. Therefore, in 2 Corinthians 3, the New Testament ministry is also called the ministry of the Spirit. The Spirit is the life-giving Spirit who gives us life. In the New Testament ministry, which is based on the new covenant, we have received this eternal life; therefore, we can fulfill the requirements of the law. Romans 8:4 says, "The righteous requirement of the law might be fulfilled in us, who do not walk according to the flesh but according to the spirit."
The Work of the New Testament Ministry Is to Accomplish God's New Testament Economy concerning the Church in the Building Up of the Body of Christ to Consummate the New Jerusalem
The work of the New Testament ministry is to accomplish God's New Testament economy concerning the church in the building up of the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem (Eph. 3:9-10). Ephesians 4:11-12 says, "He Himself gave some as apostles and some as prophets and some as evangelists and some as shepherds and teachers, for the perfecting of the saints unto the work of the ministry, unto the building up of the Body of Christ." All the gifts given by Christ to the church are to perfect the saints unto the work of the ministry. Moreover, the work of the ministry is unto the building up of the Body of Christ. Here the work of the ministry and the building up of the Body of Christ are placed together. Based on these verses we can see clearly that the work of the ministry is to build up the Body of Christ, because the Body of Christ is the corporate man that expresses God. Today many Christian workers talk about ministry, but many of them do not know what the Body of Christ is; they do not care for the Body, and they do not speak concerning the building up of the Body. God's intention, however, is for all the members of Christ's Body to be perfected unto this work, the work of the ministry to build up the Body of Christ.
THE MINISTRY OF THE NEW TESTAMENT IS UNIQUELY ONE, BUT THERE ARE MANY MINISTERS WHO HAVE A PART IN THIS ONE MINISTRY
The Unique Ministry of the New Testament Comprises All the Works (Ministries) of All the Apostles, the Ministers of the New Covenant
The ministry of the New Testament is uniquely one, but there are many ministers who have a part in this one ministry (Acts 20:24; 21:19; 2 Tim. 4:5; Col. 4:17). The unique ministry of the New Testament comprises all the works (ministries) of all the apostles, the ministers of the new covenant. Second Corinthians 3:6 says, "Who has also made us sufficient as ministers of a new covenant, ministers not of the letter but of the Spirit." In 2 Corinthians 3:8-9, when Paul speaks about the ministry, he uses the singular number; there is only one ministry because there is only one covenant. When he speaks about the ministers, however, he uses the plural number, speaking of the "ministers of a new covenant." Even though there is only one ministry, there are many ministers, and even though there are many ministers, all these ministers are in the one ministry.
The New Testament Ministry Is Uniquely One and Corporate The New Testament ministry is uniquely one and corporate, but because this ministry is the service of the Body of Christ and because the Body has many members, every member has its own personal ministry. Thus, according to the members, there are many personal ministries; however, according to the Body as a whole, there is just one ministry. Although the ministers are many, all these ministers have only one corporate ministry, which is the New Testament ministry.
In the New Testament there is only one ministry. Apparently, the Bible speaks of many ministries, but these many ministries are one ministry. On the individual side, Paul tells Timothy to fully accomplish "your ministry" (2 Tim. 4:5). This indicates that Timothy had a ministry. Likewise, in Acts 21:19, when Paul went to Jerusalem, he fellowshipped with the brothers what God had done through "his ministry," that is, through Paul's ministry. Personally speaking, all the ministers have a personal ministry, but we must be clear that these are not many different ministries but a part of the one unique ministry. In this one unique ministry there are many who have been perfected, who have the burden to serve God to carry out His covenant. They all have a portion in this one unique ministry, and their personal ministries, including Paul's, Peter's, Timothy's, Brother Nee's, and Brother Lee's ministries, are a part of the one unique ministry. We should not do any other work; we must do the work of this ministry, participating in the work of building up the Body of Christ. May the Lord raise up many ministers among us who will carry out the one work.
The one ministry with many ministers can be compared to our physical body. When we speak, it is not only our mouth which speaks. Actually, our whole body speaks: our eyes "speak" by looking at the audience, our hands gesture, and our two feet support our body. Every member of our body has a portion in this work. It is the same today in the building up of the Body of Christ. We are all doing one thing—building up the Body, but this requires many ministers. May the Lord be merciful to us to raise up many ministers to participate in this one work—the New Testament ministry for the building up of His Body.
ALL THE WORKS (THE MINISTRIES) OF THE TEACHINGS OTHER THAN THE TEACHING OF THE APOSTLES ARE NOT COUNTED IN THIS UNIQUE MINISTRY
All the works (the ministries) of the teachings other than the teaching of the apostles for the accomplishment of God's New Testament economy are not counted in this unique ministry (Acts 2:42; 1 Tim. 1:3-4). The proper ministry is the ministry according to the apostles' teaching, the teaching of God's New Testament economy, for the building up of the Body ot Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem. God's economy in faith is His household administration to dispense Himself in Christ into His chosen people that He may have a house to express Himself winch house is the church, the Body of Christ. Any teaching other than unique teaching of God's economy is considered by the apostle as a different teaching.
In 1 Timothy 1:3-4, Paul tells Timothy to warn those who teach different things. The different things here include myths and unending genealogies, which were derived from the genealogies in the Old Testament. To some extent, the genealogies are part of the Bible. The Judaizers may have said, "What is wrong with this? We are speaking things from the Old Testament." It may be true that they were derived from the Old Testament, but they had nothing to do with God's New Testament economy for His eternal purpose. The genealogies cannot build up the Body of Christ. Therefore, they cannot be counted as the unique ministry of the New Testament. Anything that is not for God's economy, for the building up of the Body of Christ, cannot be counted as the unique ministry.
DIVISIONS COME OUT OF DIFFERENT MINISTRIES WITH DIFFERENT TEACHINGS
Divisions come out of different ministries with different teachings. The different teachings of the dissenting ones are winds used by God's enemy to distract His people and carry them away from His economy concerning Christ and the church (Eph. 4:14). The dividing teachings are organized and systematized by Satan to cause serious error and thus damage the practical oneness of the Body life. The different teachings are the major source of the church's decline, degradation, and deterioration (1 Tim. 1:3-4, 6-7; 6:3-5, 20-21).
Paul's word in 1 Timothy was his charge to Timothy to inoculate the church, to save the church from degradation. Paul did not charge Timothy concerning immorality, idol worship, or other matters but concerning myths and unending genealogies. Apparently these are not sinful, but they carry people away from God's New Testament ministry for His New Testament economy. This is not a small matter; it is the first step in the degradation and deterioration of the church. Therefore, we all need to be very careful. May the Lord be merciful to all of us and keep us in this New Testament ministry. We should not look for an apostle to follow; we must look for a proper teaching to follow. We should follow the apostles' teathing because it is the New Testament ministry for God's New Testament economy in the building up of the Body of Christ.—B. C.
THERE ARE TWO SECRETS OF DISCERNING THE GENUINE NEW TESTAMENT MINISTRY
What we have seen up to this point is a marvelous revelation of the truth concerning God's New Testament ministry. Now we must see and enter into the subjective experience and realization of our participation in God's New Testament ministry to be constituted ministers of the new covenant, who are participating subjectively, experientially, and practically in this one unique ministry, which is according to the apostles' teaching, the teaching of God's New Testament economy.
The Life-study of Second Corinthians has helped us to see that there are two marvelous secrets of discerning the genuine New Testament ministry. Brother Lee's life and ministry were characterized by these two secrets, just as Paul's life and ministry were. In the same way, our own Christian life and our participation in the unique ministry of the New Testament must also be characterized by these two secrets.
Today's "Judaizers" Stir Up Questions to Distract the Believers from the Precious Person of the Lord Jesus, but the Genuine Ministry Stirs Up Our Love for the Lord Jesus as Our Bridegroom So That We May Enjoy Him to the Uttermost as Our Husband
Today's "Judaizers" stir up questions to distract the believers from the precious person of the Lord Jesus, but the genuine ministry stirs up our love for the Lord Jesus as our Bridegroom so that we may enjoy Him to the uttermost as our Husband (2 Cor. 11:2-3). The Judaizers in Paul's day were those who taught differently from the teaching of God's New Testament economy. Their different teachings were according to the religious system of Judaism. Today we are in an atmosphere of many "Judaizers," those who have teachings different than the unique teaching of the apostles, which is the teaching of God's New Testament economy.
Today's "Judaizers" with their different teachings stir up questions to distract the believers from the precious person of the Lord Jesus. First Timothy 1:3-4 shows us that the different teachings produce questionings; they put doubts in our mind. This is what today's "Judaizers" do. We can testify that by the Lord's mercy for many years we have been under the genuine New Testament ministry, and this genuine ministry stirs up our love for the Lord Jesus as our Bridegroom that we enjoy Him to the uttermost as our Husband. In 2 Corinthians 11:2 Paul tells the Corinthians, "I am jealous over you with a jealousy of God; for I betrothed you to one husband to present you as a pure virgin to Christ." The genuine New Testament ministry betroths us to Christ as our Husband. It stirs us up to love the Lord Jesus as our unique Husband so that we can enjoy Him to the uttermost. Many of us did not even know we should say, "Lord Jesus, I love You" until we came under this ministry. Our brother ministered the genuine New Testament ministry, and it has stirred us up to love the Lord Jesus to the uttermost, to appreciate Him, treasure Him, love Him, and take Him as our everything. We are thankful that we have been brought under the genuine New Testament ministry, and now we all have a share in this ministry. Every time we read a life-study, something rises up in us to say, "Lord Jesus, I love You!" The genuine ministry does not present us as students of theology. It presents us as a pure virgin to Christ. In the full-time training we are not producing students of theology; we are producing lovers of Jesus. The Lord's recovery is not to recover doctrine or theology. It is to recover Christ Himself as the unique Husband for us to love.
To love the Lord is the way to enjoy Him as our life supply. The genuine New Testament ministry brings us into the enjoyment of Christ as our life supply. The different teachings, however, do not do this. Any teaching other than the teaching of the apostles does not bring us into the genuine enjoyment of Christ as our life supply. Rather, it ministers death to us. Death is separation from the enjoyment of God. This is the first secret of discerning the genuine New Testament ministry.
Today's "Judaizers" Do Not Suffer for the Body of Christ, but the Genuine Ministry Strengthens Us to Follow Christ in the Fellowship of His Sufferings for the Sake of His Body
Today's "Judaizers" do not suffer for the Body of Christ, but the genuine ministry strengthens us to follow Christ in the fellowship of His sufferings for the sake of His Body (2 Cor. 11:23-33; Phil. 3:10; Col. 1:24). The teachings in Christianity about health, wealth, and prosperity are far off from the genuine New Testament ministry. In the last part of 2 Corinthians 11, when Paul vindicates his apostolic authority as a minister of the new covenant, he speaks about his sufferings. He was beaten with rods, shipwrecked, let down over a wall in a basket, and he suffered hunger and cold. This shows us that the genuine New Testament ministry strengthens us to follow Christ in the fellowship of His sufferings for the sake of His Body. A genuine minister of the new covenant suffers for the sake of the Body of Christ.
It is very significant that Brother Lee's last word was "sacrifice." We need to be those who sacrifice everything for God's economy, those who pour out our lives as a drink offering the way Paul did and the way Brother Nee and Brother Lee did. We hope we can be our brothers' continuation to pour out everything of our being to carry out God's economy and be strengthened to follow Christ in the fellowship of His sufferings for the sake of His Body. Hymns, #549, written by Brother Lee, says, "Enter the veil and go without the camp." To enter the veil is to enter into the deepest, most intrinsic, and most intimate fellowship with the Lord as our Bridegroom, to love Him to the uttermost. This strengthens us to go outside the camp of religion to follow Him in the fellowship of His sufferings for the sake of His Body. This is the second secret of discerning the genuine New Testament ministry.
THE MINISTRY OF THE NEW COVENANT IS PRODUCED IN THE NEW COVENANT MINISTERS BY THE EXPERIENCES OF THE RICHES OF CHRIST GAINED THROUGH SUFFERINGS, CONSUMING PRESSURES, AND THE KILLING WORK OF THE CROSS
The ministry of the new covenant is produced in the new covenant ministers by the experiences of the riches of Christ gained through sufferings, consuming pressures, and the killing work of the cross (2 Cor. 1:8; 4:8-12). We all pass through certain sufferings and consuming pressures. We need to pray that by the Lord's mercy, in whatever circumstances we are in, we would be one with Him to experience the riches of Christ so that we could be constituted ministers of the new covenant to carry out this one unique ministry.
The Ministers of the New Covenant Are the Captives of Christ in the Train of His Triumph, Scattering the Fragrance of Christ from Place to Place for His Triumphant Glory
The ministers of the new covenant are the captives of Christ in the train of His triumph, scattering the fragrance of Christ from place to place for His triumphant glory (2 Cor. 2:14-15). The messages given in 1967 entitled An Autobiography of a Person in the Spirit speak concerning the captives of Christ. They remind us that we should pray, "Lord, conquer me and make me Your captive. Don't let me win. Lord, defeat me all the time, because if I win, I lose." What the Lord needs today is not spiritual giants but many little captives in the train of Christ's triumphal procession to be a fragrance of Christ scattered throughout the earth for His triumphant glory.
The Ministers of the New Covenant Are the Ambassadors of Christ to Accomplish God's Purpose by Carrying Out the Ministry of Reconciliation in Two Steps
The ministers of the new covenant are the ambassadors of Christ to accomplish God's purpose by carrying out the ministry of reconciliation in two steps (2 Cor. 5:18-20). On the one hand, we are the captives of Christ; on the other hand, we are the ambassadors of Christ. What can be more noble than to be an ambassador of Christ?
