This is the highest career in the universe. To be an ambassador of Christ is to be a person constituted with Christ to be one with Him in the ministry of reconciliation. First, we ourselves need to pray that we would be fully reconciled to God, that there would be no shadow, no separation, between us and God. Paul's ministry had this characteristic. He was a person who was fully reconciled to God, absolutely one with God in the deepest and most intimate fellowship with the processed and consummated Triune God. Therefore, when he ministered to people, he reconciled them to God.
The first step of the reconciling ministry is to reconcile sinners to God from sin. This brings a person from the outer court into the Holy Place. However, there is another step. The second step is to reconcile the believers living in the natural life to God from the flesh. This is a full reconciliation to God from the Holy Place all the way through the veil of the flesh into the Holy of Holies. May the Lord make us all such people to carry out this unique ministry. Then wherever people are, God can entreat them through us to be reconciled to Him in a full and complete way.
THE MINISTERS OF THE NEW COVENANT CARRY OUT THE UNIQUE MINISTRY OF THE NEW COVENANT BY AN ALL-FITTING LIFE
The ministers of the new covenant carry out the unique ministry of the new covenant by an all-fitting life. The unique ministry of the new covenant, which is according to the teaching of the apostles, is not carried out by any gift. It is carried out by a life which is all-sufficient and all-mature (see 2 Cor. 6:1, note 1 in the Recovery Version). The life within us can carry out the ministry of the new covenant because it is able to fit all kinds of situations. Our life does not fit all situations. All the serving ones who go to Russia need to realize that their life does not fit in Russia, but there is another life—the divine, wonderful, uncreated life of the processed and consummated Triune God—which fits all situations. This life can endure any kind of treatment, accept any kind of environment, work in any kind of condition, and take any kind of opportunity to carry out the ministry of the new covenant. We thank the Lord that we have such an all-fitting life in our spirit.
The Function of the Ministry of the New Covenant Is to Impart Life to Others
As we carry out the New Testament ministry by an all-fitting life, we can see what the function of the ministry is. The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to impart life, that is, to dispense God, to others (2 Cor. 4:12). Our career is to dispense God into people.
The Function of the Ministry of the New Covenant Is to Supply Grace to the Saints
The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to supply grace to the saints (2 Cor. 1:15; 4:15; 6:1). We should pray, "Lord, make me a supplier of grace." In 2 Corinthians 1:15 Paul says, "In this confidence I intended to come to you previously that you might have double grace." Paul's coming to see the saints was a grace to them. His visit brought them into the genuine enjoyment of Christ as their life supply. Furthermore, Paul's second visit was a double grace to them. May it be the same with all of us! When we visit people, it should be a grace to them, and if we visit them again, it should be a multiple grace. We should be suppliers of grace in this way.
The Function of the Ministry of the New Covenant Is to Dispense the Processed and Consummated Triune God into the Believers
The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to dispense the processed and consummated Triune God into the believers (2 Cor. 13:14). In his final word to the Corinthians, Paul blesses them with the dispensing of the processed and consummated Triune God. Even in the Old Testament, the priests' job was to bless the children of Israel with the Triune God (Num. 6:22-27). In the same way, our career as New Testament priests is to bless people with the processed and consummated Triune God in His divine dispensing.
The Function of the Ministry of the New Covenant Is to Write Living Letters of Christ with the Life-giving Spirit as the Essence
The function of the ministry of the new covenant is to write living letters of Christ with the life-giving Spirit as the essence (2 Cor. 3:1-6). The letters are composed of Christ as the content to convey and express Christ. The apostles inscribe Christ as the life-giving Spirit in the hearts of the saints to make them letters of Christ. As members of the Body of Christ, this is the work we should do. In
2 Corinthians 3:3 Paul says, "Since you are being manifested that you are a letter of Christ ministered by us, inscribed not with ink but with the Spirit of the living God; not in tablets of stone but in tablets of hearts of flesh." The heavenly, divine, mystical, wonderful, and indelible ink which we minister into people to make them the living letters of Christ is the life-giving Spirit of the living God. When people are inscribed in this way, others can read and know Christ in their being. To a certain extent we have become the living letters of Christ, because we have been under the New Testament ministry which inscribes Christ into our being with the Spirit of the living God as the ink.
THE UNIQUE GOAL OF THE MINISTRY OF THE NEW COVENANT IS TO BUILD UP THE BODY OF CHRIST TO CONSUMMATE THE NEW JERUSALEM
The Unique Ministry Makes the Believers the Same as God in Life, Nature, and Expression
The unique goal of the ministry of the new covenant is to build up the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem. The unique ministry makes the believers the same as God in life, nature, and expression (2 Cor. 3:3, 6; 5:21; 3:18). The unique and genuine ministry transforms us into the same image as Christ, bringing in a divine and mystical sameness with God in life, nature, and expression, but not in the Godhead.
The Unique Ministry Incorporates the Believers into Christ for the Consummation of the Universal Divine-human Incorporation
The Believers Are Firmly Attached unto Christ to Experience the Spirit's Anointing, Sealing, and Pledging
The unique ministry incorporates the believers into Christ for the consummation of the universal divine-human incorporation. The believers are firmly attached unto Christ to experience the Spirit's anointing, sealing, and pledging (2 Cor. 1:21-22). God attaches the believers with the apostles unto Christ, the anointed One. The way He does this is through the genuine New Testament ministry, by which we experience the Spirit's anointing, sealing, and pledging to incorporate us into the Triune God.
The Believers Are Fully Reconciled to God to Become the New Jerusalem, the Enlarged and Consummate Holy of Holies
The believers are fully reconciled to God to become the New Jerusalem, the enlarged and consummate Holy of Holies (2 Cor. 5:20; Rev. 21:16). The work of the genuine ministry of the New Testament, which is according to the apostles' teaching, is to fully reconcile us to God, bringing us into the Holy of Holies so that we may become the enlarged and consummate Holy of Holies, which is the New Jerusalem.—E. M.

TOP-纲目|Outline|对照-目录
　
　
第三篇　神的经纶─神圣启示的中心线
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　神的经纶是神的家庭行政─提前一4：
一　经纶一辞原文的意思是“家庭律法”，含分配意；指家庭管理，家庭行政，家政，引伸为行政（分配）的安排，计划或经纶，所以也是家庭经营。
二　神的经纶乃是神的家庭经营，神的家庭行政，要在基督里将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，使祂得着一个家彰显祂自己，这家就是召会，基督的身体。
贰　我们必须看见神经纶的异象─弗一10：
一　神的经纶是祂的计划，要将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选、预定并救赎的人里面，作他们的生命、生命的供应和一切，以产生、构成、并建造基督生机的身体。
二　神的经纶是要得着一班人，而将祂自己作到他们里面作生命，并将祂自己与他们调和为一，使他们作基督身体的肢体而活祂。
三　神的经纶是要使蒙祂救赎的人，在生命、性情和显出的样子上成为神，但无分于祂的神格，使祂自己得着一个宇宙、团体的彰显，直到永远。
四　神的经纶是要使人在生命和性情上与祂完全一样，只是无分于祂的神格，并使祂自己与人成为一，使人与祂成为一，因而在祂的彰显上得以扩大并扩展，使祂一切神圣的属性得以彰显于人性的美德。
叁　神的经纶与祂的喜悦、意愿、决议和定旨有关─弗一5，9，11，三11，启四11：
一　神的喜悦是神所喜爱的，神所喜欢的。
二　神的意愿是神的愿望，神渴望，是祂所想要作的。
三　神的决议是祂在神圣三一的会议中所完成的诀议。
四　神的定旨是祂预先的定意。
五　神的意愿是照着祂的喜悦；神的定旨是基于祂的意愿及其决议；神的经纶是祂计划的行政，以完成祂的定旨。
肆　神的经纶是在信仰里的─提前一4：
一　神的经纶是在信仰的的范围和元素里得以开始而发展的。
二　神的经纶不是在天然的范围里，也不是在律法的行为里，乃是因着相信基督，借着重生，在新造属灵的范围里─加三23～26：
１　因着信，我们由神而生，成为祂的儿子，有分于祂的生命和性情以彰显祂。
２　因着信，我们被放在基督里，成为祂身体的肢体，分享祂一切的所是，叫祂得着彰显。
伍　加拉太这卷关于神经纶最基本的书，对神经纶的启示是独特的：
一　神的经纶是神自己在祂神圣的三一里成为赐生命的灵，作我们的生命和一切给我们享受，使祂和我们成为一而彰显祂，直到永远─三14，28。
二　神新约经纶的一个基本项目乃是：“我”在基督的死里被钉死，基督在祂的复活里活在我们里面─二20。
三　神新约的经纶是使经过过程的三一神作到我们里面，成为我们的生命和我们的所是─一16，四19。
四　神在祂经纶里的目的，是要将我们放在祂里面，并进到我们里面，活在我们里面─三27，二20。
五　神的经纶是将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，使他们成为祂的儿子，作祂团体的彰显─三26，四6～7。
陆　神的经纶是借着神的分赐完成的：
一　神的分赐乃是照着神的计划和安排，将祂自己分赐到我们里面。
二　神渴望将祂自己分赐到蒙祂拣选、救赎并重生的人里面，作他们的生命、生命的供应和一切，使祂自己与他们成为一。
三　神的分赐是借着神圣三一完成的─弗一4～5，7～10，13：
１　神圣的性情是借着父神的拣选，分赐到在基督里之信徒里面；神圣的生命是借着父神的预定而分赐的。
２　在基督里的信徒所凭以成为神超越之基业的神圣元素，借着子神的救赎分赐到信徒里面，为着时期满足时之神的经纶，要将万有都在基督里归一于一个元首之下。
３　信徒在其中所享受经过过程之三一神的神圣素质，借着灵神的印涂和作质，分赐到信徒里面。
柒　神在祂经纶里的目的，是要将祂自己在基督里建造到祂所拣选的人里面─弗三16～17上：
一　圣经所启示最重要而奥秘的事，乃是神最终的目的是要将祂自己作到祂所拣选的人里面。
二　神中心的工作是要将祂自己在基督里作到祂所拣选的人里面，使祂自己与他们成为一：
１　基督所是的一切和所完成的一切，都是为着这一件事。
２　神在我们日常生活中所采的一切步骤，都是要成就祂将自己在基督里建造到我们里面的这个目的。
三　神照着祂心愿的经纶和目标，乃是要将祂自己建造到我们里面，并把我们建造到祂里面，好将祂的神性与我们的人性调成一个实体─基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷。
捌　神的经纶如同一个大轮，有基督为其中心─结一15～21：
一　这轮的轮轴，表征基督是神经纶的中心。
二　轮辋，表征基督的配偶，召会，基督的身体。
三　作基督许多肢体的信徒是轮轴的轮辐，扩展到轮辋，扩展到基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷。
四　这个大轮不仅是神的经纶，也是神经纶的行动：
１　从创世记一章直到现今，神经纶的行动从未停止，今天这个大轮已经达到我们。
２　历世历代这个轮子都在行动，我们现今是神经纶之大轮的行动的一部分。
参读　神圣启示的中心路线，第三至四篇；新约总论，第一册，第二篇；加拉太书生命读经，第二、三、十、十五、二十二篇；约伯记生命读经，第三十八篇；约书亚记生命读经，第二篇；撒母耳记生命读经，第二十三至二十五、二十八至三十一篇；以西结的异象，第七篇。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message Three
God's Economy— the Central Line of the Divine Revelation
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　God's economy is His household administration—1 Tim. 1:4:
A.　The Greek word for?economy?means "household law," implying distribution; it denotes a household management, a household administration, a household government, and, derivatively, a dispensation, a plan, or an economy for administration (distribution); hence, it is also a household economy.
B.　God's economy is His household economy, His household administration, which is to dispense Himself in Christ into His chosen people that He may have a house to express Himself, which house is the church, the Body of Christ.
II.　We need to see a vision of God's economy—Eph. 1:10:
A.　God's economy is His plan to dispense Himself into His chosen, predestinated, and redeemed people as their life, their life supply, and their everything to produce, constitute, and build up the organic Body of Christ.
B.　God's economy is to gain a group of people and work Himself into them as life and mingle Himself with them as one so that they may live Him as the members of the Body of Christ.
C.　God's economy is to make His redeemed people God in life, in nature, and in appearance but not in the Godhead so that for eternity He might have a universal, corporate expression of Himself.
D.　God's economy is to make man the same as He is in life and nature but not in His Godhead and to make Himself one with man and man one with Him, thus to be enlarged and expanded in His expression, that all His divine attributes may be expressed in human virtues.
III.　God's economy is related to His good pleasure, will, counsel, and purpose—Eph. 1:5, 9, 11; 3:11; Rev. 4:11:
A.　God's good pleasure is what God likes, what pleases Him.
B.　God's will is God's wish, God's desire; it is what He wants to do.
C.　God's counsel is His resolution consummated in the council of the Divine Trinity.
D.　God's purpose is His intent beforehand.
E.　God's will is according to His good pleasure; God's purpose is based on His will with its counsel; and God's economy is His planned administration to carry out His purpose.
IV.　God's economy is in faith—1 Tim. 1:4:
A.　God's economy is initiated and developed in the sphere and element of faith.
B.　God's economy is not in the natural realm nor in the work of law but in the spiritual sphere of the new creation through regeneration by faith in Christ—Gal. 3:23-26:
1.　By faith we are born of God to be His sons, partaking of His life and nature to express Him.
2.　By faith we are put into Christ to become the members of His Body, sharing all that He is for His expression.
V.　Galatians, the most basic book with respect to God's economy, is unique in its revelation of God's economy:
A.　God's economy is God Himself in His Divine Trinity becoming the life-giving Spirit to be life and everything to us for our enjoyment, so that He and we may be one to express Him for eternity—3:14, 28.
B.　A basic item of God's New Testament economy is that "I" be crucified in Christ's death and that Christ live in us in His resurrection—2:20.
C.　God's New Testament economy is for the processed Triune God to be wrought into us to become our life and our very being—1:16; 4:19.
D.　God's intention in His economy is to put us into Him and to come into us and live in us—3:27; 2:20.
E.　God's economy is the dispensing of Himself into His chosen people to make them His sons for His corporate expression—3:26; 4:6-7.
VI.　God's economy is carried out by God's dispensing:
A.　God's dispensing is the imparting of Himself to us according to His plan and arrangement.
B.　God desires to dispense Himself into His chosen, redeemed, and regenerated people as their life, their life supply, and their everything, making Himself one with them.
C.　God's dispensing is carried out through the Divine Trinity—Eph. 1:4-5, 7-10, 13:
1.　The divine nature is dispensed into the believers in Christ through God the Father's choosing, and the divine life is dispensed through God the Father's predestination.
2.　The divine element, of which the believers in Christ are made God's excellent inheritance, is dispensed into the believers through God the Son's redemption unto God's economy of the fullness of the times, to head up all things in Christ.
3.　The divine essence, in which the believers enjoy the processed Triune God, is dispensed into the believers through God the Spirit's sealing and pledging.
VII.　God's intention in His economy is to build Himself in Christ into His chosen people—Eph. 3:16-17a:
A.　The most crucial and mysterious matter revealed in the Bible is that God's ultimate intention is to work Himself into His chosen people.
B.　The central work of God is to work Himself in Christ into His chosen people, making Himself one with them:
1.　Everything that Christ is and everything that Christ has accomplished are for this one thing.
2.　All the steps that God takes in our daily life are to fulfill His intention of building Himself in Christ into our being.
C.　God's economy and goal according to His heart's desire are to build Himself into our being and to build us into His being in order to mingle His divinity with our humanity into one entity—the Body of Christ, which consummates the New Jerusalem.
VIII.　God's economy is like a great wheel, having Christ as its center—Ezek. 1:15-21:
A.　The hub of this wheel signifies Christ as the center of God's economy.
B.　The rim signifies Christ's counterpart, the church, the Body of Christ.
C.　The believers as the many members of Christ are the spokes of the hub spreading to the rim, to the Body of Christ, which consummates the New Jerusalem.
D.　This great wheel is not only the economy of God but also the moving of the economy of God:
1.　From Genesis 1 until the present, the move of God's economy has never stopped, and today this great wheel has reached us.
2.　In every age and in every generation, this wheel has been moving, and now we are a part of the move of the great wheel of God's economy.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第三篇　神的经纶─神圣启示的中心线
God's Economy— the Central Line of the Divine Revelation
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
壹　神的经纶是神的家庭行政─提前一4：
I.　God's economy is His household administration—1 Tim. 1:4:
一　经纶一辞原文的意思是“家庭律法”，含分配意；指家庭管理，家庭行政，家政，引伸为行政（分配）的安排，计划或经纶，所以也是家庭经营。
A.　The Greek word for?economy?means "household law," implying distribution; it denotes a household management, a household administration, a household government, and, derivatively, a dispensation, a plan, or an economy for administration (distribution); hence, it is also a household economy.
二　神的经纶乃是神的家庭经营，神的家庭行政，要在基督里将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，使祂得着一个家彰显祂自己，这家就是召会，基督的身体。
B.　God's economy is His household economy, His household administration, which is to dispense Himself in Christ into His chosen people that He may have a house to express Himself, which house is the church, the Body of Christ.
贰　我们必须看见神经纶的异象─弗一10：
II.　We need to see a vision of God's economy—Eph. 1:10:
一　神的经纶是祂的计划，要将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选、预定并救赎的人里面，作他们的生命、生命的供应和一切，以产生、构成、并建造基督生机的身体。
A.　God's economy is His plan to dispense Himself into His chosen, predestinated, and redeemed people as their life, their life supply, and their everything to produce, constitute, and build up the organic Body of Christ.
二　神的经纶是要得着一班人，而将祂自己作到他们里面作生命，并将祂自己与他们调和为一，使他们作基督身体的肢体而活祂。
B.　God's economy is to gain a group of people and work Himself into them as life and mingle Himself with them as one so that they may live Him as the members of the Body of Christ.
三　神的经纶是要使蒙祂救赎的人，在生命、性情和显出的样子上成为神，但无分于祂的神格，使祂自己得着一个宇宙、团体的彰显，直到永远。
C.　God's economy is to make His redeemed people God in life, in nature, and in appearance but not in the Godhead so that for eternity He might have a universal, corporate expression of Himself.
四　神的经纶是要使人在生命和性情上与祂完全一样，只是无分于祂的神格，并使祂自己与人成为一，使人与祂成为一，因而在祂的彰显上得以扩大并扩展，使祂一切神圣的属性得以彰显于人性的美德。
D.　God's economy is to make man the same as He is in life and nature but not in His Godhead and to make Himself one with man and man one with Him, thus to be enlarged and expanded in His expression, that all His divine attributes may be expressed in human virtues.
叁　神的经纶与祂的喜悦、意愿、决议和定旨有关─弗一5，9，11，三11，启四11：
III.　God's economy is related to His good pleasure, will, counsel, and purpose—Eph. 1:5, 9, 11; 3:11; Rev. 4:11:
一　神的喜悦是神所喜爱的，神所喜欢的。
A.　God's good pleasure is what God likes, what pleases Him.
二　神的意愿是神的愿望，神渴望，是祂所想要作的。
B.　God's will is God's wish, God's desire; it is what He wants to do.
三　神的决议是祂在神圣三一的会议中所完成的诀议。
C.　God's counsel is His resolution consummated in the council of the Divine Trinity.
四　神的定旨是祂预先的定意。
D.　God's purpose is His intent beforehand.
五　神的意愿是照着祂的喜悦；神的定旨是基于祂的意愿及其决议；神的经纶是祂计划的行政，以完成祂的定旨。
E.　God's will is according to His good pleasure; God's purpose is based on His will with its counsel; and God's economy is His planned administration to carry out His purpose.
肆　神的经纶是在信仰里的─提前一4：
IV.　God's economy is in faith—1 Tim. 1:4:
一　神的经纶是在信仰的的范围和元素里得以开始而发展的。
A.　God's economy is initiated and developed in the sphere and element of faith.
二　神的经纶不是在天然的范围里，也不是在律法的行为里，乃是因着相信基督，借着重生，在新造属灵的范围里─加三23～26：
B.　God's economy is not in the natural realm nor in the work of law but in the spiritual sphere of the new creation through regeneration by faith in Christ—Gal. 3:23-26:
１　因着信，我们由神而生，成为祂的儿子，有分于祂的生命和性情以彰显祂。
1.　By faith we are born of God to be His sons, partaking of His life and nature to express Him.
２　因着信，我们被放在基督里，成为祂身体的肢体，分享祂一切的所是，叫祂得着彰显。
2.　By faith we are put into Christ to become the members of His Body, sharing all that He is for His expression.
伍　加拉太这卷关于神经纶最基本的书，对神经纶的启示是独特的：
V.　Galatians, the most basic book with respect to God's economy, is unique in its revelation of God's economy:
一　神的经纶是神自己在祂神圣的三一里成为赐生命的灵，作我们的生命和一切给我们享受，使祂和我们成为一而彰显祂，直到永远─三14，28。
A.　God's economy is God Himself in His Divine Trinity becoming the life-giving Spirit to be life and everything to us for our enjoyment, so that He and we may be one to express Him for eternity—3:14, 28.
二　神新约经纶的一个基本项目乃是：“我”在基督的死里被钉死，基督在祂的复活里活在我们里面─二20。
B.　A basic item of God's New Testament economy is that "I" be crucified in Christ's death and that Christ live in us in His resurrection—2:20.
三　神新约的经纶是使经过过程的三一神作到我们里面，成为我们的生命和我们的所是─一16，四19。
C.　God's New Testament economy is for the processed Triune God to be wrought into us to become our life and our very being—1:16; 4:19.
四　神在祂经纶里的目的，是要将我们放在祂里面，并进到我们里面，活在我们里面─三27，二20。
D.　God's intention in His economy is to put us into Him and to come into us and live in us—3:27; 2:20.
五　神的经纶是将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，使他们成为祂的儿子，作祂团体的彰显─三26，四6～7。
E.　God's economy is the dispensing of Himself into His chosen people to make them His sons for His corporate expression—3:26; 4:6-7.
陆　神的经纶是借着神的分赐完成的：
VI.　God's economy is carried out by God's dispensing:
一　神的分赐乃是照着神的计划和安排，将祂自己分赐到我们里面。
A.　God's dispensing is the imparting of Himself to us according to His plan and arrangement.
二　神渴望将祂自己分赐到蒙祂拣选、救赎并重生的人里面，作他们的生命、生命的供应和一切，使祂自己与他们成为一。
B.　God desires to dispense Himself into His chosen, redeemed, and regenerated people as their life, their life supply, and their everything, making Himself one with them.
三　神的分赐是借着神圣三一完成的─弗一4～5，7～10，13：
C.　God's dispensing is carried out through the Divine Trinity—Eph. 1:4-5, 7-10, 13:
１　神圣的性情是借着父神的拣选，分赐到在基督里之信徒里面；神圣的生命是借着父神的预定而分赐的。
1.　The divine nature is dispensed into the believers in Christ through God the Father's choosing, and the divine life is dispensed through God the Father's predestination.
２　在基督里的信徒所凭以成为神超越之基业的神圣元素，借着子神的救赎分赐到信徒里面，为着时期满足时之神的经纶，要将万有都在基督里归一于一个元首之下。
2.　The divine element, of which the believers in Christ are made God's excellent inheritance, is dispensed into the believers through God the Son's redemption unto God's economy of the fullness of the times, to head up all things in Christ.
３　信徒在其中所享受经过过程之三一神的神圣素质，借着灵神的印涂和作质，分赐到信徒里面。
3.　The divine essence, in which the believers enjoy the processed Triune God, is dispensed into the believers through God the Spirit's sealing and pledging.
柒　神在祂经纶里的目的，是要将祂自己在基督里建造到祂所拣选的人里面─弗三16～17上：
VII.　God's intention in His economy is to build Himself in Christ into His chosen people—Eph. 3:16-17a:
一　圣经所启示最重要而奥秘的事，乃是神最终的目的是要将祂自己作到祂所拣选的人里面。
A.　The most crucial and mysterious matter revealed in the Bible is that God's ultimate intention is to work Himself into His chosen people.
二　神中心的工作是要将祂自己在基督里作到祂所拣选的人里面，使祂自己与他们成为一：
B.　The central work of God is to work Himself in Christ into His chosen people, making Himself one with them:
１　基督所是的一切和所完成的一切，都是为着这一件事。
1.　Everything that Christ is and everything that Christ has accomplished are for this one thing.
２　神在我们日常生活中所采的一切步骤，都是要成就祂将自己在基督里建造到我们里面的这个目的。
2.　All the steps that God takes in our daily life are to fulfill His intention of building Himself in Christ into our being.
三　神照着祂心愿的经纶和目标，乃是要将祂自己建造到我们里面，并把我们建造到祂里面，好将祂的神性与我们的人性调成一个实体─基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷。
C.　God's economy and goal according to His heart's desire are to build Himself into our being and to build us into His being in order to mingle His divinity with our humanity into one entity—the Body of Christ, which consummates the New Jerusalem.
捌　神的经纶如同一个大轮，有基督为其中心─结一15～21：
VIII.　God's economy is like a great wheel, having Christ as its center—Ezek. 1:15-21:
一　这轮的轮轴，表征基督是神经纶的中心。
A.　The hub of this wheel signifies Christ as the center of God's economy.
二　轮辋，表征基督的配偶，召会，基督的身体。
B.　The rim signifies Christ's counterpart, the church, the Body of Christ.
三　作基督许多肢体的信徒是轮轴的轮辐，扩展到轮辋，扩展到基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷。
C.　The believers as the many members of Christ are the spokes of the hub spreading to the rim, to the Body of Christ, which consummates the New Jerusalem.
四　这个大轮不仅是神的经纶，也是神经纶的行动：
D.　This great wheel is not only the economy of God but also the moving of the economy of God:
１　从创世记一章直到现今，神经纶的行动从未停止，今天这个大轮已经达到我们。
1.　From Genesis 1 until the present, the move of God's economy has never stopped, and today this great wheel has reached us.
２　历世历代这个轮子都在行动，我们现今是神经纶之大轮的行动的一部分。
2.　In every age and in every generation, this wheel has been moving, and now we are a part of the move of the great wheel of God's economy.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE THREE
GOD'S ECONOMY— THE CENTRAL LINE OF THE DIVINE REVELATION
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
It has been a privilege and an honor to be under the apostles' teaching and the New Testament ministry for so many years and to be brought into God's economy. The apostles' teaching is the entire speaking of God in the New Testament. The focal point of the apostles' teaching, from the incarnation of God to the consummation of the New Jerusalem, is the New Testament economy of God. The New Testament ministry is the service rendered by all the members of the Body of Christ to carry out the economy of God. God needs such a service with many ministers of the one unique New Testament ministry to accomplish and carry out His eternal economy. In this message we will see more concerning the eternal economy of God.
GOD'S ECONOMY IS HIS HOUSEHOLD ADMINISTRATION
God's economy is His household administration (1 Tim. 1:4). The entire divine revelation of God in the Bible has a central line, which is the economy of God. In our study of the Bible before we came to the Lord's recovery, most of us never heard the term the economy of God. First Timothy 1:4 says, "Nor to give heed to myths and unending genealogies, which produce questionings rather than God's economy, which is in faith." In translating the phrase God's economy, the King James Version uses the term godly edifying. Similarly, it translates economy as fellowship in Ephesians 3:9 and as dispensation in 1:10. These terms are not adequate. It is difficult to say what godly edifying is, and a dispensation is mainly understood to be a particular period of history in which God moves among His people in a certain way. Brother Nee and Brother Lee were faithful to dig out the anglicized word economy in the divine revelation. God has an economy. It is not merely a dispensation, and it is more than godly edifying or fellowship. It is God's household plan, His arrangement, His administration, to dispense Himself in His riches, in His Trinity as the Father, Son, and Spirit, into His chosen, redeemed, and regenerated elect, that He may have the Body of Christ to express Himself and to be His expansion and spread in the universe.
The Greek Word for Economy Means "Household Law," Implying Distribution
The Greek word for economy means "household law," implying distribution. The base of this word is of the same origin as that for pasture in John 10:9, implying a distribution of the pasture to the flock. It denotes a household management, a household administration, a household government, and, derivatively, a dispensation, a plan, or an economy for administration (distribution). Hence, it is also a household economy. It comes from the Greek oikos, meaning house, and nomos, meaning law, denoting a household law. This implies a distribution. God has a plan; He wants to carry out something in the universe. His economy is for distributing Himself into His chosen people to fulfill His plan.
God's Economy Is His Household Economy, His Household Administration, Which Is to Dispense Himself in Christ into His Chosen People for His House
God's economy is His household economy, His household administration, which is to dispense Himself in Christ into His chosen people that He may have a house to express Himself, which house is the church, the Body of Christ. God's economy is the basic and foundational matter in the Bible. In order to understand the apostles' teaching and the New Testament ministry, we need to see that the focal point of the teaching and the ministry is the New Testament economy of God. His economy is a dispensing arrangement to dispense this wonderful Triune God into all of us that the Body of Christ may be produced to express Christ as the Head of the Body in the universe for all eternity. This is the focus of the apostles' teaching.
WE NEED TO SEE A VISION OF GOD'S ECONOMY
We need to see a vision of God's economy. Ephesians 1:10 says, "Unto the economy of the fullness of the times, to head up all things in Christ, the things in the heavens and the things on the earth, in Him." In every age God is moving, working, and operating to dispense Himself more and more into His chosen people, so that eventually in the New Jerusalem God's dispensing work will have reached its climax. In the whole universe there will be the New Jerusalem as a testimony of God's dispensing in full throughout all the ages of human history.
God's Economy Is His Plan to Dispense Himself into His Chosen, Predestinated, and Redeemed People as Their Life, Their Life Supply, and Their Everything to Produce, Constitute, and Build Up the Organic Body of Christ
God's economy is His plan to dispense Himself into His chosen, predestinated, and redeemed people as their life, their life supply, and their everything to produce, constitute, and build up the organic Body of Christ. The ministry of Brother Nee and Brother Lee brought us into this eternal economy of God. The High Peak of the Vision and the Reality of the Body of Christ, on page 15, provides a history of how the Lord led Brother Lee to see the eternal economy of God:
In Brother Nee the Lord's revelation and vision reached the Body of Christ. It is a wonderful coincidence that at about the time he went into prison in 1952, the Lord began to use me in Taiwan. From 1950 to this day, it has been forty-four years. Do not blame me for speaking a proud word; I am not proud. You know on what point I began in these forty-four years. I began with Christ and the church. Many of the messages concerning these two points have been published in book form. Among these a good number of the messages are on the Body of Christ. Then a little over ten years ago, probably from 1980, the Lord showed me that in order to have the Body of Christ, the dispensing of Christ is indispensable. So I began to speak concerning the dispensing of Christ. If Christ does not dispense Himself into us, how can we become His Body? From that point I went higher and saw the economy of God. Hence, beginning from 1984 I released many messages on the economy of God.
God's Economy Is to Gain a Group of People and Work Himself into Them as Life and Mingle Himself with Them as One So That They May Live Him as the Members of the Body of Christ
God's economy is to gain a group of people and work Himself into them as life and mingle Himself with them as one so that they may live Him as the members of the Body of Christ. God's economy involves a dispensing, mingling work. It is not to make us merely holy, religious, ethical, and moral. It is far deeper and far richer than this. It is a fine work of dispensing to dispense the riches of the Triune God into our being to make us the eternal Body of Christ.
God's Economy Is to Make His Redeemed People God in Life, in Nature, and in Appearance but Not in the Godhead, to Make Man the Same as He Is for His Expression
God's economy is to make His redeemed people God in life, in nature, and in appearance but not in the Godhead so that for eternity He might have a universal, corporate expression of Himself. God's economy is to make man the same as He is in life and nature but not in His Godhead and to make Himself one with man and man one with Him, thus to be enlarged and expanded in His expression, that all His divine attributes may be expressed in human virtues. This understanding concerning God's eternal economy with truth, light, and revelation reached its peak in The Ten Great Critical "Ones" for the Building Up of the Body of Christ, which was released in October 1995. Such statements of the truth are frameable quotations.
GOD'S ECONOMY IS RELATED TO HIS GOOD PLEASURE, WILL, COUNSEL, AND PURPOSE
God's economy is related to His good pleasure, will, counsel, and purpose (Eph. 1:5, 9, 11; 3:11; Rev. 4:11). The eternal economy of God, the dispensing, the arrangement, of God is not a cold, calculated purpose apart from God Himself. God's being, essence, element, and very person are intimately related and involved with His economy. The very being of God was involved in making His plan.
God's Good Pleasure Is What God Likes, What Pleases Him
God's good pleasure is what God likes, what pleases Him. God's economy is related to His good pleasure. We all have a good pleasure, and God also has a good pleasure, something that pleases Him. There is something in this universe that makes God happy. Nothing else in the universe makes Him as happy as dispensing Himself into us. Today we are under His dispensing.
God's Will Is God's Wish, God's Desire; It Is What He Wants to Do
God's will is God's wish, God's desire. God's will springs out of His pleasure, the deep desire within His being. Simply stated, God's will is what He wants to do.
God's Counsel Is His Resolution Consummated in the Council of the Divine Trinity
God's counsel is His resolution consummated in the council of the Divine Trinity. There is something that God is determined to have, and according to His will, in order to gain the desire which springs from His heart, He had a council. Out of the council of the Divine Trinity in eternity past came a counsel, and that counsel was His determination to dispense Himself into the tripartite man.
God's Purpose Is His Intent Beforehand
God's purpose is His intent beforehand to gain His desire in the universe. The entire being of God is intrinsically involved with His pleasure, counsel, will, purpose, and economy. God's emotion is involved with His good pleasure; God's will is involved, determining to gain something; and God's mind is involved, conceiving an economy to carry out His plan.
God's Will Is according to His Good Pleasure; God's Purpose Is Based on His Will with Its Counsel; and God's Economy Is His Planned Administration to Carry Out His Purpose
God's will is according to His good pleasure; God's purpose is based on His will with its counsel; and God's economy is His planned administration to carry out His purpose. God has a purpose and a plan, and He has a determination to carry out this plan to do all things. This requires a marvelous arrangement. It takes God's administration, God's economy, to bring us together for His purpose to dispense Himself with all of His riches into us to form, produce, and build up the Body of Christ.
GOD'S ECONOMY IS IN FAITH
God's Economy Is Initiated and Developed in the Sphere and Element of Faith
God's economy is in faith (1 Tim. 1:4). It is initiated and developed in the sphere and element of faith. It is not in teaching or in doctrine, and it is not carried out in a religious way, in theology, or by religious instruction. Everything that is involved with the eternal economy of God is a matter of faith.
God's Economy Is Not in the Natural Realm nor in the Work of Law but in the Spiritual Sphere of the New Creation through Regeneration by Faith in Christ
God's economy is not in the natural realm nor in the work of law but in the spiritual sphere of the new creation through regeneration by faith in Christ (Gal. 3:23-26). God's economy is not what man can conceive or carry out. It is not what we can do but what He can do and is doing. It is not what we are but what He is. Neither is it a matter of being good or doing the right things. The entire arrangement and dispensing of God are carried out in the realm and sphere of faith, which links us to the wonderful Triune God. This faith is in our spirit as a realm, a sphere, we must enter into. In this realm of faith, the divine element is transfused into us to bring all that the Triune God is and has into our being. The infusing and dispensing of the very Triune God—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit—are in the realm of faith, outside of the natural realm, the religious realm, and all other realms. This dispensing in faith is God's economy carried out in faith, linking us to the very Triune God.
God's economy is in the spiritual sphere of the new creation. We are here as God's new creation through regeneration by faith in Christ. By faith we are born of God to be His sons, partaking of His life and nature to express Him. By faith we are put into Christ to become the members of His Body, sharing all that He is for His expression. We must never forget that God's economy is His household administration. We need to see a vision of this eternal economy of God, which is not separate from the very Triune God Himself but is related to His good pleasure, His will, His counsel, and His purpose and is carried out in the sphere and element of faith.—B. L.
The Bible has sixty-six books and contains many items. It may be compared to a jigsaw puzzle. Through the ministry throughout many years, the Lord has put this jigsaw puzzle together for us bit by bit and piece by piece. Today we can see what the Bible is all about. Although it has so many subjects, points, and characters, it has only one central line. The central line concerns God's economy. Everything, including God, man, creation, and all that God has done, is doing, and will do throughout the entire span of time, has to do with His economy. God's economy is related to His very self; it is not something outside of Him.
God's economy is His plan to dispense Himself into His chosen people as their life and everything to produce and build up the organic Body of Christ. This statement summarizes the whole Bible from Genesis to Revelation. God's economy is His plan, not merely to give us grace, life, truth, and joy, but to dispense His very self into us. God loves us so much that He dispenses His very self to us. We know that God is the Father, the Son, and the Spirit, but without the revelation of His economy, we will not know why He is triune. Our God is triune for the purpose of dispensing Himself, not into the angels, but into His chosen people. His chosen people are created by Him in His image. They have virtues in their natural makeup, but they need God's divine attributes to get into their virtues. God is dispensing Himself in His Trinity into the people created and chosen by Him to be their life and their everything to produce, build up, and constitute the organic Body of Christ in an organic way.
GALATIANS, THE MOST BASIC BOOK WITH RESPECT TO GOD'S ECONOMY, IS UNIQUE IN ITS REVELATION OF GOD'S ECONOMY
Galatians, the most basic book with respect to God's economy, is unique in its revelation of God's economy. This portion of the outline of this message is taken from page 17 of the Life-study of Galatians. It summarizes the entire book of Galatians, pointing out to us in a very particular way what God's economy is. God's economy has absolutely nothing to do with the law. We may say that now that we are saved we would never revert to the law, but even the Galatians became deluded by the law. As a New Testament minister, the apostle Paul was very clear about the distraction among the Galatian believers and the challenge by man's religion. Galatians 1:4 says that Christ "gave Himself for our sins that He might rescue us out of the present evil age according to the will of our God and Father." According to Galatians, the present evil age is the religious age, the religious world which was challenging Paul's ministry. However, Paul was not distracted or confused. He used that opportunity to point out what God's New Testament economy is.
God's Economy Is God Himself in His Divine Trinity Becoming the Life-giving Spirit to Be Life and Everything to Us for Our Enjoyment, So That He and We May Be One to Express Him for Eternity
God's economy is God Himself m His Divine Trinity becoming the life-giving Spirit to be life and everything to us for our enjoyment, so that He and we may be one to express Him for eternity (3:14, 28). In 1:16 Paul says that God's intention is nothing less than to reveal His Son in us. God has no intention that we keep the law. He has only one purpose, which is to reveal His Son in us. This shows us the contrast between God's Son and man's religion. Nothing can be compared with God's Son. In verse 16 Paul does not speak of "His Christ," referring to His work, but of "His Son." To speak of the Son includes the Divine Trinity—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit—because all the fullness of the Godhead is embodied in the Son. In fact, the Son is the very Triune God Himself.
The Son as the embodiment of the Triune God revealed in Paul is the blessing of Abraham, which is the Spirit. Galatians 3:14 says, "In order that the blessing of Abraham might come to the Gentiles in Christ Jesus, that we might receive the promise of the Spirit through faith." In the Old Testament, the blessing of Abraham was the good land, which is a type of the all-inclusive Christ. This indicates that the blessing of Abraham in reality is Christ, the Son of God. However, 3:14 does not say that those who receive the blessing of Abraham receive Christ. Rather, they receive the Spirit. This means that the all-inclusive Christ today is the Spirit. In 3:1-2 Paul says, "O foolish Galatians, who has bewitched you, before whose eyes Jesus Christ was openly portrayed crucified? This only I wish to learn from you, Did you receive the Spirit out of the works of law or out of the hearing of faith?" In verse 1 there is the portrait of the crucified Christ, but verse 2 speaks of receiving the Spirit by faith. The received Spirit in verse 2 is the reality of Christ in verse 1. Chapter one tells us that God is pleased to reveal His Son in us, while chapter three tells us that the Son, the all-inclusive Christ, is the blessing of the Spirit. It also tells us that the One who is crucified is Jesus Christ, but the One who is given to us is the Spirit. Putting all these verses together is like assembling a jigsaw puzzle; they reveal the Divine Trinity becoming the life-giving Spirit.
God's economy is God Himself in His Divine Trinity becoming the life-giving Spirit to be life and everything to us. We receive Christ and put Him on by faith. Faith is not something objective; it involves an organic union with God. By faith we are joined to Christ, and by faith we are born of God. By faith we get into Christ, not only to be objectively identified with Him, but to be joined to Him in an organic way so that we are in Him and He is in us. In this way He becomes life and everything to us for our enjoyment so that He and we may be one to express Him for eternity.
Galatians shows us how Christ is versus the law, which works through the flesh. There is no enjoyment in the law, but Christ as grace is enjoyment to us. In 2:21 Paul says that he did not nullify the grace of God. Grace is the processed and consummated Triune God, who passed through incarnation, human living, death, resurrection, and ascension, and who became the life-giving Spirit to be our enjoyment as our life and everything to us. Grace is not merely something that God gives; grace is the enjoyment of God Himself. This is versus the law and is much better than the law.
The result of our organic union with God is that we become the Body of Christ. Galatians 3:28 says, "There cannot be Jew nor Greek, there cannot be slave nor free man, there cannot be male and female; for you are all one in Christ Jesus." To be a Jew or a Gentile is a natural distinction in the natural realm. In the natural realm we have distinctions of race, gender, and social status, but all natural distinctions are gone when we are one in Christ. This and the foregoing points summarize the book of Galatians.
A Basic Item of God's New Testament Economy Is That "I" Be Crucified in Christ's Death and That Christ Live in Us in His Resurrection
A basic item of God's New Testament economy is that "I" be crucified in Christ's death and that Christ live in us in His resurrection. Galatians 2:20 says, "I am crucified with Christ; and it is no longer I who live, but it is Christ who lives in me; and the life which I now live in the flesh I live in faith, the faith of the Son of God, who loved me and gave Himself up for me." The first "I" is the old "I," but Christ lives in the new "I," concerning which Paul said, "I live." It is not that Christ lives instead of me, but that Christ lives in me. This indicates the organic union between the processed and consummated Triune God as the life-giving Spirit and us as human beings. We two are mingled together as one life with one living. This is accomplished by the old "I" being crucified and by Christ's indwelling in His resurrection to produce the grafted life, two lives becoming one. The grafted life is the very essence of God's economy. God's economy has nothing to do with the law, the Sabbath, controlling our temper, or becoming holy in an outward way. It has to do with Christ living in us as one life with one living. This is the uplifted view of God's economy.
God's New Testament Economy Is for the Processed Triune God to Be Wrought into Us to Become Our Life and Our Very Being
God's New Testament economy is for the processed Triune God to be wrought into us to become our life and our very being (1:16; 4:19). God first works Himself into us by revealing His Son in us. The revelation of Christ is a searing vision. When Paul saw this vision, it wrought something into him; it was a seeing that he could not deny. God is wrought into us further by His Son being formed in us. Christ's being formed in us is His being worked into us in a permanent way. This may be compared to the way information is written on a computer CD-ROM. When the CD is written on by being seared with a laser, it becomes permanent memory. From that day on it is of no use except for what has been programmed onto it. From the time Paul was "programmed" by Christ, he was good for nothing else. The processed Triune God is wrought into us to become our life and our very being.
God's Intention in His Economy Is to Put Us into Him and to Come into Us and Live in Us
God's intention in His economy is to put us into Him and to come into us and live in us (3:27; 2:20). In 3:27 Paul says, "For as many as were baptized into Christ have put on Christ." The New Testament says that we are baptized into the Triune God (Matt. 28:19), into Christ, into the death of Christ (Rom. 6:3), and into the Body of Christ (1 Cor. 12:13). This fourfold baptism brings us into a different realm: a wonderful person, an effective death, and a living organism. Baptism is not a ritual; it brings us into a mystical and spiritual union with the processed and consummated Triune God. Through baptism we are put into Him, and He comes into us and lives in us.
God's Economy Is the Dispensing of Himself into His Chosen People to Make Them His Sons for His Corporate Expression
God's economy is the dispensing of Himself into His chosen people to make them His sons for His corporate expression (Gal. 3:26; 4:6-7). The goal of God's economy is to make us His sons. We are His creatures by our first birth, but God is doing something beyond creation. Through regeneration He dispenses Himself into us to make us His very sons with His life and nature. The word son denotes life, maturity, position, and privilege. To be God's sons also means that we have God's expression, God's perfection, and God's inheritance. Life pertains to His expression, maturity pertains to His perfection, and position and privilege pertain to His inheritance. Galatians tells us that we are made not only sons of God but heirs of God. By all this we can see that God's economy is not merely to make us holy and right according to the law but to make us people who are sons, having the life and nature of God to grow unto the same maturity and inherit the same inheritance by having the same position and the same privilege.
GOD'S ECONOMY IS CARRIED OUT BY GOD'S DISPENSING
God's Dispensing Is the Imparting of Himself to His People according to His Plan and Arrangement as Their Life, Their Life Supply, and Their Everything, Making Himself One with Them
God's economy is carried out by God's dispensing. God's dispensing is the imparting of Himself to us according to His plan and arrangement. God desires to dispense Himself into His chosen, redeemed, and regenerated people as their life, their life supply, and their everything, making Himself one with them. Dispensing is not only a matter of distribution; it is a matter of eating. When we eat, the riches of the food are dispensed into all the cells in our body to build up and constitute our body. This is a picture of God's dispensing to impart Himself to us.
God's Dispensing Is Carried Out through the Divine Trinity
The Divine Nature Is Dispensed into the Believers in Christ through God the Father's Choosing, and the Divine Life Is Dispensed through God the Father's Predestination
God's dispensing is carried out through the Divine Trinity (Eph. 1:4-5, 7-10, 13). Ephesians 1 speaks of the Body of Christ, which is built up in an organic way through the dispensing of the Triune God. The divine nature is dispensed into the believers in Christ through God the Fathers choosing, and the divine life is dispensed through God the Father's predestination. The work of God the Father was to choose us to be holy and predestinate us to be His sons. This is related to His divine nature and His divine life respectively. To be holy is a matter of His divine nature, while to be His sons is a matter of His divine life.
The Divine Element, of Which the Believers in Christ Are Made God's Excellent Inheritance, Is Dispensed into the Believers through God the Son's Redemption
The divine element, of which the believers in Christ are made God's excellent inheritance, is dispensed into the believers through God the Son's redemption unto God's economy of the fullness of the times, to head up all things in Christ. The work of the Son is to redeem us. We are redeemed in Christ, that is, in the sphere and realm of Christ, and by being redeemed, we become an inheritance to Him. The phrase in Him in Galatians 1:10 is very important. We do not receive our redemption in an objective way. Redemption brings us into Him. We may illustrate this with an oyster. A pearl is formed in an oyster after a grain of sand gets into the oyster. By getting into the oyster, the sand is in the realm of the oyster. Then the oyster secretes its element until the grain of sand becomes a pearl, which is a great treasure. This is the meaning of being redeemed in Christ: to be redeemed in Christ, we enter into Him in whom we have redemption. This redemption brings in a dispensing of Himself with His element until we become His excellent inheritance.
The Divine Essence, in Which the Believers Enjoy the Processed Triune God, Is Dispensed into the Believers through God the Spirit's Sealing and Pledging
The divine essence, in which the believers enjoy the processed Triune God, is dispensed into the believers through God the Spirit's sealing and pledging. The work of the Spirit is to seal us. The sealing "ink" is the essence of the processed and consummated Triune God as the final manifestation of the Divine Trinity. This One as the ink is sealing us all the time. This sealing started from the day we were saved, and it has never stopped. This ink is continually moving to dispense the Triune God Himself into us daily. The dispensing of the Triune God—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit—into us makes us the very organic Body of Christ.
GOD'S INTENTION IN HIS ECONOMY IS TO BUILD HIMSELF IN CHRIST INTO HIS CHOSEN PEOPLE
God's intention in His economy is to build Himself in Christ into His chosen people (Eph. 3:16-17a). This building is not an objective, material building. It is an organic building built by divinity with humanity. It is divinity built into humanity and humanity built into divinity. This is the building that God is after. In the Old Testament, David was a man after God's heart, but God desired something more than a man of integrity, a man after His heart. In 2 Samuel 7:12-14, God promised David that He would raise up a seed for him who would build a house for God. Moreover, this seed would be a son to the Father, and God would be a Father to him. The seed of David is Christ, the seed-Son, the One who accomplishes the building. In this prophecy we can see God's economy. According to Romans 1:3-4, the seed is Christ in His humanity. By resurrection Christ's humanity was designated the Son of God; in His humanity He became the Son of God. Humanity and divinity are built into one another to become a building. This is what God is building today. God has no interest in building a huge cathedral. His interest is to build divinity into humanity and humanity into divinity.
The most crucial and mysterious matter revealed in the Bible is that God's ultimate intention is to work Himself into His chosen people. The central work of God is to work Himself in Christ into His chosen people, making Himself one with them. Everything that Christ is and everything that Christ has accomplished are for this one thing. All the steps that God takes in our daily life are to fulfill His intention of building Himself in Christ into our being. God's economy and goal according to His heart's desire are to build Himself into our being and to build us into His being in order to mingle His divinity with our humanity into one entity—the Body of Christ, which consummates the New Jerusalem.
GOD'S ECONOMY IS LIKE A GREAT WHEEL, HAVING CHRIST AS ITS CENTER
God's economy is like a great wheel, having Christ as its center (Ezek. 1:15-21). All the foregoing points can be summed up by this one great wheel. God's economy is not a doctrine or a theology; it is like the great wheel revealed in Ezekiel 1.
The Hub of This Wheel Signifies Christ as the Center of God's Economy
The hub of this wheel signifies Christ as the center of God's economy. A wheel indicates a move. However, this is not an ordinary move. In this move the hub, the center, is Christ Himself.
The Rim Signifies Christ's Counterpart, the Church, the Body of Christ
The rim signifies Christ's counterpart, the church, the Body of Christ. We must never forget that Christ is the very processed and consummated Triune God in His embodiment, and He has now passed through all the processes to become the life-giving Spirit. Through faith we have been regenerated by the life-giving Spirit, and by regeneration we have received His life and nature to become the Body of Christ, which is the church, the rim of the great wheel.
The Believers as the Many Members of Christ Are the Spokes of the Hub Spreading to the Rim, to the Body of Christ, Which Consummates the New Jerusalem
The believers as the many members of Christ are the spokes of the hub spreading to the rim, to the Body of Christ, which consummates the New Jerusalem. God's move starts from the center and goes out until it reaches the rim, the Body of Christ.
This Great Wheel Is Not Only the Economy of God but Also the Moving of the Economy of God
This great wheel is not only the economy of God but also the moving of the economy of God. This wheel is not static; it is moving, and while it is moving, it is bringing the whole universe along with it. This is the only move that counts in the whole universe. Whether or not one moves to Anaheim does not count. The only move that counts is the move of the Triune God with Christ as the hub, the believers as the spokes, and the Body of Christ as the rim. From Genesis 1 until the present, the move of God's economy has never stopped, and today this great wheel has reached us. In every age and in every generation, this wheel has been moving, and now we are a part of the move of the great wheel of God's economy. We praise the Lord for the ministry that has brought us into the universal move of God's economy—A. Y.

TOP-纲目|Outline|对照-目录
　
　
第四篇　三一神─三而一的神为着祂神圣的分赐完成祂永远的经纶
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　在旧约里，神有两个基本的神圣称谓：
一　以罗欣，（创一1，）用于与神的创造有关之事上；这名为复数形，含示神圣的三一，因此是指那独一而三一的神。─引用经文
二　耶和华，（创二4，）用于神与人的关系上；这名按字面的意思是“那是祂所是者，所以是那永远的我是”，因此指三一神不仅是永存的，也是永是的。─引用经文
贰　神是三一的，就是三而一的：
一　神只有一位─诗八六10，赛四五5，林前八4。
二　神有父子灵三者的讲究─太二八19。
叁　神圣三一的三者是从永远到永远同时并存：
一　父子灵三者都是神：
１　父是神─彼前一2，弗一17。
２　子是神─来一8，约一1，罗九5。
３　灵是神─徒五3～4。
二　父子灵三者都是永远的：
１　父是永远的─赛九6。
２　子是永远的─来一12，七3。
３　灵是永远的─来九14。
三　父子灵三者，从永远到永远同时并存─约十四16～17，弗三14～17，林后十三14。
肆　神圣三一的三者永远互相内在：
一　父子灵彼此相互的内住─约十四10～11，26，十五26。
二　父子灵在祂们的互相内在里同时并存；因此，三者虽有分别，却不分开─约五19，43，八29，十六32，路一35，太一18，20，路四1，18上，太十二28。
伍　素质的三一是指三一神的素质，为着祂的存在：
一　子是父的具体化身，（西二9，）灵是子的实际。（约十四16～18。）─引用经文
二　父子灵在素质上是一，由以下所证明：
１　有一子赐给我们，但祂的名却称为永远的父─赛九6。
２　子这末后的亚当，成了赐生命的灵─林前十五45下。
３　主就是那灵，（林后三17，）又是主灵。（18。）─引用经文
陆　经纶的三一是指三一神的计划，为着祂的行动：
一　父是起源者，制定了神圣的经纶；（弗一9～10，三9，提前一4下；）子完成了父所制定的神圣经纶；（约五19，八28；）灵将子所完成的应用在神的选民身上。（十六13。）─引用经文
二　父子灵在经纶上乃是三。但祂们在经纶的神圣三一里仍然是和谐一致的，（约十30，十七21，23，）由以下所证明：─引用经文
１　父在天上说到子，子在地上站在水里，灵如同鸽子在空中飞翔─太三16～17。
２　父在创立世界以前拣选了信徒，子在时间里救赎了他们，灵在他们信了子以后印涂他们─弗一4，6～7，13。
柒　神圣的三一是为着将神分赐到祂所拣选的人里面：
一　三一神按着祂心愿的永远经纶，是要使人在生命和性情上像祂一样，但不像祂一样具有神格，因而在祂的彰显上被套扩大并扩展。
二　这事的完成是借着：照着祂的形像并按着祂的样式造人（创一26～27，）在祂成为肉体时成为人，有分于人的性情，（来二14上，）过人性生活，借着人的美德彰显祂的属性，经过包罗万有的死，复活成为神的长子和赐生命的灵，（罗八29，徒十三33，林前十五45，）将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，以祂自己作他们的生命重生他们，为着产生许多儿子，（彼前一3，）以祂许多的儿子形成众召会，并以基督的弟兄作肢体建造基督的身体，作经过过程并终极完成之三一神的生机体，终极完成新耶路撒冷，作祂永远的扩大和彰显。─引用经文
三　神要完成祂的分赐，就必须是三一的：
１　父作起源，乃是源─耶二13。
２　子作彰显，乃是泉─约四14。
３　灵作传输，乃是流─河（启二二1）─三一神的临及与应用。
四　林后十三章十四节说：“愿主耶稣基督的恩，神的爱，圣灵的交通，与你们众人同在，”给我们看见，神圣的三一不是给我们在道理上领会系统的神学，而是为着将神自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，以完成祂的经纶。
捌　神在祂神圣的三一里，乃是一个合并，祂经过了种种的过程，而与人合并为一个扩大、宇宙、神人二性的合并，终极完成新耶路撒冷：
一　神在祂神圣的三一里，乃是一个合并─约十四10～11：
１　借着互相内在。
２　借着在一起是一的行事。
二　三一神在已过的永远里举行了一个会议，（徒二23，）定意要将祂们中间的第二者成为人，历经人性生活、死与复活的种种过程，使所有蒙神救赎和重生的信徒，都合并到神这个合并里，成为一个扩大的合并。─引用经文
三　经过过程并终极完成的三一神与蒙救赎和重生的信徒，在基督的复活里成了一个扩大、宇宙、神人二性的合并，（约十四20，）终极完成新耶路撒冷，作为团体的神─神的扩大、扩展和彰显。
参读　关于父子灵三而一的神；主今日恢复之主要项目的重点；长老训练，第五册；关于主今日行动的交通，第二章；神新约的经纶，第七章；基督为父用神圣的荣耀所荣耀的结果，第三章。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message Four
The Triune God— the Three-one God for His Divine Dispensing to Carry Out His Eternal Economy
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　There are two basic divine titles for God in the Old Testament:
A.　Elohim?(Gen. 1:1) is used in relation to God's creation, and its plurality implies the Divine Trinity, thus denoting the unique yet triune God.
B.　Jehovah?(Gen. 2:4) is used in God's relationship with man, and it literally means "He that is who He is; therefore, the eternal I Am," thus denoting the Triune God as the One who is not only eternally existing but also eternally being.
II.　God is triune, three-one:
A.　God is only one—Psa. 86:10; Isa. 45:5; 1 Cor. 8:4.
B.　God has the aspect of three—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit—Matt. 28:19.
III.　The three of the Divine Trinity are eternally coexistent:
A.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are all God:
1.　The Father is God—1 Pet. 1:2; Eph. 1:17.
2.　The Son is God—Heb. 1:8; John 1:1; Rom. 9:5.
3.　The Spirit is God—Acts 5:3-4.
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are all eternal:
1.　The Father is eternal—Isa. 9:6.
2.　The Son is eternal—Heb. 1:12; 7:3.
3.　The Spirit is eternal—Heb. 9:14.
C.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit coexist simultaneously from eternity to eternity—John 14:16-17; Eph. 3:14-17; 2 Cor. 13:14.
IV.　The three of the Divine Trinity are eternally coinherent:
A.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit mutually indwell one another—John 14:10-11, 26; 15:26.
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit coexist in Their coinherence, and are thus distinct but not separate—John 5:19, 43; 8:29; 16:32; Luke 1:35; Matt. 1:18, 20; Luke 4:1, 18a; Matt. 12:28.
V.　The essential Trinity refers to the essence of the Triune God for His existence:
A.　The Son is the embodiment of the Father (Col. 2:9), and the Spirit is the reality of the Son (John 14:16-18).
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are essentially one, as evidenced by the following:
1.　A Son is given to us, yet His name is called the eternal Father—Isa 9:6.
2.　The Son as the last Adam became the life-giving Spirit—1 Cor. 15:45b.
3.　The Lord is the Spirit (2 Cor. 3:17) and the Lord Spirit (v. 18).
VI.　The economical Trinity refers to the plan of the Triune God for His move:
A.　The Father as the Originator makes the divine economy (Eph. 1:9-10; 3:9; 1 Tim. 1:4b); the Son accomplishes the divine economy made by the Father (John 5:19; 8:28); and the Spirit applies to God's elect what the Son has accomplished (16:13).
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are economically three. Yet They are still one in harmony in the economical Trinity (John 10:30; 17:21, 23), as evidenced by the following:
1.　The Father spoke in heaven concerning the Son, the Son stood in the water on the earth, and the Spirit soared as the dove in the air—Matt. 3:16-17.
2.　The Father chose the believers before the foundation of the world, the Son redeemed them in time, and the Spirit sealed them after they believed in the Son—Eph. 1:4, 6-7, 13.
VII.　The Divine Trinity is for the dispensing of God into His chosen people:
A.　The Triune God's eternal economy according to His heart's desire is to make man the same as He is in life and nature but not in His Godhead, and thus to be enlarged and expanded in His expression.
B.　This is accomplished by creating man in His image and after His likeness (Gen. 1:26-27), becoming a man in His incarnation to partake of the human nature (Heb. 2:14a), living a human life to express His attributes through man's virtues, dying an all-inclusive death, resurrecting to become the firstborn Son of God and the life-giving Spirit (Rom. 8:29; Acts 13:33; 1 Cor. 15:45), dispensing Himself into His chosen people to regenerate them with Himself as their life for producing many sons (1 Pet. 1:3), forming the churches with His many sons, and building up the Body of Christ with His brothers as the members to be the organism of the processed and consummated Triune God to consummate the New Jerusalem as His eternal enlargement and expression.
C.　To carry out His dispensing, God needs to be triune:
1.　The Father as the origin is the fountain—Jer. 2:13.
2.　The Son as the expression is the spring—John 4:14.
3.　The Spirit as the transmission is the flow—the river (Rev. 22:1)—the reaching and the application of the Triune God.
D.　Second Corinthians 13:14 says, "The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ and the love of God and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all," showing that the Divine Trinity is not for the doctrinal understanding of systematic theology but for the dispensing of God Himself into His chosen people to accomplish His economy.
VIII.　God in His Divine Trinity is an incorporation and He passed through all the processes to be incorporated with man to be an enlarged, universal, divine-human incorporation, consummating the New Jerusalem:
A.　God in His Divine Trinity is an incorporation—John 14:10-11:
1.　By coinhering mutually.
2.　By working together as one.
B.　The Triune God in eternity past held a council (Acts 2:23) to make a decision that the second among Them had to become a man and pass through the processes of human living, death, and resurrection so that all the redeemed and regenerated believers of God would be incorporated into God's incorporation to be an enlarged incorporation.
C.　The processed and consummated Triune God and the redeemed and regenerated believers became an enlarged, universal, divine-human incorporation in the resurrection of Christ (John 14:20), consummating the New Jerusalem as the corporate God—the enlargement, expansion, and expression of God.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第四篇　三一神─三而一的神为着祂神圣的分赐完成祂永远的经纶
The Triune God— the Three-one God for His Divine Dispensing to Carry Out His Eternal Economy
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
壹　在旧约里，神有两个基本的神圣称谓：
I.　There are two basic divine titles for God in the Old Testament:
一　以罗欣，（创一1，）用于与神的创造有关之事上；这名为复数形，含示神圣的三一，因此是指那独一而三一的神。─引用经文
A.　Elohim?(Gen. 1:1) is used in relation to God's creation, and its plurality implies the Divine Trinity, thus denoting the unique yet triune God.
二　耶和华，（创二4，）用于神与人的关系上；这名按字面的意思是“那是祂所是者，所以是那永远的我是”，因此指三一神不仅是永存的，也是永是的。─引用经文
B.　Jehovah?(Gen. 2:4) is used in God's relationship with man, and it literally means "He that is who He is; therefore, the eternal I Am," thus denoting the Triune God as the One who is not only eternally existing but also eternally being.
贰　神是三一的，就是三而一的：
II.　God is triune, three-one:
一　神只有一位─诗八六10，赛四五5，林前八4。
A.　God is only one—Psa. 86:10; Isa. 45:5; 1 Cor. 8:4.
二　神有父子灵三者的讲究─太二八19。
B.　God has the aspect of three—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit—Matt. 28:19.
叁　神圣三一的三者是从永远到永远同时并存：
III.　The three of the Divine Trinity are eternally coexistent:
一　父子灵三者都是神：
A.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are all God:
１　父是神─彼前一2，弗一17。
1.　The Father is God—1 Pet. 1:2; Eph. 1:17.
２　子是神─来一8，约一1，罗九5。
2.　The Son is God—Heb. 1:8; John 1:1; Rom. 9:5.
３　灵是神─徒五3～4。
3.　The Spirit is God—Acts 5:3-4.
二　父子灵三者都是永远的：
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are all eternal:
１　父是永远的─赛九6。
1.　The Father is eternal—Isa. 9:6.
２　子是永远的─来一12，七3。
2.　The Son is eternal—Heb. 1:12; 7:3.
３　灵是永远的─来九14。
3.　The Spirit is eternal—Heb. 9:14.
三　父子灵三者，从永远到永远同时并存─约十四16～17，弗三14～17，林后十三14。
C.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit coexist simultaneously from eternity to eternity—John 14:16-17; Eph. 3:14-17; 2 Cor. 13:14.
肆　神圣三一的三者永远互相内在：
IV.　The three of the Divine Trinity are eternally coinherent:
一　父子灵彼此相互的内住─约十四10～11，26，十五26。
A.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit mutually indwell one another—John 14:10-11, 26; 15:26.
二　父子灵在祂们的互相内在里同时并存；因此，三者虽有分别，却不分开─约五19，43，八29，十六32，路一35，太一18，20，路四1，18上，太十二28。
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit coexist in Their coinherence, and are thus distinct but not separate—John 5:19, 43; 8:29; 16:32; Luke 1:35; Matt. 1:18, 20; Luke 4:1, 18a; Matt. 12:28.
伍　素质的三一是指三一神的素质，为着祂的存在：
V.　The essential Trinity refers to the essence of the Triune God for His existence:
一　子是父的具体化身，（西二9，）灵是子的实际。（约十四16～18。）─引用经文
A.　The Son is the embodiment of the Father (Col. 2:9), and the Spirit is the reality of the Son (John 14:16-18).
二　父子灵在素质上是一，由以下所证明：
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are essentially one, as evidenced by the following:
１　有一子赐给我们，但祂的名却称为永远的父─赛九6。
1.　A Son is given to us, yet His name is called the eternal Father—Isa 9:6.
２　子这末后的亚当，成了赐生命的灵─林前十五45下。
2.　The Son as the last Adam became the life-giving Spirit—1 Cor. 15:45b.
３　主就是那灵，（林后三17，）又是主灵。（18。）─引用经文
3.　The Lord is the Spirit (2 Cor. 3:17) and the Lord Spirit (v. 18).
陆　经纶的三一是指三一神的计划，为着祂的行动：
VI.　The economical Trinity refers to the plan of the Triune God for His move:
一　父是起源者，制定了神圣的经纶；（弗一9～10，三9，提前一4下；）子完成了父所制定的神圣经纶；（约五19，八28；）灵将子所完成的应用在神的选民身上。（十六13。）─引用经文
A.　The Father as the Originator makes the divine economy (Eph. 1:9-10; 3:9; 1 Tim. 1:4b); the Son accomplishes the divine economy made by the Father (John 5:19; 8:28); and the Spirit applies to God's elect what the Son has accomplished (16:13).
二　父子灵在经纶上乃是三。但祂们在经纶的神圣三一里仍然是和谐一致的，（约十30，十七21，23，）由以下所证明：─引用经文
B.　The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are economically three. Yet They are still one in harmony in the economical Trinity (John 10:30; 17:21, 23), as evidenced by the following:
１　父在天上说到子，子在地上站在水里，灵如同鸽子在空中飞翔─太三16～17。
1.　The Father spoke in heaven concerning the Son, the Son stood in the water on the earth, and the Spirit soared as the dove in the air—Matt. 3:16-17.
２　父在创立世界以前拣选了信徒，子在时间里救赎了他们，灵在他们信了子以后印涂他们─弗一4，6～7，13。
2.　The Father chose the believers before the foundation of the world, the Son redeemed them in time, and the Spirit sealed them after they believed in the Son—Eph. 1:4, 6-7, 13.
柒　神圣的三一是为着将神分赐到祂所拣选的人里面：
VII.　The Divine Trinity is for the dispensing of God into His chosen people:
一　三一神按着祂心愿的永远经纶，是要使人在生命和性情上像祂一样，但不像祂一样具有神格，因而在祂的彰显上被套扩大并扩展。
A.　The Triune God's eternal economy according to His heart's desire is to make man the same as He is in life and nature but not in His Godhead, and thus to be enlarged and expanded in His expression.
二　这事的完成是借着：照着祂的形像并按着祂的样式造人（创一26～27，）在祂成为肉体时成为人，有分于人的性情，（来二14上，）过人性生活，借着人的美德彰显祂的属性，经过包罗万有的死，复活成为神的长子和赐生命的灵，（罗八29，徒十三33，林前十五45，）将祂自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，以祂自己作他们的生命重生他们，为着产生许多儿子，（彼前一3，）以祂许多的儿子形成众召会，并以基督的弟兄作肢体建造基督的身体，作经过过程并终极完成之三一神的生机体，终极完成新耶路撒冷，作祂永远的扩大和彰显。─引用经文
B.　This is accomplished by creating man in His image and after His likeness (Gen. 1:26-27), becoming a man in His incarnation to partake of the human nature (Heb. 2:14a), living a human life to express His attributes through man's virtues, dying an all-inclusive death, resurrecting to become the firstborn Son of God and the life-giving Spirit (Rom. 8:29; Acts 13:33; 1 Cor. 15:45), dispensing Himself into His chosen people to regenerate them with Himself as their life for producing many sons (1 Pet. 1:3), forming the churches with His many sons, and building up the Body of Christ with His brothers as the members to be the organism of the processed and consummated Triune God to consummate the New Jerusalem as His eternal enlargement and expression.
三　神要完成祂的分赐，就必须是三一的：
C.　To carry out His dispensing, God needs to be triune:
１　父作起源，乃是源─耶二13。
1.　The Father as the origin is the fountain—Jer. 2:13.
２　子作彰显，乃是泉─约四14。
2.　The Son as the expression is the spring—John 4:14.
３　灵作传输，乃是流─河（启二二1）─三一神的临及与应用。
3.　The Spirit as the transmission is the flow—the river (Rev. 22:1)—the reaching and the application of the Triune God.
四　林后十三章十四节说：“愿主耶稣基督的恩，神的爱，圣灵的交通，与你们众人同在，”给我们看见，神圣的三一不是给我们在道理上领会系统的神学，而是为着将神自己分赐到祂所拣选的人里面，以完成祂的经纶。
D.　Second Corinthians 13:14 says, "The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ and the love of God and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all," showing that the Divine Trinity is not for the doctrinal understanding of systematic theology but for the dispensing of God Himself into His chosen people to accomplish His economy.
捌　神在祂神圣的三一里，乃是一个合并，祂经过了种种的过程，而与人合并为一个扩大、宇宙、神人二性的合并，终极完成新耶路撒冷：
VIII.　God in His Divine Trinity is an incorporation and He passed through all the processes to be incorporated with man to be an enlarged, universal, divine-human incorporation, consummating the New Jerusalem:
一　神在祂神圣的三一里，乃是一个合并─约十四10～11：
A.　God in His Divine Trinity is an incorporation—John 14:10-11:
１　借着互相内在。
1.　By coinhering mutually.
２　借着在一起是一的行事。
2.　By working together as one.
二　三一神在已过的永远里举行了一个会议，（徒二23，）定意要将祂们中间的第二者成为人，历经人性生活、死与复活的种种过程，使所有蒙神救赎和重生的信徒，都合并到神这个合并里，成为一个扩大的合并。─引用经文
B.　The Triune God in eternity past held a council (Acts 2:23) to make a decision that the second among Them had to become a man and pass through the processes of human living, death, and resurrection so that all the redeemed and regenerated believers of God would be incorporated into God's incorporation to be an enlarged incorporation.
三　经过过程并终极完成的三一神与蒙救赎和重生的信徒，在基督的复活里成了一个扩大、宇宙、神人二性的合并，（约十四20，）终极完成新耶路撒冷，作为团体的神─神的扩大、扩展和彰显。
C.　The processed and consummated Triune God and the redeemed and regenerated believers became an enlarged, universal, divine-human incorporation in the resurrection of Christ (John 14:20), consummating the New Jerusalem as the corporate God—the enlargement, expansion, and expression of God.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE FOUR
THE TRIUNE GOD— THE THREE-ONE GOD FOR HIS DIVINE DISPENSING TO CARRY OUT HIS ETERNAL ECONOMY
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
Today the Lord's recovery throughout the earth is in one accord by the one teaching of the apostles, in the one New Testament ministry, and for the one economy of God. This is a great comfort to us at this time. Having established a foundation in the last three messages, we now come to the main items of the apostles' teaching, the first of which is God Himself, the Triune God, the three-one God for His divine dispensing to carry out His eternal economy. When Brother Lee came to America, his teaching was a challenge to the Christianity of this top Christian country. One of the main things that he taught was the Triune God, or the Divine Trinity. He fought against tritheism, which is perhaps one of the greatest heresies which has blinded many Christians who unknowingly and subconsciously believe In three God's. Two verses concerning the Triune God may be considered characteristic of the Lord's recovery. The first is Isaiah 9:6, which says, "For a child is born to us, / A son is given to us; / And the government / Is upon His shoulders; / And His name will be called / Wonderful Counselor, / Mighty God, / Eternal Father, / Prince of Peace." The child born is called the mighty God, and the Son given is called Eternal Father. This one verse is a strong pillar in the Lord's recovery showing us that the Son is the Father. The other verse is 1 Corinthians 15:45b, which says, "The last Adam became a life-giving Spirit." This verse shows us that today the Son, the resurrected Christ, is the life-giving Spirit. Moreover, this life-giving Spirit is not a Spirit other than the Holy Spirit in the Divine Trinity. These two verses "shoot down" the old, traditional, tritheistic theology. We have to pay tribute to our brother by recognizing that what is so matter-of-fact and common to us, yet wonderful, was not gained easily. It was recovered by a battle fought over many years through much suffering, slandering, maligning, and opposition. Because of the sacrifice that our brother made, we can know the Triune God today in truth and in experience.
Second Corinthians 13:14 speaks of the Triune God, saying, "The grace of the Lord Jesus Christ and the love of God and the fellowship of the Holy Spirit be with you all." Footnote 1 of this verse in the Recovery Version says,
This verse is strong proof that the trinity of the Godhead is not for the doctrinal understanding of systematic theology but for the dispensing of God Himself in His trinity into His chosen and redeemed people. In the Bible the Trinity is never revealed merely as a doctrine. It is always revealed or mentioned in regard to the relationship of God with His creatures, especially with man, who was created by Him, and more particularly with His chosen and redeemed people. The first divine title used in the divine revelation, Elohim in Hebrew, a title used in relation to God's creation, is plural in number (Gen. 1:1), implying that God, as the Creator of the heavens and the earth for man, is triune. Concerning His creation of man in His own image, after His own likeness, He used the plural pronouns Us and Our, referring to His trinity (Gen. 1:26) and implying that He would be one with man and express Himself through man in His trinity. Later, in Gen. 3:22 and 11:7 and Isa. 6:8, He referred to Himself again and again as Us in regard to His relationship with man and with His chosen people.
In order to redeem fallen man that He might again have the position to be one with man, He became incarnated (John 1:1, 14) in the Son and through the Spirit (Luke 1:31-35) to be a man, and lived a human life on the earth, also in the Son (Luke 2:49) and by the Spirit (Luke 4:1; Matt. 12:28). At the beginning of His ministry on the earth, the Father anointed the Son with the Spirit (Matt. 3:16-17; Luke 4:18) in order that He might reach men and bring them back to Him. Just before He was crucified in the flesh and resurrected to become the life-giving Spirit (1 Cor. 15:45), He unveiled His mysterious trinity to His disciples in plain words (John 14—17), stating that the Son is in the Father and the Father is in the Son (John 14:9-11), that the Spirit is the transfiguration of the Son (John 14:16-20), that the three, coexisting and coinhering simultaneously, are abiding with the believers for their enjoyment (John 14:23; 17:21-230, and that all that the Father has is the Son's and all that the Son possesses is received by the Spirit to be declared to the believers (John 16:13-15). Such a Trinity is altogether related to the dispensing of the processed God into His believers (John 14:17, 20; 15:4-5) that they may be one in and with the Triune God (John 17:21-23).
Such a speaking as this is wonderful, complete, and clear. The points of the truth in this message are very vital. The many young ones and new ones among us in particular must have a sober mind to study the outline of this message in order to know the practical and proper truth concerning the Triune God.
THERE ARE TWO BASIC DIVINE TITLES FOR GOD IN THE OLD TESTAMENT
There are two basic divine titles for God in the Old Testament. Elohim (Gen. 1:1) is used in relation to God's creation, and its plurality implies the Divine Trinity, thus denoting the unique yet triune God. Jehovah (Gen. 2:4) is used in God's relationship with man, and it literally means "He that is who He is; therefore, the eternal I Am," thus denoting the Triune God as the One who is not only eternally existing but also eternally being. These two titles of God in the Old Testament reveal to us the Divine Trinity.
GOD IS TRIUNE, THREE-ONE
God is triune, three-one. God is only one (Psa. 86:10; Isa. 45:5; 1 Cor. 8:4). The verses cited here show us beyond a shadow of a doubt that there are not three Gods but only one God. However, God has the aspect of three—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit (Matt. 28:19). This is perhaps the greatest mystery. Martin Luther once said that whoever understands the Triune God must be God Himself. How can one God be three, and how can the three be one? We can only prostrate ourselves, worship Him, extol Him, and say, "God, we praise You that You are three-one; You are triune. We cannot understand You, but we can worship You, and even the more, we can experience You."
THE THREE OF THE DIVINE TRINITY ARE ETERNALLY COEXISTENT
The three of the Divine Trinity are eternally coexistent. This means They coexist simultaneously and eternally. The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are all God. This does not mean that They are three Gods; it means that each of the three is God: The Father is God (1 Pet. 1:2; Eph. 1:17), the Son is God (Heb. 1:8; John 1:1; Rom. 9:5), and the Spirit is God (Acts 5:3-4). In addition, the Father, the Son, and the Spirit are all eternal: The Father is eternal (Isa. 9:6), the Son is eternal (Heb. 1:12; 7:3), and the Spirit is eternal (9:14). The Father is called the Eternal
Father, the Son has neither beginning of days nor end of life, and the Spirit is called the eternal Spirit. Moreover, the Father, the Son, and the Spirit coexist simultaneously from eternity to eternity (John 14:16-17; Eph. 3:14-17; 2 Cor. 13:14).
THE THREE OF THE DIVINE TRINITY ARE ETERNALLY COINHERENT
The three of the Divine Trinity are eternally coinherent. Not only do They coexist, but They coinhere, meaning that They dwell in each other. The Father, the Son, and the Spirit mutually indwell one another (John 14:10-11, 26; 15:26). The Father, the Son, and the Spirit coexist in Their coinherence and are thus distinct but not separate (John 5:19, 43; 8:29; 16:32; Luke 1:35; Matt. 1:18, 20; Luke 4:1, 18a; Matt 12:28). This is a very important concept to grasp related to the Divine Trinity. Not only are They not separate; They actually coinhere, so that the Father exists in the Son and the Spirit, the Son exists in the Father and the Spirit, and the Spirit exists in the Father and the Son. We cannot, understand this. We can only accept it as it is revealed to us in the pure revelation of the holy Scriptures.
THE ESSENTIAL TRINITY REFERS TO THE ESSENCE OF THE TRIUNE GOD FOR HIS EXISTENCE
The essential Trinity refers to the essence of the Triune God for His existence. In essence the Father, the Son, and the Spirit are one. The Son is the embodiment of the Father (Col. 2:9), and the Spirit is the reality of the Son (John 14:16-18).This shows that They are not three in essence, but one. The Father, the Son, and the Spirit are essentially one, as evidenced by the following: (1) A son is given to us, yet His name is called the eternal Father (Isa. 9:6); (2) the Son as the last Adam became the life-giving Spirit (1 Cor. 15:45b); and (3) the Lord is the Spirit (2 Cor. 3:17) and the Lord Spirit (v. 18). This again shows us that the three are essentially one. This is the revelation of the essential Trinity.
THE ECONOMICAL TRINITY REFERS TO THE PLAN OF THE TRIUNE GOD FOR HIS MOVE
The economical Trinity refers to the plan of the Triune God for His move. The essential aspect of the Trinity refers to His essence for His existence, whereas the economical aspect of the Trinity refers to the plan of the Triune God. When we speak of God's plan, we speak of His economy for His move.
The Father Makes the Divine Economy, the Son Accomplishes the Divine Economy, and the Spirit Applies What the Son Has Accomplished
The Father as the Originator makes the divine economy (Eph. 1:9-10; 3:9; 1 Tim. 1:4b); the Son accomplishes the divine economy made by the Father (John 5:19; 8:28); and the Spirit applies to God's elect what the Son has accomplished (16:13). Hymns, #7 says, "Praise the Father who has purposed! / Praise the Son who all has done! / Praise the Spirit who transmitteth! / Praise the Three who work as one!"
