He Released His Divine Life from the Shell of His Humanity
In His death, He also released His divine life from the shell of His humanity (John 12:24). The divine, uncreated, eternal life of God was contained in the humanity of Jesus. In His death, His humanity was broken, and the divine life was released. He was a grain of wheat who fell into the ground and released the life within Him through His death. Therefore, the all-inclusive death of Christ was an all-terminating, all-redeeming, new man-creating, and life-releasing death. We all need to learn this terminology.
He Laid a Foundation for His Organic Salvation and Set Up the Procedure to Attain His Ministry in the Stage of His Inclusion
In His death, He laid a foundation for His organic salvation and set up the procedure to attain His ministry in the stage of His inclusion. His judicial redemption which He accomplished was a foundation for His organic salvation. What He accomplished in the stage of incarnation was not God's salvation; it was judicial redemption, but it became a foundation for the organic salvation which He carries out in the next stage of His full ministry. We need to know what the Lord accomplished in the first stage of His ministry, and we need to be able to nourish others by ministering such a Christ in this stage.
THE SECOND STAGE OF THE FULL MINISTRY OF CHRIST IS THE STAGE OF HIS INCLUSION, THE STAGE OF CHRIST AS THE LIFE-GIVING SPIRIT, FROM HIS RESURRECTION TO THE DEGRADATION OF THE CHURCH
The second stage of the full ministry of Christ is the stage of His inclusion, the stage of Christ as the life-giving Spirit, from His resurrection to the degradation of the church. In this stage Christ is no longer in the flesh. Christ in the second stage, the stage of His inclusion, is the Christ who has become the all-inclusive, compound, life-giving Spirit. We use the word inclusion because in Christ's resurrection the Spirit of God was compounded to become the all-inclusive Spirit, including a number of rich ingredients, such as God's divinity, Christ's humanity, the all-inclusive death of Christ with its effectiveness, and the resurrection of Christ with its power. Christ in the stage of His inclusion is the all-inclusive Spirit. This stage of His inclusion is from His resurrection to the degradation of the church, a relatively short period of perhaps thir ty to sixty years.
In His Resurrection, Christ Was Begotten as God's Firstborn Son
In the stage of His inclusion, Christ accomplished three marvelous things. First, in His resurrection, Christ as a man in the flesh was begotten as God's firstborn Son. In Acts 13:33 Paul told the Jews, "God has fully fulfilled this promise to us their children in raising up Jesus, as it is also written in the second Psalm, 'You are My Son; this day have I begotten You.'" This is a marvelous verse in the New Testament. Through the ministry we realize that the Lord's resurrection was a birth to Him. He was a man in the flesh, and He was born in His resurrection to be the firstborn Son of God.
From Eternity Past without Beginning, Christ Was God's Only Begotten Son, Possessing Only Divinity, without Humanity, and Not Having Passed through Death into Resurrection
From eternity past without beginning, Christ was God's only begotten Son, possessing only divinity, without humanity, and not having passed through death into resurrection. In eternity Christ was resurrection, but He had not yet had the personal experience of passing through death into resurrection. Death was the gateway through which Christ entered into resurrection.
In Incarnation the Only Begotten Son of God Became Flesh to Be a God-man, a Man Possessing Both the Divine Nature and the Human Nature
In incarnation the only begotten Son of God became flesh to be a God-man, a man possessing both the divine nature and the human nature. Christ in His incarnation put on humanity, but this humanity had nothing to do with divinity; it was not yet divine but only human.
Through Death and Resurrection Christ in the Flesh as the Seed of David Was Designated to Be the Firstborn Son of God
Through death and resurrection Christ in the flesh as the seed of David was designated to be the firstborn Son of God (Rom. 1:3-4). In death His humanity was crucified. Divinity cannot be crucified, but humanity can. In resurrection His crucified humanity was made alive in the Spirit of His divinity (1 Pet. 3:18) and was uplifted into the sonship of the only begotten Son of God. Thus, He was begotten by God in His resurrection to be the firstborn Son of God. At the time Christ's humanity was experiencing death, the Spirit, which is His divinity, was being enlivened. This is a marvelous view of the death and resurrection of Christ. The Lord compared this to a grain of wheat falling into the ground. A grain of wheat has an outer shell and an inner life element. If the grain of wheat is simply on a table, the life is within the grain but the life is not released. It is not energized and activated. However, when the grain falls into the ground, its outer shell is broken and dies, and at the same time the life that is within it is energized and released. Christ was enlivened in the Spirit of His divinity. According to Romans 1:4, Christ's divinity is the Spirit of holiness. This Spirit, who is Christ's divinity, dispensed the divine, resurrection life into the crucified humanity of the man Jesus. By this dispensing His humanity was transformed, transfigured, and uplifted into the sonship of the only begotten Son of God. Christ was sonized in His humanity through His death and His resurrection.
This marvelous revelation of Christ's death and resurrection relates very much to our experience and enjoyment of Christ. We need to live a crucified life. We should not live by our natural human life but should put our natural life to death day by day and moment by moment so that Christ can live in us and we can live by the divine life in resurrection. The revelation of Christ's death and resurrection is a great encouragement to us because while we are experiencing the cross of Christ, a part of our natural humanity is being put to death. At the same time, we are passing through death into resurrection, and the Spirit as the divinity within us is activated and energized to impart the divine life, the resurrection life, into our crucified humanity. In this process our humanity is transformed, transfigured and uplifted into divinity. This is the process of deification by which nan becomes God in life, in nature, and in expression but not in the Godhead. We need to enjoy Christ in His death and resurrection in this way. Death is not the end; death is the gateway into resurrection. If we experience Christ in His death and resurrection, we have the same experience that He had. Day by day our old humanity is crucified, and the Spirit of divinity within us imparts the resurrection life to this crucified humanity to uplift, transform, and deify it. This is the process that we are all in today, the same process that the Lord Jesus went through as a man.
In His resurrection Christ was begotten by God to be the firstborn Son of God. This firstborn Son now has both divinity and humanity. As the only begotten Son He had only divinity, but as the firstborn Son He has divinity and humanity. That He is the firstborn Son does not mean that He is no longer the only begotten Son. He is still the only begotten Son of God in His divinity because He is the second in the Divine Trinity. John 3:16 tells us that we have to believe in the only begotten Son. However, as One who has both divinity and humanity, He has become the firstborn Son of God for the accomplishing of God's economy. He became the firstborn Son of God so that He can produce many sons, many brothers, to be the members of the Body of Christ to build up His Body to consummate the New Jerusalem.
In His Resurrection, Christ as the Last Adam Became the Life-giving Spirit
In His resurrection, Christ as the last Adam became the life-giving Spirit (1 Cor. 15:45b). This is a precious truth in the Lord's recovery. Brother Lee fought the battle for this truth throughout his entire ministry in the United States. We have to hold to this truth and declare and proclaim it everywhere. We can receive, eat, drink, and enjoy Christ because He is the life-giving Spirit. If He were not the life-giving Spirit we could have very little to do with Him, but now we are one with Him because He is the Spirit.
Christ, the Son of God as the Second of the Divine Trinity, Became the Life-giving Spirit in His Resurrection for the Release and Dispensing of the Divine Life
Christ, the Son of God as the second of the Divine Trinity, after completing His ministry on the earth, became (was transfigured into) the life-giving Spirit in His resurrection. Christ's becoming the life-giving Spirit was for the release of the divine life that was confined in the shell of His humanity and for the dispensing of this life into His believers, making them the many members which constitute His Body (John 12:24). The life-giving Spirit is for the carrying out of God's organic salvation by dispensing the divine life into all the chosen ones of God, who are the believers of Christ. We who have received the life-giving Spirit have become the sons of God, the brothers of Christ, and the members of the Body of Christ. This is for the accomplishing of God's economy.
This Life-giving Spirit Who Is the Pneumatic Christ Is Also Called the Spirit of Life, the Spirit of Jesus, the Spirit of Christ, the Spirit of Jesus Christ, and the Lord Spirit
This life-giving Spirit who is the pneumatic Christ is also called the Spirit of life (Rom. 8:2), the Spirit of Jesus (Acts 16:7), the Spirit of Christ (Rom 8:9), the Spirit of Jesus Christ (Phil. 1:19), and the Lord Spirit (2 Cor. 3:18). The term the Spirit of life means that the Spirit is life. The Spirit of Jesus implies that the humanity of Jesus, His human living, and His death as a man are compounded in this all-inclusive life-giving Spirit. The Spirit of Christ indicates that Christ's divinity and His resurrection are also in this wonderful all-inclusive, life-giving Spirit. The Spirit of Jesus Christ is the all-inclusive Spirit, who is the bountiful supply to us so that we can live Christ and magnify Christ. We all need the bountiful supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ in all our circumstances, whether they are positive or negative, so that we can live Christ and magnify Christ. As the Lord, He is the One who is in ascension on the throne, and as the Spirit, He is the One who indwells us to transform us. The Lord Spirit is the transforming Spirit, who transforms us into the image of the resurrected and glorified Christ. This is the wonderful, all-inclusive, life-giving Spirit, whom Christ became in His resurrection.—B. D.
The three stages of Christ's full ministry are a major, critical revelation in God's economy. This teaching is not merely another way to present the same thing. It is a further seeing and definition of Christ in His ministry, of how God is carrying out His economy, and how we should know and experience Christ. It would be helpful to memorize the outline of this message and learn to repeat it. This new seeing and new speaking require our study, learning, practice, and participation. When we study this, we begin to enter into the thought, the understanding, and the realization of Christ's full ministry in three stages.
These three stages correspond to the three "becomings" of Christ. His first becoming, which is related to the first stage, the stage of incarnation, is in John 1:14, which says, "The Word became flesh." God as the Word became flesh, initiating the first stage of His ministry, a ministry in the flesh. The second stage began with the becoming in
1 Corinthians 15:45b: "The last Adam became a life-giving Spirit." To describe this stage, the Lord gave Brother Lee a new word: inclusion. Using this word, he began to fellowship with us a new understanding of the Triune God, His economy, and the ministry of Christ in three stages. Today we are in the freshness of this revelation. Christ's third becoming is in the third stage of His ministry, in which He became the sevenfold intensified life-giving Spirit.
The second stage of Christ's ministry is called inclusion because in this stage many elements were included into Christ. Inclusion is typified by the compound ointment in Exodus 30:22-25. This type indicates that the Triune God has an economy to blend Himself with man. Christ's living, His death, and His resurrection were a compounding of the ointment. According to the picture of the compound ointment, the Spirit contains equal parts of death and resurrection. Because man is fallen, dead, sinful, and separated from God, he needs both death and resurrection. We need death to terminate all the negative things, the things of the old creation, and we need the resurrection life of God to bring us into His divine life. In His full ministry, Christ came to compound death and resurrection into the Spirit. Moreover, the compound Spirit is for the proper human living. Before Christ, there was no proper human life on the whole earth. The only way God could have such a living was to come and live it Himself in Christ, and this human life was compounded into the Spirit. Now this Spirit includes divinity, humanity, human living, death, and resurrection. Everything we need is in the compound Spirit; He is the all-inclusive antidote for fallen humanity. When Christ was crucified and resurrected, He became the Spirit as the compound ointment, and in His pneumatic form He can enter into every one of us. No one but God could have thought of such an economy.
In His Resurrection, Christ Regenerated the Believers for His Body
The Pneumatic Christ Became the Firstborn Son of God and the Life-giving Spirit for the Regenerating of the Believers
In His resurrection, Christ regenerated the believers for His Body (1 Pet. 1:3). The pneumatic Christ became the firstborn Son of God and the life-giving Spirit for the regenerating of the believers, making them the many sons of God born of God with Him in the one universal great delivery. This universal, great delivery of the Firstborn and the many brothers is for the composition of the house of God, even the household of God, and for the constitution of the Body of Christ to be His fullness, His expression and expansion, to consummate the eternal expression and expansion of the processed and consummated Triune God.
The Christ in Resurrection Gives Himself as the All-inclusive Life-giving Spirit without Measure through His Speaking of the Words of God
The Christ in resurrection gives Himself as the all-inclusive life-giving Spirit without measure through His speaking of the words of God (John 3:34). God gives the Spirit not stingily, not sparingly, but without measure. Moreover, the Spirit comes through His words. When we receive His words, we receive His Spirit.
All the Believers in Christ Are Built Up into a Dwelling Place of God in Their Spirit through Dispositional Sanctification, Renewing, Transformation, and Conformation
All the believers in Christ are built up into a dwelling place of God in their spirit indwelt by Him as the Spirit (Eph. 2:22) through dispositional sanctification (Rom. 15:16), renewing (Titus 3:5), transformation (2 Cor. 3:18), and conformation (Rom. 8:29). This briefly summarizes the work of the Spirit in us, the believers, to build us up into a dwelling place of God. Regeneration, dispositional sanctification, renewing, transformation, and conformation are God's organic salvation. The compound ointment with all its elements is sufficient to sanctify our disposition, renew our mind, transform our soul, and conform us to the image of Christ. The way God's organic salvation operates is through death and resurrection. As we experience Christ's death and resurrection, we begin to change how we think, and we begin to be transformed. This does not happen overnight; it is the process of divinity mingling with humanity, which takes place in the stage of inclusion.
THE THIRD STAGE OF THE FULL MINISTRY OF CHRIST IS THE STAGE OF HIS INTENSIFICATION, THE STAGE OF CHRIST AS THE SEVENFOLD INTENSIFIED SPIRIT, FROM THE DEGRADATION OF THE CHURCH TO THE CONSUMMATION OF THE NEW JERUSALEM
The third stage of the full ministry of Christ is the stage of His intensification, the stage of Christ as the sevenfold intensified Spirit, from the degradation of the church to the consummation of the New Jerusalem. In this stage Christ became the sevenfold intensified Spirit. The third stage is the intensification of the stage of inclusion. It is not different from the second stage in nature. It is the same as the stage of inclusion in its basic matters, but it is intensified. The level, intensity, application, and administration of whatever the Spirit was doing in inclusion is now seven times as much. The one Spirit is adequate to renew us, transform us, and conform us, but the Spirit had to become seven times as strong because of the degradation of the church. God in His foreknowledge saw that the church would become degraded, so He provided the sevenfold intensified Spirit to offset, challenge, and swallow up all the degradation that was to come in. Today we are under a mountain of Christian degradation. The story of Western civilization is the story of degraded and deformed Christianity, and we are all still very much under its wrong influence. Therefore, Christ had to be intensified.
In the same way, God needs to intensify us sevenfold. For us to come into the stage of inclusion is a kind of miracle in itself. To know Christ as the life-giving Spirit is far greater than Luther's revelation of justification by faith, and we are blessed just to know this much. However, our loving God, through our faithful ministering brother, showed us that we have to go further. We have to go into the stage of intensification, which is not a new stage except for its intensity. We must come out of the stage of inclusion; our living, speaking, and ministry must be in the stage of intensification. Being intensified delivers us from the degradation of the church. Brother Lee told us that his work in China was in the stage of incarnation, mostly bringing people to Christ. When he went to Taiwan, the Lord brought him further, into the stage of inclusion, to produce many churches. After this, he desired to minister in the stage of intensification.
The First Thing Which Christ Is Doing in the Third Stage of His Ministry Is to Intensify His Organic Salvation
The first thing which Christ is doing in the third stage of His ministry is to intensify His organic salvation. We still experience dispositional sanctification, but it is now seven times stronger. The death of Christ and His resurrection are still here. Everything is the same, except that it is stronger and more intense. In many things we are right, but we may not be intensified. Our sharing, for example, may be long and complicated without much impact. Therefore, our salvation needs to be intensified. Our need today is for all the steps of the organic salvation to be intensified.
On the way of Christ's ministry in the stage of His inclusion, which is to carry out His organic salvation for the producing of the church and the building up of His Body to consummate the New Jerusalem, the church became degraded, frustrating the accomplishment of God's eternal economy. Hence, Christ became the sevenfold intensified Spirit (Rev. 1:4; 4:5; 5:6; 3:1) to intensify His organic salvation sevenfold for the building up of His Body to consummate God's eternal goal—the New Jerusalem.
The Second Thing Which Christ Is Doing in the Third Stage of His Ministry Is to Produce the Overcomers
The second thing which Christ is doing in the third stage of His ministry is to produce the overcomers. The third stage of Christ's ministry is not only to call the overcomers but to produce them. In How to Be a Co-worker and an Elder and How to Fulfill Their Obligations on pages 46 and 48 Brother Lee says,
By ourselves we cannot become overcomers. Overcomers are produced, not worked out. They are produced by Christ in the third stage of His intensification…Recently, I have often repented and prayed, "Lord, I am in fear and trembling about one thing, that is, that from the past until the present, I am still not an overcomer. Lord, I pray that You would give me a few more years and measure to me another length of time in which I can exercise to become one of Your overcomers."
To become the overcomers we need Christ to produce us in the stage of intensification. Overcoming is something produced by Christ, but it is also something of our exercise. Brother Lee prayed that he could have a period of time to "exercise to become" one of the Lord's overcomers. We believe that the Lord heard that prayer and answered it. The length of time was not as long as our brother wanted, but we believe that it was the Lord's time and the Lord's way to make him an overcomer.
To be an overcomer is a matter of our desire and of our prayer. We should pray, "Lord, do whatever You need to do. I am desperate, Lord. Make me one of Your overcomers." We should not think that there is no hope for us. None of us definitely can know that we are overcomers. Only when the Lord returns will He say who are the overcoming ones and who are not. Our prayer, attitude, and desire have to be always that the Lord would make us overcomers. Our desire is an important factor. It is also important that we see that overcomers are produced. We will not wake up one morning and be an overcomer. We become an overcomer by getting into the "production line" of overcomers. God is producing overcomers, and the "market" is good for overcomers; God needs many of them. We may never reach the measure and the level of maturity and saturation that Brother Lee attained to, but there will not be only one holy person in the New Jerusalem. If this were true, the Lord would have come already. God in His economy needs many overcomers, who are produced through the intensification of the ministry of Christ. This is what He is doing today.
We must not say that now that our brother is no longer here we can never be produced as overcomers. He left us the "plan," the way to be produced as overcomers. To be an overcomer we need to eat, drink, and enjoy the Lord, but seven times more. In this respect, the stage of intensification is the same as the stage of inclusion, except that it is stronger and more intense. We need sevenfold intensity. When we rise up in the morning, we need to pray, and throughout the day we need to be produced by the sevenfold eating and drinking of Christ. We also need to be in the church life, since the church life is the "production line" for the overcomers. The church is not the goal; it is the procedure, the process, God uses to produce the goal. The church life and all the dear things related to the church are the procedure to produce us as overcomers. If we want to be overcomers, we must get into the procedure. If we do not have a vital group, how can we be overcomers? We need to be involved in the building up of the Body of Christ. In the last years of his life, our dear brother laid out the whole plan for our going on. If we want to be overcomers, we must follow the pattern. We must get into a vital group, pray for people, care for them, shepherd others, and prophesy in the meetings. Then we will be produced. This will not happen in one day, one week, or even in one year, but we will be produced as overcomers by the production in the church life. The way is very clear. We have the intensified Spirit, the God-ordained way, the church life, and all the elements we need. All we must do is carry it out. There is nothing left between us and the New Jerusalem. The whole way is clear. We simply need to go on by the sevenfold Spirit to be intensified.
Through the degradation of the church nearly all the believers in Christ became defeated in their old man by Satan, sin, the world, and their flesh. In His seven epistles to the degraded churches, Christ calls the defeated believers to be His overcomers by Himself as the sevenfold intensified Spirit for their experience of His organic salvation in His sevenfold intensification. Today we are in the age of intensification. Our work must be a work in the third stage of Christ's full ministry to intensify His organic salvation, produce overcomers, build up the Body of Christ, and consummate the New Jerusalem. This is the overcomers' work.
The Third Thing Which Christ Is Doing in the Third Stage of His Ministry Is to Consummate the New Jerusalem
The third thing which Christ is doing in the third stage of His ministry is to consummate the New Jerusalem. According to the entire revelation of the New Testament, the unique goal of the Christian work should be the New Jerusalem, which is the ultimate goal of God's eternal economy. The degradation of the church is mainly due to the fact that nearly all the Christian workers are distracted to take many things other than the New Jerusalem as their goal. Hence, to be overcomers answering the Lord's call under the degradation of the church, we need to overcome all the things which replace the New Jerusalem as the goal and take the goal of God's eternal economy, that is, the New Jerusalem, as our unique and ultimate goal. As we are here day by day, enjoying the Lord, praying, and taking care of people, we are being constituted. We may not notice it, but we are gaining spiritual weight, and the Body is being built up day by day. It is hardly noticeable today, but one day we will arrive at the point where the Body is built up, the bride is ready, and the Lord comes back. In that day we may look at each other and say, "Where is the New Jerusalem?" Then we will see that we have become the New Jerusalem and that the Lord has come to marry us. This is the result of the stage of intensification. The consummation will be the New Jerusalem, and one day it will be here.
God calls the defeated believers to be the overcomers. Once, after a brother had been defeated in a certain matter, Brother Lee shepherded him by saying, "It is never too late." Today we may have a new beginning with a new consecration: "Lord, make me, produce me, as one of Your overcomers. Make me a builder of Your Body so that one day we will consummate the New Jerusalem." If the Lord could be satisfied with one holy person, He would have come already, but the way to complete Christ's ministry is for many to become overcomers. Then one day we will meet together and have a glorious reunion in the New Jerusalem in the kingdom stage, which is a reward for all the overcoming believers. May the Lord touch us to be faithful to this revelation. We need to learn the new vocabulary, eat the heavenly food, and live in the church life.—D. T.

TOP-纲目|Outline|对照-目录
　
　
第七篇　包罗万有的灵─赐生命、复合、七倍加强的灵
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　神是灵，启示神的神圣本质乃是灵─约四24：
一　包罗万有之灵的源头是神，而神就是灵。
二　约翰四章二十四节里的“灵”字，不是指神的身位，乃是指神的性质。
贰　包罗万有的灵是三一神的第三者─太二八19，林后十三14：
一　那灵是三一神的终极完成与总和。
二　父是源头，化身于子；子是父的具体化身，实化为灵。
三　在神圣三一的三者中间，就着那灵对我们是三一神的实化、应用、和临及这一面的意义说，那灵是最重要的。
叁　包罗万有的灵是具有神性元素的神的灵─创一2，太十二28，罗八9，林前二11～12：
一　在“神的灵”这个辞里，“神”与“灵”是同位语；因此，“神的灵”意思就是：神是灵，灵是神。
二　在创世记一章里，神的灵在水面上孵育运行，好在神的旧造中产生生命。
三　我们在哥林多前书看见，神那运行在我们里面，也就是住在我们里面的运行之灵，也是启示的灵，将神一切的事启示给我们。
肆　包罗万有的灵是耶和华的灵，主的灵，就是神在与人的关系中，带着神圣三一的元素临及人─出三6，14～15，士三10，赛六一1，路四18，林后三17：
一　创世记二章有另一个称谓，耶和华，因为在这一章，神开始与祂所创造的人接触。
二　耶和华的灵是神的临及人，也是祂这伟大的我是对人的照顾。
伍　包罗万有的灵是圣灵，具有圣别、神圣的性情，耶稣乃是由这灵生在马利亚里面─路一35，太一18，20：
一　因为主耶稣是从圣灵成孕的，所以祂出生为一个性情是圣的人，像神自己是圣的一样。
二　主耶稣的成孕，是关系到神使祂自己成为人的开始，也是神使人成为神的开始，好叫祂能成为人，并且叫人能在生命和性情上成为祂，但无分于祂的神格，使神人二者成为一个实体。
陆　包罗万有的灵是赐生命的灵，带着神圣生命的分赐─林前十五45下，林后三6：
一　赐生命的灵有能力赐生命给我们。
二　赐生命的灵现今在信徒里面作工，赐生命给他们的全人。
柒　包罗万有的灵是生命的灵，具有神圣生命的丰富─罗八2：
一　生命的灵是在复活里那是灵的基督，作信徒的神圣生命之灵。
二　生命的灵是生命的实际，因为生命的灵包含神圣生命的元素。
捌　包罗万有的灵是实际的灵，就是神所是、所有、所作的灵─约十四17，十五26，十六13：
一　借着实际的灵，凡三一神所是的，都是我们的；凡祂所有的，都是我们的；凡祂所作成的，也都是我们的。
二　实际的灵是我们与三一神之间的连系，使我们在经历上与三一神成为一。
玖　包罗万有的灵是耶稣的灵，这灵是耶稣在祂受苦之人性中的实际─徒十六7：
一　因为保罗在行传十六章受苦，耶稣的灵与他同在，不仅有神的神圣元素，也有人性、为人生活、钉十字架和受死等等元素。
二　保罗传讲的职事，乃是为基督身体缘故受苦的职事，因此需要这样一位包罗万有的灵─西一24。
拾　包罗万有的灵是基督的灵，具有复活的元素─罗八9：
一　基督的灵是在神性里的基督，祂征服了死，并成了在复活里的生命，有复活的能力。
二　具有复活元素的基督的灵，是征服死并分赐生命的灵。
拾壹　包罗万有的灵是耶稣基督的灵，具有神性、人性、为人生活、钉十字架、并复活这一切元素的全备供应─腓一19：
一　耶稣基督的灵是那曾在地上过受苦生活之耶稣，与现今在复活里之基督的灵。
二　保罗在他的受苦中，经历了主在人性里的受苦，以及主的复活。
拾贰　包罗万有的灵是复合的灵，由复合的膏油所表征─出三十22～31：
一　复合的膏油是由一欣橄榄油与四种成分─没药、肉桂、菖蒲、桂皮─调和并复合所组成，这些成分各有其单位和数字。
二　复合的膏油预表人与神复合在一起，具有基督那甜美有功效的死、基督复活的香味和能力、三一神、以及负责任的能力。
三　复合的膏油是为着涂抹与敬拜神有关的每一样东西和每一个人，将他们从一切凡俗的事物分别出来，使他们成为至圣，为着神的事奉。
拾叁　包罗万有的灵是主灵，具有升天和元首身分这两种元素─林后三17～18：
一　主灵乃是：那是灵的主，以及那是主的灵。
二　“主灵”是一个复合的名称，指那是灵的基督。
三　主灵乃是为着我们的变化。
拾肆　包罗万有的灵是七灵，具有七倍的加强─启一4，四5，五6：
一　七灵实际上乃是神的一灵，为着神施行祂行政的行动而成了七倍，以执行神在宇宙中的经纶。
二　这样一位加强的灵是为使我们有活力，在召会堕落时成为得胜者。
三　七灵，就是在宝座前点着的七盏火灯，正在焚烧、审判、光照、搜寻、暴露、并炼净我们，为着产生并建造作为金灯台的众召会。
四　七灵，就是基督的眼，正在鉴察我们，并将祂一切的丰富注入我们里面。
拾伍　包罗万有的灵是那灵，就是终极完成的灵，作经过过程之三一神的终极完成─约七39，启二二17：
一　那灵是经过过程之三一神的终极完成，新妇是蒙救赎、重生、变化的三部分人，二者成为婚配。
二　作终极完成之神的那灵，与变化过的三部分人，要成为婚配，作一个属天、宇宙的对偶，直到永远。
参读　基督徒的生活，第三篇；新约总论，第四册，第七十九至八十篇；三一神终极完成之灵与信徒重生之灵联结的果效，第一篇；出埃及记生命读经，第一百六十至一百六十二篇信息；那灵，第一至二篇；那灵同我们的灵，第一至五章。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message Seven
The All-inclusive Spirit— the Life-giving, Compound, Sevenfold Intensified Spirit
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　God being Spirit reveals that God's divine substance is Spirit—John 4:24:
A.　The source of the all-inclusive Spirit is God, who is Spirit.
B.　The word?Spirit?in John 4:24 does not refer to God's person but to God's nature.
II.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the third of the Triune God—Matt. 28:19; 2 Cor. 13:14:
A.　The Spirit is the consummation and the totality of the Triune God.
B.　The Father as the source is embodied in the Son, and the Son as the embodiment of the Father is realized as the Spirit.
C.　Among the three of the Trinity, the Spirit is the most important in the sense of His being the realization, application, and reaching of the Triune God to us.
III.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of God with the element of divinity—Gen. 1:1-2; Matt. 12:28; Rom. 8:9; 1 Cor. 2:11-12:
A.　In the phrase?the Spirit of God, God?is in apposition to?Spirit;?thus, the?Spirit of God?means that God is the Spirit and the Spirit is God.
B.　In Genesis 1 the Spirit of God moved to brood over the face of the waters for the producing of life in God's old creation.
C.　In 1 Corinthians we see that the moving Spirit of God who moves in us, that is, dwells in us, is also the revealing Spirit who reveals to us all the things of God.
IV.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jehovah, the Spirit of the Lord, as the reaching of God in His relationship with man with the elements of the Divine Trinity—Exo. 3:6, 14-15; Judg. 3:10; Isa. 61:1; Luke 4:18; 2 Cor. 3:17:
A.　In Genesis 2 there is another title,?Jehovah,?because in this chapter God begins to have contact with the man created by Him.
B.　The Spirit of Jehovah is God's reaching of man and His care for man as the great I AM.
V.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Holy Spirit, with the element of the holy, divine nature, of whom Jesus was begotten in Mary—Luke 1:35; Matt. 1:18, 20:
A.　Because the Lord Jesus was conceived of the Holy Spirit, He was brought forth as someone who was holy in nature just as God Himself is holy.
B.　The conception of the Lord Jesus is related to the beginning of God making Himself man and of God making man God that He might become man and man might become Him in life and nature but not in the Godhead, that the two could become one entity.
VI.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the life-giving Spirit with the impartation of the divine life—1 Cor. 15:45b; 2 Cor. 3:6:
A.　The life-giving Spirit has the ability to give us life.
B.　The life-giving Spirit is now working in the being of the believers to give life to their whole being.
VII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of life with the riches of the divine life—Rom. 8:2:
A.　The Spirit of life is the pneumatic Christ in resurrection as the Spirit of the divine life to the believers.
B.　The Spirit of life is the reality of life, for this Spirit contains the element of the divine life.
VIII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of reality, the Spirit of what God is, has, and does—John 14:17; 15:26; 16:13:
A.　Whatever the Triune God is, is ours; whatever He has, is ours; and whatever He has done, is ours by the Spirit of reality.
B.　The Spirit of reality is the linking between us and the Triune God, making us one with the Triune God in experience.
IX.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jesus, who is the reality of Jesus in His suffering humanity—Acts 16:7:
A.　Because Paul was suffering in Acts 16, the Spirit of Jesus was with him having not only the divine element of God but also the elements of humanity, human living, and crucifixion, the suffering of death.
B.　Such an all-inclusive Spirit was needed by Paul in his preaching ministry, a ministry with sufferings for the sake of the Body of Christ—Col. 1:24.
X.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Christ with the element of resurrection—Rom. 8:9:
A.　The Spirit of Christ is Christ in His divinity, who conquered death and became life in resurrection with the resurrection power.
B.　The Spirit of Christ with the element of resurrection is the death-conquering and the life-dispensing Spirit.
XI.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jesus Christ with the bountiful supply of all the elements of humanity, human living, crucifixion, and resurrection—Phil. 1:19:
A.　The Spirit of Jesus Christ is the Spirit of the Jesus who lived a life of suffering on the earth and of the Christ who is now in resurrection.
B.　In his suffering Paul experienced both the Lord's suffering in His humanity and the Lord's resurrection.
XII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the compound Spirit typified by the compound ointment—Exo. 30:22-31:
A.　The compound ointment is composed of a hin of olive oil blended and compounded with four elements—myrrh, cinnamon, calamus, and cassia—with their respective units and numbers.
B.　The compound ointment typifies man and God compounded together with the sweet and effective death of Christ and the flavor and power of Christ's resurrection, the Triune God, and the power for responsibility.
C.　The compound ointment is for anointing everything and every person related to God's worship to separate them from anything common, making them most holy for God's service.
XIII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Lord Spirit with the elements of ascension and lordship—2 Cor. 3:17-18:
A.　The Lord Spirit is the Lord who is the Spirit and the Spirit who is the Lord.
B.　The Lord Spirit?is a compound title referring to the pneumatic Christ.
C.　The Lord Spirit is for our transformation.
XIV.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the seven Spirits with the sevenfold intensification—Rev. 1:4; 4:5; 5:6:
A.　The seven Spirits actually are the one Spirit of God who is sevenfold for God's move to carry out God's administration, to execute God's economy in the universe.
B.　Such an intensified Spirit is for us to be vitalized, to be overcomers in the degradation of the church.
C.　The seven Spirits as the seven lamps of fire burning before the throne are burning, judging, enlightening, searching, exposing, and purifying us for producing and building up the churches as the golden lampstands.
D.　The seven Spirits as the eyes of Christ are observing us and transfusing us with all His riches.
XV.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit, the consummated Spirit as the consummation of the processed Triune God—John 7:39; Rev. 22:17:
A.　The Spirit as the consummation of the processed Triune God marries the bride as the consummation of the redeemed, regenerated, and transformed tripartite man.
B.　The Spirit as the consummated God and the transformed tripartite man will be married to be one heavenly, universal couple for eternity.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第七篇　包罗万有的灵─赐生命、复合、七倍加强的灵
The All-inclusive Spirit— the Life-giving, Compound, Sevenfold Intensified Spirit
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
壹　神是灵，启示神的神圣本质乃是灵─约四24：
I.　God being Spirit reveals that God's divine substance is Spirit—John 4:24:
一　包罗万有之灵的源头是神，而神就是灵。
A.　The source of the all-inclusive Spirit is God, who is Spirit.
二　约翰四章二十四节里的“灵”字，不是指神的身位，乃是指神的性质。
B.　The word?Spirit?in John 4:24 does not refer to God's person but to God's nature.
贰　包罗万有的灵是三一神的第三者─太二八19，林后十三14：
II.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the third of the Triune God—Matt. 28:19; 2 Cor. 13:14:
一　那灵是三一神的终极完成与总和。
A.　The Spirit is the consummation and the totality of the Triune God.
二　父是源头，化身于子；子是父的具体化身，实化为灵。
B.　The Father as the source is embodied in the Son, and the Son as the embodiment of the Father is realized as the Spirit.
三　在神圣三一的三者中间，就着那灵对我们是三一神的实化、应用、和临及这一面的意义说，那灵是最重要的。
C.　Among the three of the Trinity, the Spirit is the most important in the sense of His being the realization, application, and reaching of the Triune God to us.
叁　包罗万有的灵是具有神性元素的神的灵─创一2，太十二28，罗八9，林前二11～12：
III.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of God with the element of divinity—Gen. 1:1-2; Matt. 12:28; Rom. 8:9; 1 Cor. 2:11-12:
一　在“神的灵”这个辞里，“神”与“灵”是同位语；因此，“神的灵”意思就是：神是灵，灵是神。
A.　In the phrase?the Spirit of God, God?is in apposition to?Spirit;?thus, the?Spirit of God?means that God is the Spirit and the Spirit is God.
二　在创世记一章里，神的灵在水面上孵育运行，好在神的旧造中产生生命。
B.　In Genesis 1 the Spirit of God moved to brood over the face of the waters for the producing of life in God's old creation.
三　我们在哥林多前书看见，神那运行在我们里面，也就是住在我们里面的运行之灵，也是启示的灵，将神一切的事启示给我们。
C.　In 1 Corinthians we see that the moving Spirit of God who moves in us, that is, dwells in us, is also the revealing Spirit who reveals to us all the things of God.
肆　包罗万有的灵是耶和华的灵，主的灵，就是神在与人的关系中，带着神圣三一的元素临及人─出三6，14～15，士三10，赛六一1，路四18，林后三17：
IV.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jehovah, the Spirit of the Lord, as the reaching of God in His relationship with man with the elements of the Divine Trinity—Exo. 3:6, 14-15; Judg. 3:10; Isa. 61:1; Luke 4:18; 2 Cor. 3:17:
一　创世记二章有另一个称谓，耶和华，因为在这一章，神开始与祂所创造的人接触。
A.　In Genesis 2 there is another title,?Jehovah,?because in this chapter God begins to have contact with the man created by Him.
二　耶和华的灵是神的临及人，也是祂这伟大的我是对人的照顾。
B.　The Spirit of Jehovah is God's reaching of man and His care for man as the great I AM.
伍　包罗万有的灵是圣灵，具有圣别、神圣的性情，耶稣乃是由这灵生在马利亚里面─路一35，太一18，20：
V.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Holy Spirit, with the element of the holy, divine nature, of whom Jesus was begotten in Mary—Luke 1:35; Matt. 1:18, 20:
一　因为主耶稣是从圣灵成孕的，所以祂出生为一个性情是圣的人，像神自己是圣的一样。
A.　Because the Lord Jesus was conceived of the Holy Spirit, He was brought forth as someone who was holy in nature just as God Himself is holy.
二　主耶稣的成孕，是关系到神使祂自己成为人的开始，也是神使人成为神的开始，好叫祂能成为人，并且叫人能在生命和性情上成为祂，但无分于祂的神格，使神人二者成为一个实体。
B.　The conception of the Lord Jesus is related to the beginning of God making Himself man and of God making man God that He might become man and man might become Him in life and nature but not in the Godhead, that the two could become one entity.
陆　包罗万有的灵是赐生命的灵，带着神圣生命的分赐─林前十五45下，林后三6：
VI.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the life-giving Spirit with the impartation of the divine life—1 Cor. 15:45b; 2 Cor. 3:6:
一　赐生命的灵有能力赐生命给我们。
A.　The life-giving Spirit has the ability to give us life.
二　赐生命的灵现今在信徒里面作工，赐生命给他们的全人。
B.　The life-giving Spirit is now working in the being of the believers to give life to their whole being.
柒　包罗万有的灵是生命的灵，具有神圣生命的丰富─罗八2：
VII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of life with the riches of the divine life—Rom. 8:2:
一　生命的灵是在复活里那是灵的基督，作信徒的神圣生命之灵。
A.　The Spirit of life is the pneumatic Christ in resurrection as the Spirit of the divine life to the believers.
二　生命的灵是生命的实际，因为生命的灵包含神圣生命的元素。
B.　The Spirit of life is the reality of life, for this Spirit contains the element of the divine life.
捌　包罗万有的灵是实际的灵，就是神所是、所有、所作的灵─约十四17，十五26，十六13：
VIII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of reality, the Spirit of what God is, has, and does—John 14:17; 15:26; 16:13:
一　借着实际的灵，凡三一神所是的，都是我们的；凡祂所有的，都是我们的；凡祂所作成的，也都是我们的。
A.　Whatever the Triune God is, is ours; whatever He has, is ours; and whatever He has done, is ours by the Spirit of reality.
二　实际的灵是我们与三一神之间的连系，使我们在经历上与三一神成为一。
B.　The Spirit of reality is the linking between us and the Triune God, making us one with the Triune God in experience.
玖　包罗万有的灵是耶稣的灵，这灵是耶稣在祂受苦之人性中的实际─徒十六7：
IX.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jesus, who is the reality of Jesus in His suffering humanity—Acts 16:7:
一　因为保罗在行传十六章受苦，耶稣的灵与他同在，不仅有神的神圣元素，也有人性、为人生活、钉十字架和受死等等元素。
A.　Because Paul was suffering in Acts 16, the Spirit of Jesus was with him having not only the divine element of God but also the elements of humanity, human living, and crucifixion, the suffering of death.
二　保罗传讲的职事，乃是为基督身体缘故受苦的职事，因此需要这样一位包罗万有的灵─西一24。
B.　Such an all-inclusive Spirit was needed by Paul in his preaching ministry, a ministry with sufferings for the sake of the Body of Christ—Col. 1:24.
拾　包罗万有的灵是基督的灵，具有复活的元素─罗八9：
X.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Christ with the element of resurrection—Rom. 8:9:
一　基督的灵是在神性里的基督，祂征服了死，并成了在复活里的生命，有复活的能力。
A.　The Spirit of Christ is Christ in His divinity, who conquered death and became life in resurrection with the resurrection power.
二　具有复活元素的基督的灵，是征服死并分赐生命的灵。
B.　The Spirit of Christ with the element of resurrection is the death-conquering and the life-dispensing Spirit.
拾壹　包罗万有的灵是耶稣基督的灵，具有神性、人性、为人生活、钉十字架、并复活这一切元素的全备供应─腓一19：
XI.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jesus Christ with the bountiful supply of all the elements of humanity, human living, crucifixion, and resurrection—Phil. 1:19:
一　耶稣基督的灵是那曾在地上过受苦生活之耶稣，与现今在复活里之基督的灵。
A.　The Spirit of Jesus Christ is the Spirit of the Jesus who lived a life of suffering on the earth and of the Christ who is now in resurrection.
二　保罗在他的受苦中，经历了主在人性里的受苦，以及主的复活。
B.　In his suffering Paul experienced both the Lord's suffering in His humanity and the Lord's resurrection.
拾贰　包罗万有的灵是复合的灵，由复合的膏油所表征─出三十22～31：
XII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the compound Spirit typified by the compound ointment—Exo. 30:22-31:
一　复合的膏油是由一欣橄榄油与四种成分─没药、肉桂、菖蒲、桂皮─调和并复合所组成，这些成分各有其单位和数字。
A.　The compound ointment is composed of a hin of olive oil blended and compounded with four elements—myrrh, cinnamon, calamus, and cassia—with their respective units and numbers.
二　复合的膏油预表人与神复合在一起，具有基督那甜美有功效的死、基督复活的香味和能力、三一神、以及负责任的能力。
B.　The compound ointment typifies man and God compounded together with the sweet and effective death of Christ and the flavor and power of Christ's resurrection, the Triune God, and the power for responsibility.
三　复合的膏油是为着涂抹与敬拜神有关的每一样东西和每一个人，将他们从一切凡俗的事物分别出来，使他们成为至圣，为着神的事奉。
C.　The compound ointment is for anointing everything and every person related to God's worship to separate them from anything common, making them most holy for God's service.
拾叁　包罗万有的灵是主灵，具有升天和元首身分这两种元素─林后三17～18：
XIII.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Lord Spirit with the elements of ascension and lordship—2 Cor. 3:17-18:
一　主灵乃是：那是灵的主，以及那是主的灵。
A.　The Lord Spirit is the Lord who is the Spirit and the Spirit who is the Lord.
二　“主灵”是一个复合的名称，指那是灵的基督。
B.　The Lord Spirit?is a compound title referring to the pneumatic Christ.
三　主灵乃是为着我们的变化。
C.　The Lord Spirit is for our transformation.
拾肆　包罗万有的灵是七灵，具有七倍的加强─启一4，四5，五6：
XIV.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the seven Spirits with the sevenfold intensification—Rev. 1:4; 4:5; 5:6:
一　七灵实际上乃是神的一灵，为着神施行祂行政的行动而成了七倍，以执行神在宇宙中的经纶。
A.　The seven Spirits actually are the one Spirit of God who is sevenfold for God's move to carry out God's administration, to execute God's economy in the universe.
二　这样一位加强的灵是为使我们有活力，在召会堕落时成为得胜者。
B.　Such an intensified Spirit is for us to be vitalized, to be overcomers in the degradation of the church.
三　七灵，就是在宝座前点着的七盏火灯，正在焚烧、审判、光照、搜寻、暴露、并炼净我们，为着产生并建造作为金灯台的众召会。
C.　The seven Spirits as the seven lamps of fire burning before the throne are burning, judging, enlightening, searching, exposing, and purifying us for producing and building up the churches as the golden lampstands.
四　七灵，就是基督的眼，正在鉴察我们，并将祂一切的丰富注入我们里面
C.　The seven Spirits as the eyes of Christ are observing us and transfusing us with all His riches.
拾伍　包罗万有的灵是那灵，就是终极完成的灵，作经过过程之三一神的终极完成─约七39，启二二17：
XV.　The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit, the consummated Spirit as the consummation of the processed Triune God—John 7:39; Rev. 22:17:
一　那灵是经过过程之三一神的终极完成，新妇是蒙救赎、重生、变化的三部分人，二者成为婚配。
A.　The Spirit as the consummation of the processed Triune God marries the bride as the consummation of the redeemed, regenerated, and transformed tripartite man.
二　作终极完成之神的那灵，与变化过的三部分人，要成为婚配，作一个属天、宇宙的对偶，直到永远。
B.　The Spirit as the consummated God and the transformed tripartite man will be married to be one heavenly, universal couple for eternity.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE SEVEN
THE ALL-INCLUSIVE SPIRIT—THE LIFE-GIVING, COMPOUND, SEVENFOLD INTENSIFIED SPIRIT
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
The twelve messages of this series, The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Ministry, are in two categories. The first six messages contain the visions and revelations of God's New Testament ministry, while the following six are more experiential. The first category includes the apostles' teaching, the New Testament ministry, the economy of God, the Triune God, the all-inclusive Christ, and the full ministry of Christ in three stages. All these matters are high and heavenly. They are our basic stand. We must lay hold on them, fight for them, and live by them. They must be the reality of our daily life and labor. However, all these truths conclude with the Spirit; the Spirit is the reality of all these truths. The apostles' teaching came from the apostles being filled with the Spirit. The New Testament ministry, Paul says, is not of the letter but of the Spirit. Moreover, as our Brother Lee, God's servant, trained us year after year, God's economy is to dispense Himself into His chosen people, and this dispensing is the transmission of the Spirit. Likewise, the Triune God is Spirit, and the all-inclusive Christ and His ministry in three stages consummate with the sevenfold intensified Spirit. We must be impressed with the truth of the Spirit. When our brother first came to this country, it seems that he had no other burden. His one burden was concerning the Spirit. Wherever he went, he spoke on the all-inclusive life-giving Spirit. Once when he spoke on 1 Corinthians 15:45b—"The last Adam became a life-giving Spirit"—a brother opposed him, advising him not to speak so strongly in this way. Brother Lee replied, "If I do not speak this, I will have nothing to say." Some who knew him were shocked by this statement because, having been under his training for many years in Taiwan, they knew how much he had to say. However, the truth of the Spirit is the reality, the substance, of all that he spoke.
The Spirit is so crucial. The Spirit is our revelation, enjoyment, and experience. The Spirit is the substance and the reality of all the spiritual things. Without the Spirit we only have doctrines, teachings, and knowledge. All that we know, hear, enjoy, and appreciate is theoretical to us until it is realized in our spirit, which is mingled with and indwelt by the Spirit. When we touch the reality in our spirit and the Spirit operates in us, we enter into the reality of the apostles' teaching, we serve in the New Testament ministry, we live God's economy, we experience and enjoy the Triune God, we have the all-inclusive Christ as our portion, and we fully participate in His full ministry in three stages. All these matters become our reality. Without the Spirit we do not have the real spiritual things. Watchman Nee helped us to see that Christ is the sum of all spiritual things, and Brother Lee helped us to see that this Christ is the Spirit. Without the Spirit all the spiritual things are outward, doctrinal, theoretical, and merely knowledge to us. They may even be the content of our conversation, yet they are without reality. When the Spirit is with us, when we touch the Spirit, enjoy the Spirit, partake of the Spirit, and release, protect, defend, exercise, and feed our spirit, our spirit is nourished. It is strong and exercised, and it partakes of the revelation, understanding, and reality of the spiritual things. In this way, all the spiritual things which the Lord's servant has given to us in the past thirty years become the reality of the churches.
From the beginning, we should have the understanding within us that we need the Spirit. In our daily life we must have a life in the enjoyment of the Spirit. Without the Spirit we are void and empty. Without the Spirit we are meaningless. Without the Spirit we may have many outward Christian activities, but we do not have the reality. The reality comes from the Spirit. The Christian living simply should be a living in the Spirit, of the Spirit, and by the Spirit. A healthy Christian living can never be disassociated from the Spirit. The Lord Jesus Christ as the first, unique God-man was conceived by the Spirit and baptized in the Spirit. In the first message He gave, He said, "The Spirit of the Lord is upon Me" (Luke 4:18). From this we can see that when the Lord was on this earth, He never deviated from the Spirit. Because of this, He was always in such oneness with the Father.
GOD BEING SPIRIT REVEALING THAT GOD'S DIVINE SUBSTANCE IS SPIRIT
God being Spirit reveals that God's divine substance is Spirit (John 4:24). This and the following main point of this message define who the Spirit is: God is Spirit, and He is the third of the Triune God. The next thirteen points of this message show the progression of the Spirit: the Spirit of God, the Spirit of Jehovah, the Holy Spirit, the life-giving Spirit, the Spirit of life, the Spirit of reality, the Spirit of Jesus, the Spirit of Christ, the Spirit of Jesus Christ, the compound Spirit, the Lord Spirit, the seven Spirits, and the Spirit. We all, especially the young people among us, should memorize the points of this outline and enjoy them. This is the content of Brother Lee's ministry. Because we love this ministry so much, we should have a deep impression and pray, "Lord, I would never be apart from my spirit, which is indwelt by the Spirit. I would never let my spirit become weakened, empty, or inactive. I want to have my spirit strengthened by the Spirit all the time."
The source of the all-inclusive Spirit is God, who is Spirit. The word Spirit in John 4:24 does not refer to God's person but to God's nature. When we call, "O Lord," God comes into us, and we have the impression and sensation that we are touching the Spirit as the substance and nature of God, who is Spirit. When we call on God, we receive the Spirit because God is Spirit.
THE THIRD OF THE TRIUNE GOD
The all-inclusive Spirit is the third of the Triune God (Matt. 28:19; 2 Cor. 13:14). The Spirit is the consummation and the totality of the Triune God. The Father as the source is embodied in the Son, and the Son as the embodiment of the Father is realized as the Spirit. On the one hand, we may feel to say that Christ is the most important among the three of the Trinity. On the other hand, in experience we realize that among the three of the Trinity, the Spirit is the most important in the sense of His being the realization, application, and reaching of the Triune God to us.
THE SPIRIT OF GOD WITH THE ELEMENT OF DIVINITY
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of God with the element of divinity (Gen. 1:1-2; Matt. 12:28; Rom. 8:9; 1 Cor. 2:11-12). In Genesis 1:2, the word for God is Elohim. In the phrase the Spirit of God, God is in apposition to Spirit; thus, the Spirit of God means that God is the Spirit and the Spirit is God. The Spirit of God refers to God the Spirit. In Genesis 1 the Spirit of God moved to brood over the face of the waters for the producing of life in God's old creation. The old creation came about through the Spirit of God. In 1 Corinthians we see that the moving Spirit of God who moves in us, that is, dwells in us, is also the revealing Spirit who reveals to us all the things of God. When we touch the truth of the Spirit of God, we see two aspects: According to the Old Testament, the Spirit of God is the Spirit who produces, and according to the New Testament, the Spirit of God is the Spirit who reveals to us all the things of God. No matter how much we have been trained, the spiritual things still have to be revealed to us as we are in spirit, where the Spirit reveals the things of God.
THE SPIRIT OF JEHOVAH, THE SPIRIT OF THE LORD, WITH THE ELEMENTS OF THE DIVINE TRINITY
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jehovah, the Spirit of the Lord, as the reaching of God in His relationship with man with the elements of the Divine Trinity (Exo. 3:6, 14-15; Judg. 3:10; Isa. 61:1; Luke 4:18; 2 Cor. 3:17). In Genesis 2 there is another title, Jehovah, because in this chapter God begins to have contact with the man created by Him. The Spirit of God in the Old Testament was for producing, for creation, and the Spirit of Jehovah was for God to reach out to man. The Spirit of Jehovah is God's reaching of man and His care for man as the great I Am. His being the great I Am means that He is whatever we need, as the very supply and answer to all our needs.
THE HOLY SPIRIT WITH THE ELEMENT OF THE HOLY, DIVINE NATURE, OF WHOM JESUS WAS BEGOTTEN IN MARY
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Holy Spirit, with the element of the holy, divine nature, of whom Jesus was begotten in Mary (Luke 1:35; Matt. 1:18, 20). Because the Lord Jesus was conceived of the Holy Spirit, He was brought forth as someone who was holy in nature just as God Himself is holy. Likewise, when we touch the Spirit, the Spirit sanctifies us with the element of holiness. The conception of the Lord Jesus was the beginning of God making Himself man and of God making man God that He might become man and man might become Him in life and nature but not in the Godhead, that the two could become one entity. We become God in life and nature by partaking of, taking in, and enjoying the Holy Spirit.
THE LIFE-GIVING SPIRIT WITH THE IMPARTATION OF THE DIVINE LIFE
The all-inclusive Spirit is the life-giving Spirit with the impartation of the divine life (1 Cor. 15:45b; 2 Cor. 3:6). The Spirit is not only the Spirit of God, the Spirit of Jehovah, and the Holy Spirit. Now He is also the life-giving Spirit. The life-giving Spirit has the ability to give us life, and the life-giving Spirit is now working in the being of the believers to give life to their whole being. After we begin to grow in the Lord, we may often feel void, empty, defeated, hopeless, and meaningless. At such times, we must call, "O Lord!" When we call and pray-read, the Spirit gives us life.
THE SPIRIT OF LIFE WITH THE RICHES OF THE DIVINE LIFE
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of life with the riches of the divine life (Rom. 8:2). The Spirit of life is the pneumatic Christ in resurrection as the Spirit of the divine life to the believers. The pneumatic Christ is Christ as the Spirit. That He is the Spirit in resurrection means that He surpasses all death. As the life-giving Spirit He gives us life. Death is a powerful factor in us. Sometimes we feel we are under the bondage of death. How can we be helped, where is our hope, and how can we go on? It is by the Spirit of life. Paul cried out, "Wretched man that I am! Who will deliver me from the body of this death?" (Rom. 7:24). Then he said, "The law of the Spirit of life has freed me in Christ Jesus from the law of sin and of death" (8:2). The Spirit of life is the pneumatic Christ in resurrection, and in resurrection death cannot hold Him; He overcomes all death. We are so thankful that the ministry among us has helped us to see the Spirit of life. In this life there is resurrection. In this life nothing can confine us, and death cannot lay hold of us. We overcome everything by the Spirit of life. Resurrection is installed in us by the Spirit of life. The Spirit of life is also the reality of life, for this Spirit contains the element of the divine life.
THE SPIRIT OF REALITY, THE SPIRIT OF WHAT GOD IS, HAS, AND DOES
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of reality, the Spirit of what God is, has, and does (John 14:17; 15:26; 16:13). Whatever the Triune God is, is ours; whatever He has, is ours; and whatever He has done, is ours. All this is by the Spirit of reality. The Spirit of reality takes care of our needs and our limitations, and He brings us all that God is, has, and has done. Only a foolish person would say that he has more needs than can be supplied by the Spirit. We have the Spirit of reality, and in this Spirit we have everything. We have God: We have who God is, we have what God has, and we have what God has done. All this is in our spirit because we have the Spirit.
Moreover, the Spirit of reality is the linking between us and the Triune God, making us one with the Triune God in experience. This makes our Christian life very subjective. The Spirit makes us one with the Triune God not in doctrine or in mere thought but in experience. We experience the Triune God because we have the Spirit of reality.—T. C.
Many of the points in this series of messages concerning the crucial contents of God's New Testament ministry were either recovered through the ministry of Brother Nee and Brother Lee, or our brothers' ministry represents a great progression in the recovery of these divine truths. The apostles' teaching, the New Testament ministry, and God's economy have never been properly revealed or defined as they have been in this ministry. Concerning the Triune God, the truths have been opened, and the veils have been pulled back, not only related to the truth but also to our experience. Likewise, this ministry has revealed so much concerning the all-inclusive Christ which we never saw before, and this ministry has caused us to fall in love with the Lord. Moreover, many of the truths concerning the full ministry of Christ in His three divine and mystical stages have never before been spoken in this way in the history of Christianity, yet they have now been opened to us.
In the same way, almost none of the points and aspects of the Spirit, which we are now considering, have ever been so thoroughly defined as they are defined today. Hardly any theologian has ever properly defined all the points in the outline of this message. Some may have referred to these aspects of the Spirit but without offering a thorough definition of them. Today we are enjoying the ministry concerning the Spirit, and we are feasting upon this ministry as it becomes our divine portion day by day. We should be so thankful that all these points are not merely objective truths to us in the Lord's recovery. On the one hand, we must hold these truths objectively, but on the other hand, if they are not experiential to us, God's economy has not reached its goal. All these items must become experiential to us. The Spirit of reality is making us one with the Triune God, not in doctrine but in experience. The problem today is that almost no believer has tapped into this experiential oneness with the Triune God. We have to be so thankful to the Lord that the Spirit of reality is being unveiled today in the Lord's recovery, not only for the sake of the truths but also to bring us into the full experience of the truths. This in particular is what Brother Lee brought us into. We are not here taking a course in theology. Rather, this is a "crash course" in the experience of God's New Testament ministry. This is an enjoyment and a feast. We are filled because this is not merely doctrine to us but our very experience. The apostles' teaching and all these matters must become experiential to us. Otherwise, these messages are vain and empty. If, however, they bring us into a living experience, all the truths that have been released will become our joy and enjoyment.
THE SPIRIT OF JESUS, WHO IS THE REALITY OF JESUS IN HIS SUFFERING HUMANITY
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jesus, who is the reality of Jesus in His suffering humanity (Acts 16:7). Jesus was the name given to our Lord by God. The name Jesus denotes the Lord's humanity. Jesus, Jehovah the Savior, was His name as He lived on the earth after His incarnation. His human living for thirty-three and a half years was fraught with all kinds of suffering. At the end of His life in the flesh He endured the ultimate suffering, which was His crucifixion. Through resurrection He was transfigured to be the Spirit of Jesus, and in this Spirit is incarnation, humanity, human living, and crucifixion.
Because Paul was suffering in Acts 16, the Spirit of Jesus was with him having not only the divine element of God but also the elements of humanity, human living, and crucifixion, the suffering of death. Such an all-inclusive Spirit was needed by Paul in his preaching ministry, a ministry with sufferings for the sake of the Body of Christ (Col. 1:24). Paul was able to endure such sufferings because of the Spirit of Jesus. Jesus lived in him as the all-inclusive Spirit, and because Jesus had passed through this kind of living, He was able to be one with Paul and to bring Paul through every trial. In our service to the Lord we encounter all manner of sufferings, but the Spirit of Jesus always meets us in our sufferings. By the Spirit of Jesus, no suffering for the sake of the Body of Christ is too great.
THE SPIRIT OF CHRIST WITH THE ELEMENT OF RESURRECTION
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Christ with the element of resurrection (Rom. 8:9). The Spirit of Christ is Christ in His divinity, who conquered death and became life in resurrection with the resurrection power. The Spirit of Christ with the element of resurrection is the death-conquering and the life-dispensing Spirit. The context of Romans 8:9, which speaks of the Spirit of Christ, is the resurrection of Christ (v. 11), showing that the Spirit of Christ is related to His resurrection. His resurrection was death- conquering; He overcame death by His resurrection power. His resurrection was also life-dispensing. Today as the One who is not only human but divine, He brings us life because He passed through death into resurrection. He not only passed through humanity with all of its experiences to be the Spirit of Jesus, but He also passed through death into resurrection to be the Spirit of Christ, the death-conquering and life-dispensing Spirit. Such a Spirit of Christ must become our experience. We not only enjoy the all-inclusive Spirit as the Spirit of Jesus in our suffering, but we also enjoy the Spirit of Christ in conquering death and dispensing life.
THE SPIRIT OF JESUS CHRIST WITH THE BOUNTIFUL SUPPLY OF ALL THE ELEMENTS OF DIVINITY, HUMANITY, HUMAN LIVING, CRUCIFIXION, AND RESURRECTION
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit of Jesus Christ with the bountiful supply of all the elements of divinity, humanity, human living, crucifixion, and resurrection. We always need the bountiful supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ. This supply meets all our needs. The Spirit of Jesus Christ is the Spirit of the Jesus who lived a life of suffering on the earth and of the Christ who is now in resurrection. In his suffering Paul experienced both the Lords suffering in His humanity and the Lord's resurrection.
Philippians 1:19-21 says, "For I know that for me this will turn out to salvation through your petition and the bountiful supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ, according to my earnest expectation and hope that in nothing I will be put to shame, but with all boldness, as always, even now Christ will be magnified in my body, whether through life or through death. For to me, to live is Christ and to die is gain." When Paul wrote this, he was suffering in prison. This was perhaps the topmost suffering for a person at that time. However, in his suffering Paul experienced both the Lord's suffering in His humanity and the Lord's resurrection. He declared that in his suffering he had the bountiful supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ. What a statement this was! He passed through this topmost suffering by his experience of the Spirit of Jesus Christ. A number of brothers were with Brother Lee during his last days and months. Many times when we would come together to pray for him, we would pray, "Lord, regardless of how intense his sufferings are, regardless of what he has to pass through, may our brother be put to shame in nothing, and may it be that for him to live is Christ." Those who were around him, especially the nurses and doc tors and those who cared for him in an intimate way, can testify that Brother Lee enjoyed the bountiful supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ. We all pass through certain kinds of sufferings, and eventually we may pass through death, but we praise the Lord that we all have the bountiful supply of the Spirit of Jesus Christ. This is not merely something doctrinal; rather, it is something very experiential.
THE COMPOUND SPIRIT TYPIFIED BY THE COMPOUND OINTMENT
The all-inclusive Spirit is the compound Spirit typified by the compound ointment (Exo. 30:22-31). The truth concerning the compound Spirit is one of the top revelations given to us by the Lord through Brother Lee. About one hundred years ago, the Brethren saw that the olive oil typifies the Spirit, but this was as far as they progressed in the divine revelation. Today the progression of the revelation in the Lord's recovery has gone far beyond the hin of olive oil. Brother Lee opened up all the details concerning the spices which were added to the olive oil.
Composed of a Hin of Olive Oil Blended and Compounded with Four Elements with Their Respective Units and Numbers
The compound ointment is composed of a hin of olive oil blended and compounded with four elements—myrrh, cinnamon, calamus, and cassia—with their respective units and numbers. The compound ointment contains five hundred shekels of myrrh, two hundred fifty shekels each of cinnamon and calamus, and five hundred shekels of cassia. The quantities of the four spices are three times five hundred shekels, but the second five hundred is split into two units of two hundred fifty. Three is the number of the Triune God, the second of whom—the Lord Jesus Christ—was cut in His death on the cross. The single measure of olive oil represents God Himself, and in the Bible four signifies the created man, especially in Ezekiel and Revelation, where we see the four living creatures among whom man takes the lead. Therefore, God is in this ointment, and man is also in it. This man is the Lord Jesus Christ.
Typifying Man and God Compounded Together with the Death and Resurrection of Christ, the Triune God, and the Power for Responsibility
The compound ointment typifies man and God compounded together with the sweet and effective death of Christ and the flavor and power of Christ's resurrection, the Triune God, and the power for responsibility. Myrrh in the Bible always signifies death; the myrrh in the ointment speaks of the death of Christ. Cinnamon is a sweet, aromatic spice. This speaks of the sweetness and the effectiveness of Christ's death. Calamus is a reed that shoots up toward the heavens out of the marsh. This is a type of the precious resurrection of Christ. Cassia is another aromatic spice, whose scent was used to repel insects and snakes. This signifies the effective power and authority of the Lord's resurrection, which repels all the demonic "insects" and the great serpent, Satan. All these elements are the ingredients in the compound ointment. Such a compound ointment is the blending, mingling, incorporation, and compounding of the oil with all the spices. God is there, and the man Christ Jesus, who passed through all the processes as typified and signified by the four spices, is also there. The Triune God is there, and this Triune God is mingled with man.
The compound ointment contains five main elements. The number five is composed of one plus four. Five hundred shekels is a hundred fives, and two times two hundred fifty is another hundred fives. Five signifies responsibility. How can we bear responsibility for the Lord's move? None of us can bear responsibility. We are weak; we cannot speak, preach, testify, or do anything. It seems as if we are absolutely impotent. One who ministers for the Lord may feel that he cannot even walk up to the platform to speak. In ourselves none of us can do anything, but One has been mingled with our spirit, and He is the compound ointment who bears all the responsibility. The fingers on our hand illustrate this principle. If a brother holds a book with his four fingers, it is easy for someone to take it away from him. This is a picture of how our humanity can bear no responsibility. If, however, the brother holds the book with his thumb plus his four fingers, it is very hard to take the book from him. This illustrates that if God is added to us, we are able to bear responsibility. Four can never bear the responsibility, but four plus one can bear not only a little responsibility but full responsibility, signified by one hundred times five. We possess such a wonderful compound Spirit. He is not merely our doctrine but our experience.
For Anointing Everything and Every Person Related to God's Worship
The compound ointment is for anointing everything and every person related to God's worship to separate them from anything common, making them most holy for God's service. The ointment is to anoint the tabernacle, all the utensils within the tabernacle, and the priests themselves for their service to God. The compound ointment is a wonderful type, and Brother Lee gave many messages on it. This is also a great matter in the Bible, a great revelation given by the Lord to His recovery.
THE LORD SPIRIT WITH THE ELEMENTS OF ASCENSION AND LORDSHIP
The Lord Spirit is the Lord who is the Spirit and the Spirit who is the Lord. The Lord Spirit is a compound title referring to the pneumatic Christ. The Lord Spirit is for our transformation (2 Cor. 3:17-18). The all-inclusive Spirit is the Lord Spirit with the elements of ascension and lordship. The elements of the all-inclusive Spirit include God, man, divinity, humanity, incarnation, human living, crucifixion, and resurrection, plus ascension and lordship. All these have been compounded together to become the wonderful compound Spirit, and such a Spirit now dwells in our spirit. How can we overcome? It is by the Spirit. How can we live a proper human life with our family, spouse, and children? It is by the Spirit. How can we preach the gospel? It is also by this Spirit. The way to have all things under our feet is to partake of the ascension of Christ and even of His lordship. All these elements are in the all-inclusive Spirit, and they are all ours to experience. There is not one thing that we need that cannot be supplied to us by the all-inclusive Spirit. In every way, whenever we live by this all-inclusive Spirit, He meets our every need.
THE SEVEN SPIRITS WITH THE SEVENFOLD INTENSIFICATION
The One Spirit of God Who Is Sevenfold for God's Move
The all-inclusive Spirit is the seven Spirits with the sevenfold intensification (Rev. 1:4; 4:5; 5:6) The seven Spirits actually are the one Spirit of God who is sevenfold for God's move to carry out God's administration, to execute God's economy in the universe. The sevenfold intensified Spirit is not only for our experience; it is through the sevenfold Spirit that God executes His divine administration on this earth. The sevenfold Spirit is running through the whole earth to carry out God's economy. Who opened up Russia in the early 1990s? This was carried out by the throne of God and the sevenfold Spirit running through the whole earth. No man was sufficient to open up Russia; the seven Spirits did this, and now the Lord is carrying out and executing His economy, even in that land.
For Us to Be Vitalized, to Be Overcomers in the Degradation of the Church
Such an intensified Spirit is for us to be vitalized, to be overcomers in the degradation of the church. How can we be overcomers? When we contact the sevenfold intensified Spirit, who is full of life, we are vitalized immediately. We become living not merely by reading the Bible but by touching the Spirit in the Word. We must touch the sevenfold Spirit when we pray and call on the name of the Lord, and when we touch Him, we are vitalized, and we become another kind of person. We may think that those who migrated to Russia for the Lord's move are the giants in the Lord's recovery. In one sense, actually, they are the weak ones. Because of this, some questioned whether it would be possible for the Lord to carry out His recovery in Russia through these migrating ones. However, the co-workers had the sevenfold intensified Spirit, and this Spirit was operating to run in that country and raise up His recovery there.
Recently more of the full-time training graduates went to Russia, and some of them were assigned to labor in the Ukraine, which is mostly Russian-speaking. In one of the localities there, the only co-workers available to visit the saints were three sisters. When the local saints first saw them, they were disappointed. Still, they began to fellowship and pray together, and after a few days they were all rejoicing that the Lord had brought those sisters to them. Those sisters had become "strong lions" by the sevenfold Spirit. The sevenfold Spirit makes us strong ones, not weak ones. Such a Spirit is intensified to vitalize us to make us another kind of person.
The Seven Lamps of Fire Burning, Judging, Enlightening, Searching, Exposing, and Purifying Us
The seven Spirits as the seven lamps of fire burning before the throne are burning, judging, enlightening, searching, exposing, and purifying us for producing and building up the churches as the golden lampstands. We truly need this sevenfold intensified Spirit to be applied to us as the seven lamps of fire burning before His throne. We all need to be burned, judged, enlightened, searched, exposed, and purified. This is all for God's economy.
The Eyes of Christ Observing Us and Transfusing Us with All His Riches
The seven Spirits as the eyes of Christ are observing us and transfusing us with all His riches. The sevenfold Spirit is not only burning, judging, enlightening, searching, exposing, and purifying; He is also looking at us, observing us, and as He observes us, He infuses and transfuses all that He is into us as the sevenfold Spirit.
THE SPIRIT, THE CONSUMMATED SPIRIT AS THE CONSUMMATION OF THE PROCESSED TRIUNE GOD
The all-inclusive Spirit is the Spirit, the consummated Spirit as the consummation of the processed Triune God (Rev. 22:17). John 7:39 says, "But this He said concerning the Spirit, whom those who believed into Him were about to receive; for the Spirit was not yet, because Jesus had not yet been glorified." Through glorification by His resurrection Christ became the Spirit who "was not yet" before His resurrection.
The Spirit as the consummation of the processed Triune God marries the bride as the consummation of the redeemed, regenerated, and transformed tripartite man. This life-giving Spirit is the consummation of the processed Triune God, and this One who is ultimately, finally, and completely processed will marry a wonderful bride, who is the consummation of the redeemed, regenerated, and transformed tripartite man. The Spirit as the consummated God and the transformed tripartite man will be married to be one heavenly, universal couple for eternity. The day of our human marriage was a happy one, but we are expecting a happier day. Christian couples sometimes are heavenly, but often they are earthly. One day, however, we will be the bride to marry this wonderful consummated Spirit, and we will be one heavenly, universal couple for eternity. What a glorious future we have!—-B. P.

TOP-纲目|Outline|对照-目录
　
　
第八篇　永远的生命─非受造、不能毁坏、不朽坏的生命，我们在其中得救并在其中作王
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　我们物质的身体里有生物的生命（希腊文，bios，白阿司），我们的魂里有心理的生命（希腊文，psuche，朴宿克），但我们得重生时接受了另一个生命，就是永远的生命（希腊文，zoe，奏厄）：
一　永远的生命不仅是永久的，更是在时间和性质上都是永远的生命─约三16，36，约壹一2。
二　永远的生命是神非受造的生命、不能毁坏的生命、和不朽坏的生命─弗四18，来七16，提后一10。
三　永远的生命是那在神儿子里面的生命，并且这生命就是神的儿子─约壹五11～12，一2，约一4，十四6。
四　永远的生命是信徒凭以得重生的生命，这生命且成了信徒的生命，使信徒成为神的儿女和基督的肢体─西三4上，约一12～13，弗五30。
五　永远的生命是我们该持定的生命─提前六12。
贰　永远的生命成了从神给我们的祝福，有三个阶段，这三个阶段是在三个时代：
一　在今世，召会时代，我们接受永远的生命作白白的恩赐，给我们享受，并凭以活着─约三15～16。
二　在来世，国度时代，我们承受永远的生命为赏赐，那时对永远生命的享受要比在今世的享受更丰满─太十九17，路十八29～30，启二7。
三　在永世，就是在以新耶路撒冷为中心的新天新地里，我们要享受永远生命的终极完成，作为最完满的祝福─启二二1～2，14。
叁　神把悔改以得永远的生命赐给祂所拣选的人，也指定、命定他们得这生命─徒十一18，十三48。
肆　基督在十字架上受死的义行，叫众人都被称义得生命─罗五18：
一　生命是神救恩的目标，因此称义乃是生命的称义。
二　我们借著称义，已经达到并符合神义的标准，所以现在神能将祂的生命分赐给我们。
伍　信徒在这生命的新样中生活行动─罗六4。
陆　三一神的生命分赐到三部分人里面，而在这生命里借着重生、圣别、更新、变化、模成并荣化，在主观方面拯救信徒─罗五10下：
一　第一，这生命是在那灵里神的生命─罗八2。
二　第二，这生命借着重生，成了我们灵里的生命─罗八10。
三　而后，这生命要从我们的灵，浸透我们的心思，使我们心思所属的魂变化，而成为在我们魂里的生命─罗八6。
四　最终，这生命要渗入我们的身体，成为我们身体里的生命，终极的结果，是我们的身体改变形状，也就是我们的身体得赎─罗八11，腓三21，罗八23。
柒　信徒需要借着恩典在生命中作王管理万有，而得永远的生命─罗五17，21：
一　神完整的救恩是使我们借着洋溢之恩并洋溢之义的恩赐，在生命中作王：
１　义的恩赐是为着神法理的救赎；恩典是为使我们经历神生机的拯救：
a　义的恩赐是神法理的救赎实际的应用在我们身上。
b　恩典是神自己作我们全丰全足的供应，为着我们生机的拯救。
２　在生命中作王，乃是对神生机拯救完满的经历。
二　我们重生所得的生命是神圣、属灵、属天、作王、君尊的生命─可四26，约壹三9。
三　罗马五章里的在生命中作王，是罗马六至十六章里一切事的钥匙：
１　我们必须从这观点来看罗马六至十六章里的一切。
２　我们若在生命中作王，我们就在这些章里所陈明的一切事上有分。
四　按经历说，在生命中作王的意思就是在神圣生命的管治之下：
１　基督是在生命中作王的榜样，祂一直在父神圣生命的管治之下─太八9。
２　保罗是一个榜样，他在生活和职事上，都在神圣生命的管治之下─林后二12～14。
３　所有得着洋溢之恩并洋溢之义的恩赐的信徒，都必须操练在神圣生命中受约束和限制。
五　我们在生命中作王，活在神圣生命的管治之下，其结果乃是真实并实际的身体生活，显在召会生活中。
六　罗马十二至十三章中活出身体生活的每一项，都需要我们受神圣生命的管治：
１　我们必须为神的怜恤所夺取─十二1上。
２　我们必须将身体献上，当作活祭─十二1下。
３　我们不该模仿这世代，反要借着心思的更新而变化─十二2。
４　我们不该看自己过于所当看的，乃要照着神所分给各人信心的度量，看得清明适度─十二3。
５　我们应当承认我们在一个身体上有好些肢体，但肢体不都有一样的功用─十二4。
七　我们需要借着在生命中作王，为着身体的生活，活出最高美德的生活：
１　我们爱人不可假冒，并且爱弟兄要彼此亲热─罗十二9上，10上。
２　我们殷勤不可懒惰，要灵里火热，常常服事主─十二11。
３　我们在患难中应当忍耐─十二12中。
４　我们应当与喜乐的人同乐，与哀哭的人同哭─十二15。
５　若是可能，我们总要尽力与众人和睦─十二18。
八　在生命中作王乃是“以至于永远的生命”─罗五21：
１　“以至于永远的生命”是一个特别的说法。
２　约翰四章十四节下半说，“我所赐的水，要在他里面成为泉源，直涌入永远的生命”：
a　“涌入”（即罗马五章二十一节的“得”，直译，以至于）说到目的，意思也是“成为”。
b　永远的生命至终要成为新耶路撒冷。
c　“涌入永远的生命”意思乃是“归入新耶路撒冷”。
３　新耶路撒冷是神圣生命的总和，也就是神生命的总和。
４　我们在生命中作王的结果和目标乃是新耶路撒冷，就是神人二性联调的宇宙合并。
参读　主恢复的简说，第肆大点；主今日恢复之主要项目的重点；约翰福音结晶读经，第十四篇；晨兴圣言─罗马书中神完整的救恩结晶读经，第二至三周；罗马书生命读经，第六十二篇；三一神作三部分人的生命，第六至七篇。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message Eight
The Eternal Life— the Uncreated, Indestructible, Incorruptible Life in Which We Are Saved and in Which We Reign
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　In our physical body we have a biological life (Gk.?bios), in our soul we have a psychological life (Gk.?psuche), but when we were regenerated we received another life, the eternal life (Gk.?zoe):
A.　The eternal life is the life that is not only everlasting but also eternal both in time and in nature—John 3:16, 36; 1 John 1:2.
B.　The eternal life is the uncreated life of God, the indestructible life, and the incorruptible life—Eph. 4:18; Heb. 7:16; 2 Tim. 1:10.
C.　The eternal life is the life that is in the Son of God and that is the Son of God—1 John 5:11-12; 1:2; John 1:4; 14:6.
D.　The eternal life is the life with which the believers are regenerated and which becomes the believers' life, making the believers the children of God and the members of Christ—Col. 3:4a; John 1:12-13; Eph. 5:30.
E.　The eternal life is the life on which we should lay hold—1 Tim. 6:12.
II.　The eternal life as a blessing from God to us is in three stages, and these three stages are in three ages:
A.　In the present age, the church age, we receive the eternal life as a free gift for us to enjoy and live by—John 3:15-16.
B.　In the coming age, the kingdom age, we inherit eternal life as a reward with an enjoyment of the eternal life that is fuller than the enjoyment in this age—Matt. 19:17; Luke 18:29-30; Rev. 2:7.
C.　In the eternal age in the new heaven and new earth with the New Jerusalem as the center, we will enjoy the ultimate consummation of the eternal life in its fullest blessing—Rev. 22:1-2, 14.
