III.　God gives His chosen people repentance unto eternal life and has appointed, ordained, them to receive this life—Acts 11:18; 13:48.
IV.　Christ's righteous act of dying on the cross is unto justification of life to all men—Rom. 5:18:
A.　Life is the goal of God's salvation; thus, justification is "of life."
B.　Through justification we have come up to the standard of God's righteousness and correspond with it, so that now He can impart His life to us.
V.　The believers walk in the newness of this life—Rom. 6:4.
VI.　The life of the Triune God is dispensed into the tripartite man to save the believers subjectively in this life through regeneration, sanctification, renewing, transformation, conformation, and glorification—Rom. 5:10b:
A.　First, this life was the divine life in the Spirit—Rom. 8:2.
B.　Second, it became the life in our spirit through regeneration—Rom. 8:10.
C.　Then from our spirit it saturates our mind for the transformation of our soul, to which our mind belongs, and becomes the life in our soul—Rom. 8:6.
D.　Eventually, it will permeate our body and become the life in our body, ultimately issuing in the transfiguration of our body, that is, the redemption of our body—Rom. 8:11; Phil. 3:21; Rom. 8:23.
VII.　The believers need to reign in life with grace over all things unto eternal life—Rom. 5:17, 21:
A.　God's complete salvation is for us to reign in life by the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness:
1.　The gift of righteousness is for God's judicial redemption; grace is for us to experience God's organic salvation:
a.　The gift of righteousness is God's judicial redemption applied to us in a practical way.
b.　Grace is God Himself as our all-sufficient supply for our organic salvation.
2.　Reigning in life is the full experience of the organic salvation of God.
B.　We have been regenerated with a divine, spiritual, heavenly, kingly, and royal life—Mark 4:26; 1 John 3:9.
C.　Reigning in life in Romans 5 is the key to everything in Romans 6—16:
1.　We need to see everything in Romans 6—16 in this light.
2.　If we reign in life, we are in all the matters presented in these chapters.
D.　In experience, to reign in life means to be under the ruling of the divine life:
1.　Christ is a pattern of reigning in life by being under the ruling of the divine life of the Father—Matt. 8:9.
2.　Paul is an example of one who, in his life and ministry, was under the ruling of the divine life—2 Cor. 2:12-14.
3.　There is the need for all the believers who have received the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness to practice the restriction and limitation in the divine life.
E.　The issue of our reigning in life, living under the ruling of the divine life, is the real and practical Body life expressed in the church life.
F.　Each item of the living of the Body life in Romans 12—13 requires us to be ruled by the divine life:
1.　We need to be captivated by the compassions of God—12:1a.
2.　We must present our bodies a living sacrifice—12:1b.
3.　We should not be fashioned according to this age but be transformed by the renewing of the mind—12:2.
4.　We should not think more highly of ourselves than we ought to think, but think so as to be sober-minded, as God has apportioned to each a measure of faith—12:3.
5.　We should consider that we have many members in one body, and all the members do not have the same function—12:4.
G.　We need to live a life of the highest virtues for the Body life by reigning in life:
1.　We should love without hypocrisy and love one another warmly in brotherly love—12:9a, 10a.
2.　We should not be slothful in zeal but burning in spirit, serving the Lord—12:11.
3.　We should endure in tribulation—12:12b.
4.　We should rejoice with those who rejoice and weep with those who weep—12:15.
5.　If possible, as far as it depends on us, we should live in peace with all men—12:18.
H.　Reigning in life is "unto eternal life"—Rom. 5:21:
1.　Unto eternal life?is a particular expression.
2.　John 4:14b says, "The water that I will give him will become in him a spring of water gushing up into eternal life":
a.　Into?(unto?in Rom. 5:21) speaks of destination and also means "to become" or "to be."
b.　The eternal life eventually will be the New Jerusalem.
c.　Into eternal life?means?into the New Jerusalem.
3.　The New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine life, the totality of the life of God.
4.　The issue and goal of our reigning in life is the New Jerusalem, the universal incorporation of the union and mingling of divinity with humanity.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第八篇　永远的生命─非受造、不能毁坏、不朽坏的生命，我们在其中得救并在其中作王
The Eternal Life— the Uncreated, Indestructible, Incorruptible Life in Which We Are Saved and in Which We Reign
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
壹　我们物质的身体里有生物的生命（希腊文，bios，白阿司），我们的魂里有心理的生命（希腊文，psuche，朴宿克），但我们得重生时接受了另一个生命，就是永远的生命（希腊文，zoe，奏厄）：
I.　In our physical body we have a biological life (Gk.?bios), in our soul we have a psychological life (Gk.?psuche), but when we were regenerated we received another life, the eternal life (Gk.?zoe):
一　永远的生命不仅是永久的，更是在时间和性质上都是永远的生命─约三16，36，约壹一2。
A.　The eternal life is the life that is not only everlasting but also eternal both in time and in nature—John 3:16, 36; 1 John 1:2.
二　永远的生命是神非受造的生命、不能毁坏的生命、和不朽坏的生命─弗四18，来七16，提后一10。
B.　The eternal life is the uncreated life of God, the indestructible life, and the incorruptible life—Eph. 4:18; Heb. 7:16; 2 Tim. 1:10.
三　永远的生命是那在神儿子里面的生命，并且这生命就是神的儿子─约壹五11～12，一2，约一4，十四6。
C.　The eternal life is the life that is in the Son of God and that is the Son of God—1 John 5:11-12; 1:2; John 1:4; 14:6.
四　永远的生命是信徒凭以得重生的生命，这生命且成了信徒的生命，使信徒成为神的儿女和基督的肢体─西三4上，约一12～13，弗五30。
D.　The eternal life is the life with which the believers are regenerated and which becomes the believers' life, making the believers the children of God and the members of Christ—Col. 3:4a; John 1:12-13; Eph. 5:30.
五　永远的生命是我们该持定的生命─提前六12。
E.　The eternal life is the life on which we should lay hold—1 Tim. 6:12.
贰　永远的生命成了从神给我们的祝福，有三个阶段，这三个阶段是在三个时代：
II.　The eternal life as a blessing from God to us is in three stages, and these three stages are in three ages:
一　在今世，召会时代，我们接受永远的生命作白白的恩赐，给我们享受，并凭以活着─约三15～16。
A.　In the present age, the church age, we receive the eternal life as a free gift for us to enjoy and live by—John 3:15-16.
二　在来世，国度时代，我们承受永远的生命为赏赐，那时对永远生命的享受要比在今世的享受更丰满─太十九17，路十八29～30，启二7。
B.　In the coming age, the kingdom age, we inherit eternal life as a reward with an enjoyment of the eternal life that is fuller than the enjoyment in this age—Matt. 19:17; Luke 18:29-30; Rev. 2:7.
三　在永世，就是在以新耶路撒冷为中心的新天新地里，我们要享受永远生命的终极完成，作为最完满的祝福─启二二1～2，14。
C.　In the eternal age in the new heaven and new earth with the New Jerusalem as the center, we will enjoy the ultimate consummation of the eternal life in its fullest blessing—Rev. 22:1-2, 14.
叁　神把悔改以得永远的生命赐给祂所拣选的人，也指定、命定他们得这生命─徒十一18，十三48。
III.　God gives His chosen people repentance unto eternal life and has appointed, ordained, them to receive this life—Acts 11:18; 13:48.
肆　基督在十字架上受死的义行，叫众人都被称义得生命─罗五18：
IV.　Christ's righteous act of dying on the cross is unto justification of life to all men—Rom. 5:18:
一　生命是神救恩的目标，因此称义乃是生命的称义。
A.　Life is the goal of God's salvation; thus, justification is "of life."
二　我们借著称义，已经达到并符合神义的标准，所以现在神能将祂的生命分赐给我们。
B.　Through justification we have come up to the standard of God's righteousness and correspond with it, so that now He can impart His life to us.
伍　信徒在这生命的新样中生活行动─罗六4。
V.　The believers walk in the newness of this life—Rom. 6:4.
陆　三一神的生命分赐到三部分人里面，而在这生命里借着重生、圣别、更新、变化、模成并荣化，在主观方面拯救信徒─罗五10下：
VI.　The life of the Triune God is dispensed into the tripartite man to save the believers subjectively in this life through regeneration, sanctification, renewing, transformation, conformation, and glorification—Rom. 5:10b:
一　第一，这生命是在那灵里神的生命─罗八2。
A.　First, this life was the divine life in the Spirit—Rom. 8:2.
二　第二，这生命借着重生，成了我们灵里的生命─罗八10。
B.　Second, it became the life in our spirit through regeneration—Rom. 8:10.
三　而后，这生命要从我们的灵，浸透我们的心思，使我们心思所属的魂变化，而成为在我们魂里的生命─罗八6。
C.　Then from our spirit it saturates our mind for the transformation of our soul, to which our mind belongs, and becomes the life in our soul—Rom. 8:6.
四　最终，这生命要渗入我们的身体，成为我们身体里的生命，终极的结果，是我们的身体改变形状，也就是我们的身体得赎─罗八11，腓三21，罗八23。
D.　Eventually, it will permeate our body and become the life in our body, ultimately issuing in the transfiguration of our body, that is, the redemption of our body—Rom. 8:11; Phil. 3:21; Rom. 8:23.
柒　信徒需要借着恩典在生命中作王管理万有，而得永远的生命─罗五17，21：
VII.　The believers need to reign in life with grace over all things unto eternal life—Rom. 5:17, 21:
一　神完整的救恩是使我们借着洋溢之恩并洋溢之义的恩赐，在生命中作王：
A.　God's complete salvation is for us to reign in life by the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness:
１　义的恩赐是为着神法理的救赎；恩典是为使我们经历神生机的拯救：
1.　The gift of righteousness is for God's judicial redemption; grace is for us to experience God's organic salvation:
a　义的恩赐是神法理的救赎实际的应用在我们身上。
a.　The gift of righteousness is God's judicial redemption applied to us in a practical way.
b　恩典是神自己作我们全丰全足的供应，为着我们生机的拯救。
b.　Grace is God Himself as our all-sufficient supply for our organic salvation.
２　在生命中作王，乃是对神生机拯救完满的经历。
2.　Reigning in life is the full experience of the organic salvation of God.
二　我们重生所得的生命是神圣、属灵、属天、作王、君尊的生命─可四26，约壹三9。
B.　We have been regenerated with a divine, spiritual, heavenly, kingly, and royal life—Mark 4:26; 1 John 3:9.
三　罗马五章里的在生命中作王，是罗马六至十六章里一切事的钥匙：
C.　Reigning in life in Romans 5 is the key to everything in Romans 6—16:
１　我们必须从这观点来看罗马六至十六章里的一切。
1.　We need to see everything in Romans 6—16 in this light.
２　我们若在生命中作王，我们就在这些章里所陈明的一切事上有分。
2.　If we reign in life, we are in all the matters presented in these chapters.
四　按经历说，在生命中作王的意思就是在神圣生命的管治之下：
D.　In experience, to reign in life means to be under the ruling of the divine life:
１　基督是在生命中作王的榜样，祂一直在父神圣生命的管治之下─太八9。
1.　Christ is a pattern of reigning in life by being under the ruling of the divine life of the Father—Matt. 8:9.
２　保罗是一个榜样，他在生活和职事上，都在神圣生命的管治之下─林后二12～14。
2.　Paul is an example of one who, in his life and ministry, was under the ruling of the divine life—2 Cor. 2:12-14.
３　所有得着洋溢之恩并洋溢之义的恩赐的信徒，都必须操练在神圣生命中受约束和限制。
3.　There is the need for all the believers who have received the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness to practice the restriction and limitation in the divine life.
五　我们在生命中作王，活在神圣生命的管治之下，其结果乃是真实并实际的身体生活，显在召会生活中。
E.　The issue of our reigning in life, living under the ruling of the divine life, is the real and practical Body life expressed in the church life.
六　罗马十二至十三章中活出身体生活的每一项，都需要我们受神圣生命的管治：
F.　Each item of the living of the Body life in Romans 12—13 requires us to be ruled by the divine life:
１　我们必须为神的怜恤所夺取─十二1上。
1.　We need to be captivated by the compassions of God—12:1a.
２　我们必须将身体献上，当作活祭─十二1下。
2.　We must present our bodies a living sacrifice—12:1b.
３　我们不该模仿这世代，反要借着心思的更新而变化─十二2。
3.　We should not be fashioned according to this age but be transformed by the renewing of the mind—12:2.
４　我们不该看自己过于所当看的，乃要照着神所分给各人信心的度量，看得清明适度─十二3。
4.　We should not think more highly of ourselves than we ought to think, but think so as to be sober-minded, as God has apportioned to each a measure of faith—12:3.
５　我们应当承认我们在一个身体上有好些肢体，但肢体不都有一样的功用─十二4。
5.　We should consider that we have many members in one body, and all the members do not have the same function—12:4.
七　我们需要借着在生命中作王，为着身体的生活，活出最高美德的生活：
G.　We need to live a life of the highest virtues for the Body life by reigning in life:
１　我们爱人不可假冒，并且爱弟兄要彼此亲热─罗十二9上，10上。
1.　We should love without hypocrisy and love one another warmly in brotherly love—12:9a, 10a.
２　我们殷勤不可懒惰，要灵里火热，常常服事主─十二11。
2.　We should not be slothful in zeal but burning in spirit, serving the Lord—12:11.
３　我们在患难中应当忍耐─十二12中。
3.　We should endure in tribulation—12:12b.
４　我们应当与喜乐的人同乐，与哀哭的人同哭─十二15。
4.　We should rejoice with those who rejoice and weep with those who weep—12:15.
５　若是可能，我们总要尽力与众人和睦─十二18。
5.　If possible, as far as it depends on us, we should live in peace with all men—12:18.
八　在生命中作王乃是“以至于永远的生命”─罗五21：
H.　Reigning in life is "unto eternal life"—Rom. 5:21:
１　“以至于永远的生命”是一个特别的说法。
1.　Unto eternal life?is a particular expression.
２　约翰四章十四节下半说，“我所赐的水，要在他里面成为泉源，直涌入永远的生命”：
2.　John 4:14b says, "The water that I will give him will become in him a spring of water gushing up into eternal life":
a　“涌入”（即罗马五章二十一节的“得”，直译，以至于）说到目的，意思也是“成为”。
a.　Into?(unto?in Rom. 5:21) speaks of destination and also means "to become" or "to be."
b　永远的生命至终要成为新耶路撒冷。
b.　The eternal life eventually will be the New Jerusalem.
c　“涌入永远的生命”意思乃是“归入新耶路撒冷”。
c.　Into eternal life?means?into the New Jerusalem.
３　新耶路撒冷是神圣生命的总和，也就是神生命的总和。
3.　The New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine life, the totality of the life of God.
４　我们在生命中作王的结果和目标乃是新耶路撒冷，就是神人二性联调的宇宙合并。
4.　The issue and goal of our reigning in life is the New Jerusalem, the universal incorporation of the union and mingling of divinity with humanity.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE EIGHT
THE ETERNAL LIFE—THE UNCREATED, INDESTRUCTIBLE, INCORRUPTIBLE LIFE IN WHICH WE ARE SAVED AND IN WHICH WE REIGN
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
The eternal life is God the Father in Christ Jesus as the Spirit flowing into us. This life is a wonderful person who is God Himself. When we speak of eternal life, we are not speaking of something other than the person of God. John 3:16 is a very popular verse in Christianity. It says, "For God so loved the world that He gave His only begotten Son, that every one who believes into Him would not perish, but would have eternal life." Many Christians take this eternal life to merely mean everlasting life, thinking that it is only the blessing of going to a heavenly mansion to enjoy a better life, a blissful environment which they will enjoy for eternity after they die. Actually, the eternal and divine life is God Himself entering into us to be our life, so that we may receive another life apart from our human life. As footnote 1 of this verse in the Recovery Version tells us, God so loved sinful, fallen people "that He gave them His only begotten Son, His expression, that they might obtain His eternal life to become His many sons and be His corporate expression for the fulfillment of His eternal New Testament economy." Such an explanation uplifts our understanding of the eternal life.
HAVING A BIOLOGICAL LIFE AND A PSYCHOLOGICAL LIFE, BUT RECEIVING ANOTHER LIFE, THE ETERNAL LIFE
In our physical body we have a biological life (Gk. bios), in our soul we have a psychological life (Gk. psuche), but when we were regenerated we received another life, the eternal life (Gk. zoe). We should "major" in the zoe life, not the bios or psuche. As we who were close to Brother Lee observed his diminishing health, we were saddened. However, since by the Lord's mercy and in His recovery we have received light from the holy Word, our sadness was contained. We knew that Brother Lee did not have merely a physical life. In him was the eternal life, who is God Himself, and this life will never die. The biological life will pass away, but the zoe life will last forever. Those who came to this training from abroad paid a great price. To be sure, they did not come to see Brother Lee in his physical or psychological life. They came because they realize that among us there was a person who lived a life of denying his human life by following the divine and eternal life within him.
The eternal life is the life that is not only everlasting but also eternal both in time and in nature (John 3:16, 36; 1 John 1:2). Eternal mainly denotes the nature of this divine life, not the time element. The eternal life is the uncreated life of God, the indestructible life, and the incorruptible life (Eph. 4:18; Heb. 7:16; 2 Tim. 1:10). The eternal life is the life that is in the Son of God and that is the Son of God (1 John 5:11-12; 1:2; John 1:4; 14:6). Moreover, the eternal life is the life with which the believers are regenerated and which becomes the believers' life, making the believers the children of God and the members of Christ (Col. 3:4a; John 1:12-13; Eph. 5:30). Therefore, the eternal life is the life on which we should lay hold (1 Tim. 6:12). To deal with the degradation of the churches and fight the good fight of the faith in the Christian life and ministry, we need to lay hold on this eternal life. The Crucial Points of the Major Items of the Lord's Recovery Today on pages 18-19 says,
Thank the Lord that in the last seventy years He has recovered among us the scriptural view and the proper realization of the eternal life of God, which we have received of God through our believing in the Son of God,
Jesus Christ. It is a life on the highest plane, being the divine life of God and even the complete Triune God Himself, uncreated, incorruptible, indestructible, and also eternal. To be eternal means to be perfect and complete in quality, quantity, time, space, and existence. The eternal life that we received through our believing in Christ is perfect and complete in its quality, in its quantity, in time, in space, and in its existence. It is eternally perfect and complete. It exists eternally in time and in space. It is not transient but everlasting in all aspects. It is with this eternal and everlasting, perfect and complete, incorruptible and indestructible, wonderful and marvelous life that we have been regenerated, that we are being transformed, and that we will be glorified with the consummated Triune God Himself as our eternal glory. This is eternal life!
THE ETERNAL LIFE AS A BLESSING FROM GOD TO US BEING IN THREE STAGES, WHICH ARE IN THREE AGES
The eternal life as a blessing from God to us is in three stages, and these three stages are in three ages. In the present age, the church age, we receive the eternal life as a free gift for us to enjoy and live by. The Triune God is embodied in the all-inclusive Christ, and this all-inclusive Christ is realized as the all-inclusive Spirit, who is dispensing the divine and eternal life into all of us who are chosen by Him. According to John 3:15-16, we receive the eternal life when we believe into Christ. This takes place in the present age. However, there are other verses in the Bible that tell us that we must pay a price to enter into eternal life. Eternal life is something that we can enjoy and live by. If we continue to enjoy this eternal life and live by it, we will become the overcomers. Then in the coming age, the kingdom age, we inherit eternal life as a reward with an enjoyment of the eternal life that is fuller than the enjoyment in this age (Luke 18:29-30; Rev. 2:7). In Matthew 19:17 the Lord told one who came to Him, "If you want to enter into life, keep the commandments." We have to keep His commandments in order to enjoy eternal life as our reward.
In the eternal age in the new heaven and new earth with the New Jerusalem as the center, we will enjoy the ultimate consummation of the eternal life in its fullest blessing (Rev. 22:1-2,14). By the end of the thousand years of the kingdom age, we all will have become the overcomers. As the overcomers, we will enter into the eternal age. Today we enjoy the eternal life, and if we faithfully enjoy and live by this eternal life, we will inherit eternal life in a fuller way in the kingdom age. Finally, in the eternal age we will enjoy the eternal life to the fullest. This is our destiny.
GOD GIVING HIS CHOSEN PEOPLE REPENTANCE UNTO ETERNAL LIFE AND APPOINTING, ORDAINING, THEM TO RECEIVE THIS LIFE
God gives His chosen people repentance unto eternal life and has appointed, ordained, them to receive this life (Acts 11:18; 13:48). We may feel that we are no different from our classmates and neighbors, but the Lord has chosen us to give us repentance. This repentance is unto eternal life, which God has appointed and ordained us to receive.
CHRIST'S RIGHTEOUS ACT OF DYING ON THE CROSS BEING UNTO JUSTIFICATION OF LIFE TO ALL MEN
Christ's righteous act of dying on the cross is unto justification of life to all men (Rom. 5:18). Life is the goal of God's salvation; thus, justification is "of life." Life, not justification, is the goal. Through justification we have come up to the standard of God's righteousness and correspond with it, so that now He can impart His life to us. Judicial redemption is not the goal; it is only a procedure. What God wants is not merely good, perfect, clean, or justified men. What God wants is God-men, men who are full of God, full of the divine and eternal life. This life enters into us, and we can enter into it and walk in it. God's goal in our organic salvation is to work the eternal life into us and to cause this life to grow unto full maturity.
THE BELIEVERS WALKING IN THE NEWNESS OF THIS LIFE
The believers walk in the newness of this life (Rom. 6:4). This is the resurrection life, the life that causes us to reign in life. We received this life as a free gift, and we can now live in the realm of this life. If we do, the Triune God will continually dispense Himself into us until He accomplishes His full salvation.
THE LIFE OF THE TRIUNE GOD BEING DISPENSED INTO THE TRIPARTITE MAN TO SAVE THE BELIEVERS SUBJECTIVELY IN THIS LIFE
The life of the Triune God is dispensed into the tripartite man to save the believers subjectively in this life through regeneration, sanctification, renewing, transformation, conformation, and glorification. The Triune God wants to dispense Himself into the tripartite man. First Thessalonians 5:23 tells us that we have a spirit, a soul, and a body. However, before Brother Lee came to this country, very few people knew that man is tripartite, and many did not know that we have a human spirit. When some first heard that our human spirit is a container to receive the eternal life, they were shocked at this "new teaching." By the revelation which our brother passed on to us, we know that man is tripartite, and God is dispensing His eternal life into our tripartite being. Romans 5:10 says, "For if we, being enemies, were reconciled to God through the death of His Son, much more we will be saved in His life, having been reconciled." To be saved much more in His life is through God's organic salvation.
First, this life was the divine life in the Spirit (Rom. 8:2). Second, it became the life in our spirit through regeneration (v. 10). This life that God gave us came into our spirit which is the deepest part of our being, but it did not stay only there. From our spirit it saturates our mind for the transformation of our soul, to which our mind belongs, and becomes the life in our soul (v. 6). Eventually, it will permeate our body and become the life in our body, ultimately issuing in the transfiguration of our body, that is, the redemption of our body. This is our hope of glory. Romans 8:11 says that God will give life to our mortal bodies through the Spirit, and Philippians 3:21 says that Christ will transfigure the body of our humiliation to be conformed to the body of His glory. Romans 8:23 says that we groan in ourselves, eagerly awaiting sonship, the redemption of our body. By reading these verses we are comforted. We are not people without hope. What the Lord has given us is a full salvation. He has entered into us as eternal life in our spirit. Then He will transform our soul, and He will transfigure our body.—A. L.
The life of the Triune God is being dispensed into our being in a marvelous, rich way. When the Lord came in His incarnation, He said, "I have come that they may have life and may have it abundantly" (John 10:10b). This life is the zoe life. Before we received the Lord, we had the bios and the psuche life. Everyone in the world today is taking care of their physical and psychological lives, but now we are centering on the zoe life and being saved in this life. Christ said, "I am...the life" (11:25; 14:6). No one had ever before said this in the history of the universe. He is the uncreated, indestructible, incorruptible, eternal, wonderful life of the Triune God. This person is life, and in Him is life. Through His death this life was released from within Him, and in His resurrection He became a life-giving Spirit who is in our spirit now as the life-giver, desiring to give us His life. There is at least one part of our being—our human spirit—that is one hundred percent life. Our spirit is life, and when we set our mind on the spirit, our mind also becomes life. Then He gives life to our mortal body until our whole being is life, and we are fully saved in His life.
THE BELIEVERS NEEDING TO REIGN IN LIFE WITH GRACE OVER ALL THINGS UNTO ETERNAL LIFE
The believers need to reign in life with grace over all things unto eternal life (Rom. 5:17,21). The last conference that Brother Lee gave, in February 1997, was entitled The Experience of God's Organic Salvation Equaling Reigning in Christ's Life. The experience of our being saved in life from regeneration all the way to glorification is our reigning in life. Previously we may have thought that we would reign in life some day in the future. However, we need to reign in life now. Romans 1 through 4 unveils Gods judicial redemption, while Romans 5 through 16 unveils God's organic salvation. In Romans 5 there are four reigning things. Sin reigns and death reigns, but that is not all. Grace reigns in us and causes us to reign. It is also in chapter five that Paul speaks about reigning in life, showing that reigning in life is the key to experiencing God's entire organic salvation revealed in Romans 6 through 16. When we reign in life, we are in the process of being saved in His life to be constituted His overcoming bride for His good pleasure, satisfaction, and delight.
God's Complete Salvation for Us to Reign in Life by the Abundance of Grace and of the Gift of Righteousness
God's complete salvation is for us to reign in life by the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness. Romans 5:17 says, "Much more those who receive the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness will reign in life through the One, Jesus Christ." If we are to reign in life, we need to be the best receivers. We must say, "Lord, I open my whole being to receive You in abundance. I want to receive You as the abundance of grace and as the abundance of the gift of righteousness." Our reigning in life is the issue not of our endeavoring but of our receiving.
The gift of righteousness is for God's judicial redemption, while grace is for us to experience God's organic salvation. The gift of righteousness is God's judicial redemption applied to us in a practical way. Grace is God Himself as our all-sufficient supply for our organic salvation. Reigning in life is the full experience of the organic salvation of God. God's judicial redemption and His organic salvation comprise His complete salvation. We receive Christ as the abundance of the gift of righteousness and as the abundance of grace, and the spontaneous issue is that we reign in life. Therefore, every day the first thing we should do in the morning is to open our entire being to the Lord and say, "Lord, I want to receive You as my righteousness. I take You as my sin offering. I take You as my trespass offering. I take You as my burnt offering. I take You as the reality of all the offerings. I take You as the gift of righteousness." Then we need to open to receive Him as the abundance of grace, which is God in Christ as the Spirit to be our rich supply for our enjoyment. This experience issues in our reigning in life as kings.
Having Been Regenerated with a Divine, Spiritual, Heavenly, Kingly, and Royal Life
We have been regenerated with a divine, spiritual, heavenly, kingly, and royal life (Mark 4:26; 1 John 3:9). When we received Christ, the King of kings came into our spirit. We have the King's "genes" in us; that is, we have His heavenly, divine, spiritual, and royal life in our spirit, which causes us to be kings. To be a king is the destiny of every regenerated one. God's unique intention in the universe is that we would reign with Him. Revelation 22:5 says, "They will reign forever and ever." We will be the kings for eternity. We will begin to reign sooner or later, and it is better if it is sooner. We need to reign in life in this age so that we can reign with Him for a thousand years. We reign in life in this age not by struggling but by daily receiving the abundance of grace and the abundance of the gift of righteousness. We have the royal genes in us. Now we just need to receive the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness so that these genes will grow until we are fully matured kings.
Reigning in Life in Romans 5 Being the Key to Everything in Romans 6—16
Reigning in life in Romans 5 is the key to everything in Romans 6—16. We need to see everything in Romans 6—16 in this light. If we reign in life, we are in all the matters presented in these chapters. We reign in life in sanctification, in renewing, in transformation, and in conformation to the image of Christ, and when we reign in life, we are in the process of glorification. Reigning in life equals the full experience of God's organic salvation. When we reign in life we are in all the organic processes of being saved in His life. When we are reigning in life, we overcome all of our environmental circumstances, and we are in the actual, practical reality of living a grafted life with Christ.
In Experience, to Reign in Life Meaning to Be under the Ruling of the Divine Life
To reign in life does not mean that we rule over our spouse or our roommate. To reign in life is to reign over Satan, sin, and death, and in experience, this is to be under the ruling of the divine life. The Lord Jesus Himself is a wonderful pattern of this kind of living. Christ is a pattern of reigning in life by being under the ruling of the divine life of the Father. Everything He did was under the ruling of the divine life of the Father within Him. He rejected His human life and lived by the divine life of the Father. All of His work was under the restriction, limitation, and control of the Father's divine life. In Matthew 8:5-13 a centurion came to the Lord, beseeching Him concerning his paralyzed servant. He said, "Speak a word, and my servant will be healed. For I also am a man under authority, having soldiers under me. And I say to this one, Go, and he goes; and to another, Come, and he comes; and to my slave, Do this, and he does it" (vv. 8b-9). What a revelation he had concerning the Lord's authority! It was so great a revelation that the Lord marveled and said, "Truly I say to you, With no one in Israel have I found such great faith" (v. 10). What kind of man was Jesus? He was a man under authority. He was One under the ruling of the divine life of the Father, and because He was under the ruling of the divine life, He was reigning in life.
Isaiah 11:2, speaking of Christ in His human living, says, "And the Spirit of Jehovah will rest upon Him, / The Spirit of wisdom and understanding, / The Spirit of counsel and might, / The Spirit of knowledge and the fear of Jehovah." Christ was filled with the Spirit of the fear of Jehovah. No human being ever feared God as much as Jesus did. This means that the Lord in His humanity had such a reverence, respect, regard, and awe of the Father that He did everything under the rule and control of the divine life of the Father within Him, desiring to not offend the Father in any way. This is why everything He did pleased the Father. He was a man one hundred percent under the ruling of the divine life, and we need to be the same.
Paul is an example of one who, in his life and ministry, was under the ruling of the divine life (2 Cor. 2:12-14). Paul was in Christ's triumphal procession as a captive of Christ. When he came to Troas for the gospel of Christ and a door was open to him in the Lord, he had no rest in his spirit. This shows that he was dominated, governed, directed, led, and moved by his mingled spirit, which had become zoe, the divine life itself. He was under the ruling of the life within him. We need to be the same.
There is the need for all the believers who have received the abundance of grace and of the gift of righteousness to practice the restriction and limitation in the divine life. May the Lord as the sevenfold intensified Spirit bring us into this practice in a sevenfold intensified way, that we may be under the ruling of the divine life to reign in life in this age, reign with Him for a thousand years as His bride, and ultimately bring in the eternal age, where we will reign forever and ever as the wife of Christ.
The Issue of Our Reigning in Life Being the Real and Practical Body Life
The issue of our reigning in life, living under the ruling of the divine life, is the real and practical Body life expressed in the church life.
Each Item of the Living of the Body Life in Romans 12—13 Requiring Us to Be Ruled by the Divine Life
Each item of the living of the Body life in Romans 12—13 requires us to be ruled by the divine life. We cannot live the Body life if we are not under the ruling of the divine life. We need to be captivated by the compassions of God (12:1a). We must present our bodies a living sacrifice (v. lb). We should not be fashioned according to this age but be transformed by the renewing of the mind (v. 2). We should not think more highly of ourselves than we ought to think, but think so as to be sober-minded, as God has apportioned to each a measure of faith (v. 3). Such a thinking is the result of our reigning in life. To be sober-minded is to have the realization of the proper order in the Body. The root of the recent rebellion in the Lord's recovery was a thinking that was not sober-minded. If one thinks that he has a greater measure of faith than the one raised up by God for His ministry, he is not sober-minded. This is to think more highly of oneself than he ought to think. We are happy to see that the graduates of the full-time training have the feeling that they are nothing, can do nothing, and have nothing, that they are big "zeros" who need Christ to be everything to them. It would be terrible if they came out of the training thinking that they are wonderful and glorious, the "supermen" who will save the church in their locality. A certain book among the unbelievers teaches people that everyone is "okay." This thought is not sober-minded. When we are saved and come into the church life, we find that no one is okay. The only One who is "okay" is the One who is life in our spirit. When we are being ruled by the divine life, we also should consider that we have many members in one body, and all the members do not have the same function (v. 4).
Needing to Live a Life of the Highest Virtues for the Body Reigning in Life
We need to live a life ot the highest virtues for the Body life by reigning in life. We should love without hypocrisy and love one another warmly in brotherly love (12:9a, 10a). When we are reigning in life, we love one another. We even vie with one another for showing honor to one another. To love and honor in this way is to reign in life. We should not be slothful in zeal but burning in spirit, serving the Lord (v. 11). We should endure in tribulation (v. 12b). We should rejoice with those who rejoice, and weep with those who weep (v. 15). If possible, as far as it depends on us, we should live in peace with all men (v. 18). All these are characteristics of those who are reigning in life.
Reigning in Life Being "unto Eternal Life"
Reigning in life is "unto eternal life." Romans 5:21 says that grace reigns through righteousness "unto eternal life." Unto eternal life is a particular expression. John 4:14b says, "The water that I will give him will become in him a spring of water gushing up into eternal life." Into {unto in Romans 5:21) speaks of destination and also means "to become" or "to be." The eternal life eventually will be the New Jerusalem. Therefore, into eternal life means into the New Jerusalem. The New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine life, the totality of the life of God. John 4:14b encapsulates the entire New Testament economy of God: The Father is the fountain, the Son is the spring, the Spirit is the river, this Spirit is flowing into eternal life, and the totality of the eternal life is the New Jerusalem.
The issue and goal of our reigning in life is the New Jerusalem, the universal incorporation of the union and mingling of divinity with humanity. When we reign in life with grace over all things, we become zoe, the eternal life; that is, we become God in life but not in His Godhead. The totality of zoe is the New Jerusalem, the city of zoe. This is the destination of our reigning in life. We reign in life with grace over all things with the view of the destination of the New Jerusalem, which is the totality of the eternal life. We are becoming the New Jerusalem by reigning in life.—E. M.

TOP-纲目|Outline|对照-目录
　
　
第九篇　神完整的救恩─法理的救赎加上生机的拯救
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　神完整的救恩有法理和生机的两面：
一　神法理的救赎是神完整救恩法理的一面：
１　是照着神的公义─罗一17上，三21～26，九30～31。
２　是神借着基督在十字架上救赎的死，满足了神公义的律法在罪人身上一切的要求─加三13，彼前二24，林后五21，来九12。
３　是在肉体里的基督，在祂地上职事物质的范围里所完成的。
４　结果在客观方面使神：
a　赦免信徒的罪─路二四47，弗一7。
b　洗净信徒的罪─来一3。
c　称义信徒─罗三24～25。
d　叫原是神仇敌的信徒与祂自己和好─罗五10上。
e　叫信徒在地位上成为圣别归祂自己，作祂圣别的子民─林前一2，来十三12，十29。
f　使信徒够资格并有地位进入神的恩典中，以完成神救恩的目的。
５　神法理的救赎是神完整救恩的手续，使信徒有分于神生机的拯救，这是神完整救恩的目的─罗五21。
二　神生机的拯救是神完整救恩生机的一面：
１　是借着神的生命─罗一17下，徒十一18，罗五10下，17下，18下，21下。
２　是神救恩的目的，借着神的神圣生命，完成神在祂经纶中，在信徒身上所要达到的一切目的。
３　结果在主观一面使信徒得着重生、喂养、圣化、更新、变化、建造、模成和荣化。
４　神生机拯救里的一切项目，不是在法理和客观一面由在肉体里的基督在祂地上的职事里完成的，乃是在生机和主观一面由基督这赐生命的灵在祂天上的职事里完成的。
贰　神生机的拯救：
一　重生是神圣生命的繁生：
１　重生乃是神整个救恩的中心，也是神的救恩在生机方面的开始。
２　重生乃是神的灵在蒙救赎之信徒的灵里，把他们重生再造─约三6下。
３　重生乃是借着基督的复活，使祂将神圣的生命分赐到他们里面作权柄，叫他们成为神亲生的儿女，作祂的种类─彼前一3，约一12～13。
４　信徒借着重生，在他们天然、属人的生命之外，得着神永远、神圣的生命─约三15，36。
二　牧养中的喂养，是神圣生命的滋养：
１　喂养是重生的延续，借着基督的保养和顾惜而牧养祂的群羊，使祂的羊在神圣生命上得以长大成熟─弗五29，约十10～11，14～16，二一15～17，来十三20，彼前五4，二25。
２　喂养使才生的婴孩（初信者）得着滋养，好叫他们借着神话中之奶的供应，渐渐长大得救─彼前二2。
３　喂养乃是用那是生命之灵的固体的话，供应长大的信徒─来五14，六63。
４　喂养的结果是信徒在神圣生命上成熟，而得着变化，并模成基督的形像─林后三18，罗十二2，八29。
５　喂养也是借着信徒相互的牧养，好建造基督的身体，为着完成神永远的经纶，达到神永远的定旨─弗四11～16，约二一15～17，彼前五2～3。
三　圣化是用神的神圣性情构成信徒：
１　圣化乃是信徒内在的圣别，他们借着圣灵，就是生命的灵在他们性情里的工作，而在神圣生命上长大─罗十五16，八2。
２　信徒被神的神圣、圣别性情所圣化，使他们成圣归神，为要成就神拣选他们的目的─彼后一4，弗一4。
３　圣化含有变化的作用─罗六19，22。
４　圣别要终极的显在新耶路撒冷身上，使其成为圣城─启二一2，10，二二19。
四　更新是神新造的过程：
１　信徒被圣灵圣化时，自然就得到在属灵生命上的更新─林后五17。
２　更新乃是重生之洗涤的继续，（多三5，）也是基于一直在进行的圣别过程，使信徒成为新的。─引用经文
３　更新的完成：
a　借着更新的灵调着由基督内住之信徒重生的灵而成为一灵，扩展到信徒的心思里，以更新他们全人，使他们作新人的肢体─多三5，弗四23。
b　借着信徒在复活里，在生命的新样中生活行动─罗六4，弗四22～24，腓一19～21。
４　更新是借着信徒受环境中苦难的销毁─林后四16。
５　信徒必须彻底而完全的得更新，使他们能实际的成为属于神、并为着神的真正新造─加六15。
６　更新使信徒成为新的，像新耶路撒冷一样─启二一2。
五　变化是在神圣生命中新陈代谢的作用：
１　这个作用使信徒全人被变化，开始于心思的更新，使他们完全有分于神的神性─罗十二2下。
２　变化不是任何一种外面的改正或调整，乃是一种新陈代谢的作用，借着将基督神圣生命的元素加到他们里面，而在外面彰显出基督的形像。
３　变化是由主灵（是灵的基督）所完成，将信徒变化成为基督荣耀的形像─林后三18。
４　信徒应当凭着灵活着、凭着灵而行，（加五16，25，）并照着调和的灵而行，（罗八4下，）使基督神圣的生命有路规律他们，并将他们变化成为主荣耀的形像。─引用经文
六　建造是在神圣生命中联络在一起，并结合在一起：
１　神的建造是借着变化的灵在信徒身上所作的工，联络并结合在一起而产生的─弗四16。
２　建造是信徒在一切事上长到元首基督里面的结果─弗四15。
３　这乃是建造基督的身体，以终极完成圣城新耶路撒冷的建造─弗四16，启三12，二一10～11。
七　模成是在神圣生命中成熟：
１　模成是信徒在神圣生命中得着重生、喂养、圣化，更新和变化的完成─罗八29。
２　模成是信徒借着他们灵里那使人成熟的灵，在神圣的生命上成熟，成为长成的人，达到基督丰满之身材的度量─西一28，弗四13。
３　模成乃是被模成神长子的形像─腓三10，一19～21上，约壹三2。
八　荣化是神完整救恩的完满彰显：
１　在重生时，神用祂的灵印涂重生的信徒，直到他们得赎的日子─弗一13，四30。
２　成熟的信徒要借着一生被神的荣耀浸透而从里面得荣耀，也要借着被带进神的荣耀而从外面得荣耀─弗四30，帖后一9，罗八23，30，来二10。
３　成熟信徒的得荣，乃是他们在神生机救恩里神圣儿子名分的最高之分；这儿子名分是他们重生时所得着的─加四5，罗八23。
４　信徒身体的得赎，乃是他们的身体在主回来时改变形状─腓三20～21。
５　借着荣化，神完成并实现了祂永远的定旨，就是新耶路撒冷─经过过程并终极完成的三一神，与祂重生、变化、模成、得荣的三部分选民，联结并调和的结晶。
参读　神救恩生机的一面；神生机救恩的秘诀─“那灵自己同我们的灵”。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message Nine
God's Complete Salvation— Judicial Redemption plus Organic Salvation
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　God's complete salvation is of two aspects—the judicial aspect and the organic aspect:
A.　God's judicial redemption is the judicial aspect of God's complete salvation:
1.　It is according to the righteousness of God—Rom. 1:17a; 3:21-26; 9:30-31.
2.　It is through God's fulfilling of all the requirements of His righteous law on sinners by Christ's redemptive death on the cross—Gal. 3:13; 1 Pet. 2:24; 2 Cor. 5:21; Heb. 9:12.
3.　It was accomplished in the physical realm of Christ's earthly ministry by the Christ in the flesh.
4.　It results objectively in God's:
a.　Forgiveness of the believers' sins—Luke 24:47; Eph. 1:7.
b.　Washing away the believers' sins—Heb. 1:3.
c.　Justifying the believers—Rom. 3:24-25.
d.　Reconciling the believers who were His enemies to Himself—Rom. 5:10a.
e.　Sanctifying the believers in their position unto Himself as His holy people—1 Cor. 1:2; Heb. 13:12; 10:29.
f.　Thereby qualifying and positioning the believers to enter into the grace of God for the accomplishment of the purpose of God's salvation.
5.　God's judicial redemption is the procedure of God's complete salvation for the believers to participate in God's organic salvation as the purpose of the complete salvation of God—Rom. 5:21.
B.　God's organic salvation is the organic aspect of God's complete salvation:
1.　It is through the life of God—Rom. 1:17b; Acts 11:18; Rom. 5:10b, 17b, 18b, 21b.
2.　As the purpose of God's salvation, it accomplishes all that God wants to achieve in the believers in His economy through His divine life.
3.　It results subjectively in the believers' regeneration, feeding, dispositional sanctification, renewing, transformation, building up, conformation, and glorification.
4.　All of the items of God's organic salvation are carried out not by the Christ in the flesh in His earthly ministry judicially and objectively but by the Christ as the life-giving Spirit in His heavenly ministry organically and subjectively.
II.　God's organic salvation:
A.　Regeneration is the propagation of the divine life:
1.　Regeneration is the center of God's entire salvation and the commencement of God's salvation in its organic aspect.
2.　It is to regenerate and re-create the redeemed believers in their spirit by the Spirit of God—John 3:6b.
3.　It is through the resurrection of Christ that He may impart His life into them as the authority for them to be the children of God, begotten of God as His species—1 Pet. 1:3; John 1:12-13.
4.　Through regeneration the believers have the eternal, divine life of God in addition to their natural, human life—John 3:15, 36.
B.　Feeding in shepherding is the nourishment of the divine life:
1.　Feeding is the continuation of regeneration through Christ's shepherding His flock by nourishing and cherishing that His sheep may grow in the divine life unto maturity—Eph. 5:29; John 10:10-11, 14-16; 21:15-17; Heb. 13:20; 1 Pet. 5:4; 2:25.
2.　Feeding nourishes His newborn babes (new believers) that they may grow and be saved gradually through the supply of the milk in the word of God—1 Pet. 2:2.
3.　Feeding supplies His growing believers with the solid word, which is the Spirit of life—Heb. 5:14; John 6:63.
4.　Feeding results in the believers' maturity in the divine life unto transformation and conformation to the image of Christ—2 Cor. 3:18; Rom. 12:2; 8:29.
5.　Feeding is also by the believers through the mutual shepherding for the building up of the Body of Christ for the accomplishment of God's eternal economy and the achievement of God's eternal purpose—Eph. 4:11-16; John 21:15-17; 1 Pet. 5:2-3.
C.　Dispositional sanctification constitutes the believers with God's divine nature:
1.　It is an inward sanctifying of the believers who are growing in the divine life by the working of the Holy Spirit, the Spirit of life, in their disposition—Rom. 15:16; 8:2.
2.　The believers are sanctified with the divine, holy nature of God for them to be holy unto God and thus fulfill God's purpose in choosing us—2 Pet. 1:4; Eph. 1:4.
3.　Dispositional sanctification implies transformation—Rom. 6:19, 22.
4.　Sanctification will ultimately be manifested in the New Jerusalem as the holy city—Rev. 21:2, 10; 22:19.
D.　Renewing is the process of God's new creation:
1.　The believers are spontaneously renewed in their spiritual life when they are sanctified by the Holy Spirit—2 Cor. 5:17.
2.　Renewing is the continuation of the washing of regeneration (Titus 3:5) and is based upon the ongoing process of sanctification, making the believers new.
3.　It is carried out:
a.　By the renewing Spirit mingling with the believers' regenerated spirit indwelt by Christ as one spirit to spread into the believers' mind to renew their entire being as a member of the new man—Titus 3:5; Eph. 4:23.
b.　By the believers' walking in the newness of life in resurrection—Rom. 6:4; Eph. 4:22-24; Phil. 1:19-21.
4.　It is through the consuming by the believers' environmental sufferings—2 Cor. 4:16.
5.　The believers must be thoroughly and absolutely renewed that they may be practically the genuine new creation of God and for God—Gal. 6:15.
6.　Renewing causes the believers to be new as the New Jerusalem—Rev. 21:2.
E.　Transformation is the metabolic process in the divine life:
1.　This process transforms the believers' entire being, beginning from the renewing of the mind, that they may fully participate in God's divinity—Rom. 12:2b.
2.　It is not any kind of outward correction or adjustment but a kind of metabolism, by the addition of the element of the divine life of Christ into their being, to be expressed outwardly in the image of Christ.
3.　It is accomplished by the Lord Spirit (the pneumatic Christ) transforming the believers into the image of the glory of Christ—2 Cor. 3:18.
4.　The believers should live and walk by the Spirit (Gal. 5:16, 25) and walk according to the mingled spirit (Rom. 8:4b), that the divine life of Christ may have the way to regulate them and transform them into the image of the Lord in glory.
F.　Building up is the joining and knitting together in the divine life:
1.　God's building is brought forth through the joining and knitting together by the working of the transforming Spirit on the believers—Eph. 4:16.
2.　It is the issue of the believers' growing into the Head, Christ, in all things—Eph. 4:15.
3.　This is the building up of the Body of Christ to consummate the building of the holy city, New Jerusalem—Eph. 4:16; Rev. 3:12; 21:10-11.
G.　Conformation is the maturity in the divine life:
1.　Conformation is the consummation of the believers' regeneration, feeding, sanctification, renewing, and transformation in the divine life—Rom. 8:29.
2.　Conformation is when the believers have matured in the divine life by the maturing Spirit in their spirit to be a full-grown man, at the measure of the stature of the fullness of Christ—Col. 1:28; Eph. 4:13.
3.　Conformation is to be conformed to the image of God's firstborn Son—Phil. 3:10; 1:19-21a; 1 John 3:2.
H.　Glorification is the full manifestation of God's complete salvation:
1.　In regeneration God seals the regenerated believers with His Spirit unto the day of redemption—Eph. 1:13; 4:30.
2.　The matured believers will be glorified from within through the lifelong saturation with the glory of God and from without through their being brought into God's glory—Eph. 4:30; 2 Thes. 1:10; Rom. 8:23, 30; Heb. 2:10.
3.　The glorification of the matured believers is the top portion of their divine sonship in God's organic salvation, which they received at the time of their regeneration—Gal. 4:5; Rom. 8:23.
4.　The redemption of the believers' body is the transfiguration of their body at the Lord's coming back—Phil. 3:20-21.
5.　Through glorification God realizes the fulfillment of His eternal purpose—the New Jerusalem—the crystallization of the union and mingling of the processed and consummated Triune God with His regenerated, transformed, conformed, and glorified tripartite elect.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第九篇　神完整的救恩─法理的救赎加上生机的拯救
God's Complete Salvation— Judicial Redemption plus Organic Salvation
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
壹　神完整的救恩有法理和生机的两面：
I.　God's complete salvation is of two aspects—the judicial aspect and the organic aspect:
一　神法理的救赎是神完整救恩法理的一面：
A.　God's judicial redemption is the judicial aspect of God's complete salvation:
１　是照着神的公义─罗一17上，三21～26，九30～31。
1.　It is according to the righteousness of God—Rom. 1:17a; 3:21-26; 9:30-31.
２　是神借着基督在十字架上救赎的死，满足了神公义的律法在罪人身上一切的要求─加三13，彼前二24，林后五21，来九12。
2.　It is through God's fulfilling of all the requirements of His righteous law on sinners by Christ's redemptive death on the cross—Gal. 3:13; 1 Pet. 2:24; 2 Cor. 5:21; Heb. 9:12.
３　是在肉体里的基督，在祂地上职事物质的范围里所完成的。
3.　It was accomplished in the physical realm of Christ's earthly ministry by the Christ in the flesh.
４　结果在客观方面使神：
4.　It results objectively in God's:
a　赦免信徒的罪─路二四47，弗一7。
a.　Forgiveness of the believers' sins—Luke 24:47; Eph. 1:7.
b　洗净信徒的罪─来一3。
b.　Washing away the believers' sins—Heb. 1:3.
c　称义信徒─罗三24～25。
c.　Justifying the believers—Rom. 3:24-25.
d　叫原是神仇敌的信徒与祂自己和好─罗五10上。
d.　Reconciling the believers who were His enemies to Himself—Rom. 5:10a.
e　叫信徒在地位上成为圣别归祂自己，作祂圣别的子民─林前一2，来十三12，十29。
e.　Sanctifying the believers in their position unto Himself as His holy people—1 Cor. 1:2; Heb. 13:12; 10:29.
f　使信徒够资格并有地位进入神的恩典中，以完成神救恩的目的。
f.　Thereby qualifying and positioning the believers to enter into the grace of God for the accomplishment of the purpose of God's salvation.
５　神法理的救赎是神完整救恩的手续，使信徒有分于神生机的拯救，这是神完整救恩的目的─罗五21。
5.　God's judicial redemption is the procedure of God's complete salvation for the believers to participate in God's organic salvation as the purpose of the complete salvation of God—Rom. 5:21.
二　神生机的拯救是神完整救恩生机的一面：
B.　God's organic salvation is the organic aspect of God's complete salvation:
１　是借着神的生命─罗一17下，徒十一18，罗五10下，17下，18下，21下。
1.　It is through the life of God—Rom. 1:17b; Acts 11:18; Rom. 5:10b, 17b, 18b, 21b.
２　是神救恩的目的，借着神的神圣生命，完成神在祂经纶中，在信徒身上所要达到的一切目的。
2.　As the purpose of God's salvation, it accomplishes all that God wants to achieve in the believers in His economy through His divine life.
３　结果在主观一面使信徒得着重生、喂养、圣化、更新、变化、建造、模成和荣化。
3.　It results subjectively in the believers' regeneration, feeding, dispositional sanctification, renewing, transformation, building up, conformation, and glorification.
４　神生机拯救里的一切项目，不是在法理和客观一面由在肉体里的基督在祂地上的职事里完成的，乃是在生机和主观一面由基督这赐生命的灵在祂天上的职事里完成的。
4.　All of the items of God's organic salvation are carried out not by the Christ in the flesh in His earthly ministry judicially and objectively but by the Christ as the life-giving Spirit in His heavenly ministry organically and subjectively.
贰　神生机的拯救：
II.　God's organic salvation:
一　重生是神圣生命的繁生：
A.　Regeneration is the propagation of the divine life:
１　重生乃是神整个救恩的中心，也是神的救恩在生机方面的开始。
1.　Regeneration is the center of God's entire salvation and the commencement of God's salvation in its organic aspect.
２　重生乃是神的灵在蒙救赎之信徒的灵里，把他们重生再造─约三6下。
2.　It is to regenerate and re-create the redeemed believers in their spirit by the Spirit of God—John 3:6b.
３　重生乃是借着基督的复活，使祂将神圣的生命分赐到他们里面作权柄，叫他们成为神亲生的儿女，作祂的种类─彼前一3，约一12～13。
3.　It is through the resurrection of Christ that He may impart His life into them as the authority for them to be the children of God, begotten of God as His species—1 Pet. 1:3; John 1:12-13.
４　信徒借着重生，在他们天然、属人的生命之外，得着神永远、神圣的生命─约三15，36。
4.　Through regeneration the believers have the eternal, divine life of God in addition to their natural, human life—John 3:15, 36.
二　牧养中的喂养，是神圣生命的滋养：
B.　Feeding in shepherding is the nourishment of the divine life:
１　喂养是重生的延续，借着基督的保养和顾惜而牧养祂的群羊，使祂的羊在神圣生命上得以长大成熟─弗五29，约十10～11，14～16，二一15～17，来十三20，彼前五4，二25。
1.　Feeding is the continuation of regeneration through Christ's shepherding His flock by nourishing and cherishing that His sheep may grow in the divine life unto maturity—Eph. 5:29; John 10:10-11, 14-16; 21:15-17; Heb. 13:20; 1 Pet. 5:4; 2:25.
２　喂养使才生的婴孩（初信者）得着滋养，好叫他们借着神话中之奶的供应，渐渐长大得救─彼前二2。
2.　Feeding nourishes His newborn babes (new believers) that they may grow and be saved gradually through the supply of the milk in the word of God—1 Pet. 2:2.
３　喂养乃是用那是生命之灵的固体的话，供应长大的信徒─来五14，六63。
3.　Feeding supplies His growing believers with the solid word, which is the Spirit of life—Heb. 5:14; John 6:63.
４　喂养的结果是信徒在神圣生命上成熟，而得着变化，并模成基督的形像─林后三18，罗十二2，八29。
4.　Feeding results in the believers' maturity in the divine life unto transformation and conformation to the image of Christ—2 Cor. 3:18; Rom. 12:2; 8:29.
５　喂养也是借着信徒相互的牧养，好建造基督的身体，为着完成神永远的经纶，达到神永远的定旨─弗四11～16，约二一15～17，彼前五2～3。
5.　Feeding is also by the believers through the mutual shepherding for the building up of the Body of Christ for the accomplishment of God's eternal economy and the achievement of God's eternal purpose—Eph. 4:11-16; John 21:15-17; 1 Pet. 5:2-3.
三　圣化是用神的神圣性情构成信徒：
C.　Dispositional sanctification constitutes the believers with God's divine nature:
１　圣化乃是信徒内在的圣别，他们借着圣灵，就是生命的灵在他们性情里的工作，而在神圣生命上长大─罗十五16，八2。
1.　It is an inward sanctifying of the believers who are growing in the divine life by the working of the Holy Spirit, the Spirit of life, in their disposition—Rom. 15:16; 8:2.
２　信徒被神的神圣、圣别性情所圣化，使他们成圣归神，为要成就神拣选他们的目的─彼后一4，弗一4。
2.　The believers are sanctified with the divine, holy nature of God for them to be holy unto God and thus fulfill God's purpose in choosing us—2 Pet. 1:4; Eph. 1:4.
３　圣化含有变化的作用─罗六19，22。
3.　Dispositional sanctification implies transformation—Rom. 6:19, 22.
４　圣别要终极的显在新耶路撒冷身上，使其成为圣城─启二一2，10，二二19。
4.　Sanctification will ultimately be manifested in the New Jerusalem as the holy city—Rev. 21:2, 10; 22:19.
四　更新是神新造的过程：
D.　Renewing is the process of God's new creation:
１　信徒被圣灵圣化时，自然就得到在属灵生命上的更新─林后五17。
1.　The believers are spontaneously renewed in their spiritual life when they are sanctified by the Holy Spirit—2 Cor. 5:17.
２　更新乃是重生之洗涤的继续，（多三5，）也是基于一直在进行的圣别过程，使信徒成为新的。─引用经文
2.　Renewing is the continuation of the washing of regeneration (Titus 3:5) and is based upon the ongoing process of sanctification, making the believers new.
３　更新的完成：
3.　It is carried out:
a　借着更新的灵调着由基督内住之信徒重生的灵而成为一灵，扩展到信徒的心思里，以更新他们全人，使他们作新人的肢体─多三5，弗四23。
a.　By the renewing Spirit mingling with the believers' regenerated spirit indwelt by Christ as one spirit to spread into the believers' mind to renew their entire being as a member of the new man—Titus 3:5; Eph. 4:23.
b　借着信徒在复活里，在生命的新样中生活行动─罗六4，弗四22～24，腓一19～21。
b.　By the believers' walking in the newness of life in resurrection—Rom. 6:4; Eph. 4:22-24; Phil. 1:19-21.
４　更新是借着信徒受环境中苦难的销毁─林后四16。
4.　It is through the consuming by the believers' environmental sufferings—2 Cor. 4:16.
５　信徒必须彻底而完全的得更新，使他们能实际的成为属于神、并为着神的真正新造─加六15。
5.　The believers must be thoroughly and absolutely renewed that they may be practically the genuine new creation of God and for God—Gal. 6:15.
６　更新使信徒成为新的，像新耶路撒冷一样─启二一2。
6.　Renewing causes the believers to be new as the New Jerusalem—Rev. 21:2.
五　变化是在神圣生命中新陈代谢的作用：
E.　Transformation is the metabolic process in the divine life:
１　这个作用使信徒全人被变化，开始于心思的更新，使他们完全有分于神的神性─罗十二2下。
1.　This process transforms the believers' entire being, beginning from the renewing of the mind, that they may fully participate in God's divinity—Rom. 12:2b.
２　变化不是任何一种外面的改正或调整，乃是一种新陈代谢的作用，借着将基督神圣生命的元素加到他们里面，而在外面彰显出基督的形像。
2.　It is not any kind of outward correction or adjustment but a kind of metabolism, by the addition of the element of the divine life of Christ into their being, to be expressed outwardly in the image of Christ.
３　变化是由主灵（是灵的基督）所完成，将信徒变化成为基督荣耀的形像─林后三18。
3.　It is accomplished by the Lord Spirit (the pneumatic Christ) transforming the believers into the image of the glory of Christ—2 Cor. 3:18.
４　信徒应当凭着灵活着、凭着灵而行，（加五16，25，）并照着调和的灵而行，（罗八4下，）使基督神圣的生命有路规律他们，并将他们变化成为主荣耀的形像。─引用经文
4.　The believers should live and walk by the Spirit (Gal. 5:16, 25) and walk according to the mingled spirit (Rom. 8:4b), that the divine life of Christ may have the way to regulate them and transform them into the image of the Lord in glory.
六　建造是在神圣生命中联络在一起，并结合在一起：
F.　Building up is the joining and knitting together in the divine life:
１　神的建造是借着变化的灵在信徒身上所作的工，联络并结合在一起而产生的─弗四16。
1.　God's building is brought forth through the joining and knitting together by the working of the transforming Spirit on the believers—Eph. 4:16.
２　建造是信徒在一切事上长到元首基督里面的结果─弗四15。
2.　It is the issue of the believers' growing into the Head, Christ, in all things—Eph. 4:15.
３　这乃是建造基督的身体，以终极完成圣城新耶路撒冷的建造─弗四16，启三12，二一10～11。
3.　This is the building up of the Body of Christ to consummate the building of the holy city, New Jerusalem—Eph. 4:16; Rev. 3:12; 21:10-11.
七　模成是在神圣生命中成熟：
G.　Conformation is the maturity in the divine life:
１　模成是信徒在神圣生命中得着重生、喂养、圣化，更新和变化的完成─罗八29。
1.　Conformation is the consummation of the believers' regeneration, feeding, sanctification, renewing, and transformation in the divine life—Rom. 8:29.
２　模成是信徒借着他们灵里那使人成熟的灵，在神圣的生命上成熟，成为长成的人，达到基督丰满之身材的度量─西一28，弗四13。
2.　Conformation is when the believers have matured in the divine life by the maturing Spirit in their spirit to be a full-grown man, at the measure of the stature of the fullness of Christ—Col. 1:28; Eph. 4:13.
３　模成乃是被模成神长子的形像─腓三10，一19～21上，约壹三2。
3.　Conformation is to be conformed to the image of God's firstborn Son—Phil. 3:10; 1:19-21a; 1 John 3:2.
八　荣化是神完整救恩的完满彰显：
H.　Glorification is the full manifestation of God's complete salvation:
１　在重生时，神用祂的灵印涂重生的信徒，直到他们得赎的日子─弗一13，四30。
1.　In regeneration God seals the regenerated believers with His Spirit unto the day of redemption—Eph. 1:13; 4:30.
２　成熟的信徒要借着一生被神的荣耀浸透而从里面得荣耀，也要借着被带进神的荣耀而从外面得荣耀─弗四30，帖后一9，罗八23，30，来二10。
2.　The matured believers will be glorified from within through the lifelong saturation with the glory of God and from without through their being brought into God's glory—Eph. 4:30; 2 Thes. 1:10; Rom. 8:23, 30; Heb. 2:10.
３　成熟信徒的得荣，乃是他们在神生机救恩里神圣儿子名分的最高之分；这儿子名分是他们重生时所得着的─加四5，罗八23。
3.　The glorification of the matured believers is the top portion of their divine sonship in God's organic salvation, which they received at the time of their regeneration—Gal. 4:5; Rom. 8:23.
４　信徒身体的得赎，乃是他们的身体在主回来时改变形状─腓三20～21。
4.　The redemption of the believers' body is the transfiguration of their body at the Lord's coming back—Phil. 3:20-21.
５　借着荣化，神完成并实现了祂永远的定旨，就是新耶路撒冷─经过过程并终极完成的三一神，与祂重生、变化、模成、得荣的三部分选民，联结并调和的结晶。
5.　Through glorification God realizes the fulfillment of His eternal purpose—the New Jerusalem—the crystallization of the union and mingling of the processed and consummated Triune God with His regenerated, transformed, conformed, and glorified tripartite elect.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE NINE
GOD'S COMPLETE SALVATION-JUDICIAL REDEMPTION PLUS ORGANIC SALVATION
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
GOD'S COMPLETE SALVATION BEING OF TWO ASPECTS— THE JUDICIAL ASPECT AND THE ORGANIC ASPECT
God's complete salvation is judicial redemption plus organic salvation. It is of two aspects—the judicial aspect and the organic aspect. Judicial is related to law, whereas organic is related to life. The judicial aspect is the procedure; it is not the goal. The organic aspect is the goal. In order for us to understand the procedure and the goal, we have to see God's eternal purpose and God's eternal economy. Our God is a God of purpose. He has His heart's desire and good pleasure, which is to be one with man, to enter into him in order to gain a group of people to be His corporate expression and His counterpart, His bride and His wife. The way He accomplishes this purpose is by His economy. God's economy is His plan to dispense Himself into His chosen people as their life and everything to produce and build up the organic Body of Christ. To this end, God created man in His own image. We have illustrated this by a hand and a glove. A glove is created according to the image of the hand. The hand has one thumb and four fingers, so the glove also has one thumb and four fingers. Once we see a glove, we know how a hand looks. The purpose of the glove is for a hand to come into it. If the glove were created in any other image, it would be hard for the hand to come into it, but because the glove is created in the image of the hand, it is easy for the hand to get in. Once the hand gets in, the glove expresses the hand. If the glove beckons to someone, it is actually the hand beckoning; the glove is one with the hand because the hand has come into the glove and filled every part of it. Therefore, the glove is the full expression of the hand. This illustrates how God created man in His own image in order to enter into him.
Even if we human beings were not clear about God's purpose and economy, Satan still knows them very well. Therefore, very shortly after God created man according to His image, Satan came in to damage man, to make man fallen and to usurp him. This can be illustrated by throwing the glove into the garbage, where it becomes filthy; no one would want to put his hand into the glove at this point. Because God is righteous, holy, and glorious, He could not enter into man after man was usurped and damaged by Satan. If a glove became filthy, we might discard it and buy another one, but God would never do this with man. Nothing can distract Him from His eternal purpose. He has determined that He wants to gain a group of men, and He is going to do it. Therefore, instead of discarding man, He accomplished something to cleanse him so that He could come into him. Judicial redemption is the procedure of God's salvation, but it is not the purpose. The purpose, the goal, is for God to enter into man and fill him. The organic aspect is the goal; redemption is to make us clean so that God's life can enter into us.
God's Judicial Redemption Being the Judicial Aspect of God's Complete Salvation According to the Righteousness of God through Christ's Redemptive Death Which He Accomplished in His Earthly Ministry
God's judicial redemption is the judicial aspect of God's complete salvation. It is according to the righteousness of God (Rom. 1:17a; 3:21-26; 9:30-31), and it is through God's fulfilling of all the requirements of His righteous law on sinners by Christ's redemptive death on the cross (Gal. 3:13; 1 Pet. 2:24; 2 Cor. 5:21; Heb. 9:12). It was accomplished in the physical realm of Christ's earthly ministry by the Christ in the flesh. None of us can make ourselves clean for God to enter into us, so one day God Himself came to be a man, a God-man, Jesus Christ. He is the complete God and the perfect man. Before a person believes in the Lord Jesus Christ, Satan tries to make him think that Jesus is only a man and not God. One may say that Jesus is the most wonderful person in human history, that He is the greatest man, but as long as one does not say that Jesus is God, he cannot be saved. Once a person believes into Christ as the Son of God and receives Him, he is saved. At this point Satan may try his best to make the saved one think that Jesus is only God and not a man. However, Jesus Christ is the God-man. As the perfect man He lived a perfect human life, and He went to the cross to be crucified for our sake. Christ was crucified as a man; therefore, when He was judged, a man was judged. Since He did not commit any sin, He should not have been judged, but He bore our sins in His body. Only He could accomplish the work of redemption. Moreover, He is not only a perfect man; He is also the eternal God. Therefore, the redemption He accomplished for us is an eternal redemption. Because He is the God-man, He has accomplished the work of redemption, and He has put Satan to death. What a wonderful redemption He accomplished through His all-inclusive death!
The Objective Results of God's Judicial Redemption
God's judicial redemption has five objective results. The first is the forgiveness of the believers' sins (Luke 24:47; Eph. 1:7). Psalm 97:2 says that God's righteousness is the foundation of His throne. As the Ruler, the Administrator, of the whole universe, our God cannot be unrighteous, and He cannot do anything that is unrighteous. We may love our children in the way of spoiling them. We may say, "If you have done anything wrong, I still love you. Just go and do not worry about anything." God, however, cannot do things in that loose way. All that He has done, is doing, and will do is according to His righteousness. Therefore, He Himself came to be a man to die for our sins and thereby accomplish the work of redemption, causing the righteous requirements of God's law to be fully satisfied. Christ has borne the punishment, the judgment, for all our sins. Because of this, He can righteously forgive our sins.
The second objective result of judicial redemption is the washing away of the believers' sins. Hebrews 1:3 says that Christ, "having made purification of sins, sat down on the right hand of the Majesty on high." He not only forgives our sins; He also washes them away. In the Old Testament times, the sins of the people could only be covered. Therefore, the priests had to stand and offer the sin offerings every day. However, since our Lord Jesus is the God-man, the redemption He has accomplished is an eternal redemption. Because of this, He only had to offer Himself once, and then He sat down at the right hand of the Majesty on high. His washing away of our sins makes us as clean as if we had never sinned.
The third objective result of judicial redemption is the justification of the believers (Rom. 3:24-25). On the negative side, He has forgiven our sins and washed away our sins. On the positive side, He has justified us. Justification means that God approves us, not according to our standard but according to His own standard. To be approved according to God's standard is not based on what we have done. It is based on what Jesus Christ has done on the cross.
The fourth objective result of judicial redemption is the reconciling of the believers, who were God's enemies, to Himself (Rom. 5:10a). We were not only sinners; we were also enemies of God. The forgiveness and washing away of sins is for sinners. It does not deal with the problem of being an enemy. For this, Christ reconciled us back to God, bringing the two parties who were in conflict into harmony.
The fifth objective result of judicial redemption is the sanctifying of the believers in their position unto God as His holy people (Heb. 13:12; 10:29). First Corinthians 1:2 says, "To the church of God which is in Corinth, to those who have been sanctified in Christ Jesus, the called saints." When we read this verse, we may be puzzled, wondering whether the believers in Corinth were sanctified. The church in Corinth had all kinds of problems. They had gross sins, divisions, disputes, and other problems. However, the sanctification mentioned in this verse refers to positional sanctification, not dispositional sanctification.
In Christ's judicial redemption we see these five wonderful objective results. All these results are necessary, good, and very important, but they are all part of the procedure. Therefore, Romans 5:10 says, "For if we, being enemies, were reconciled to God through the death of His Son, much more we will be saved in His life, having been reconciled." Were reconciled means that we received judicial redemption when we believed in the Lord Jesus Christ, while much more indicates that the resulting forgiveness, washing away of sins, justification, reconciliation, and the change in our position by being separated from the world are not the end. They are only the procedure. We still need to be saved in His life.
We may illustrate judicial redemption in this way. If a man owes someone a very large sum of money and is unable to repay it, he can righteously be brought before a judge. According to the law, the debtor should be put in prison. However, if the judge loves the debtor and he is rich, he can choose to pay the debt for him. Once the judge pays the debt, the debtor no longer owes anything. This is the meaning of what Christ accomplished on the cross. The cross is the "crossroad" of God's righteousness and His love. According to God's righteousness, He has to judge and punish us, but according to His love, He does not want to punish us. Therefore, He Himself came to be a man and die for us to pay our debt for us. The result is that the righteous requirement of the law has been satisfied, and we are judicially redeemed.
Judicial redemption, however, is not sufficient for the accomplishment of God's purpose. When Christ died for us, He cleared our debt outwardly, but that did not change our being inwardly. The debtor in the foregoing illustration may be an uneducated person, having no way to make a living. Once his debt is paid, he will still have to borrow money in order to live. If the judge really loves the man, he should not only pay his debt; he also should do something to change the man's being. What God wants is that we would be like Him. This is accomplished by His entering into us to be our life and everything to us. He does not want to teach or improve us in an outward way. Rather, God's economy is to dispense Himself into His chosen people as their life and everything to produce and build up the organic Body of Christ. Therefore, after judicial redemption, the judicial aspect of God's full salvation, we still need organic salvation. God's judicial redemption qualifies and positions the believers to enter into the grace of God for the accomplishment of the purpose of God's salvation. It is the procedure of God's complete salvation for the believers to participate in God's organic salvation as the purpose of the complete salvation of God (Rom. 5:21).
God's Organic Salvation Being the Organic Aspect of God's Complete Salvation
God's organic salvation is the organic aspect of God's complete salvation. It is through the life of God (Rom. 1:17b; Acts 11:18; Rom. 5:10b, 17b, 18b, 21b). As the purpose of God's salvation, it accomplishes all that God wants to achieve in the believers in His economy through His divine life. It results subjectively in the believers' regeneration, feeding, dispositional sanctification, renewing, transformation, building up, conformation, and glorification. These eight steps are the processes that we pass through. The Triune God has already gone through His processes to become the consummated Spirit of the processed and consummated Triune God. Now we need to go through our processes. The processes we pass through are the organic aspect of God's salvation. All of the items of God's organic salvation are carried out not by the Christ in the flesh in His earthly ministry judicially and objectively but by the Christ as the life-giving Spirit in His heavenly ministry organically and subjectively.
GOD'S ORGANIC SALVATION
Regeneration—the Propagation of the Divine Life
The first step of God's organic salvation is regeneration as the propagation of the divine life. Regeneration is the center of God's entire salvation and the commencement of God's salvation in its organic aspect. It is to regenerate and re-create the redeemed believers in their spirit by the Spirit of God (John 3:6b). It is through the resurrection of Christ that He may impart His life into them as the authority for them to be the children of God, begotten of God as His species (1 Pet. 1:3; John 1:12-13). Through regeneration the believers have the eternal, divine life of God in addition to their natural, human life (3:15, 36).
Regeneration is not a matter of self-improvement. It is not according to the Chinese philosophical saying that "all things of yesterday are dead; today all things are born anew." Rather, regeneration is to receive a new life, the divine life, the life of God, in addition to our human life. We were all born once in the human life when we received the human life from our parents. In regeneration, we receive a new life, the divine life, into us. This is our second birth. It is not merely to be called; it is to be born again, to be born anew.
Regeneration makes us God-men. God came to be a man, so He was the first God-man. Now we human beings can receive the life of God to also be God-men. Our own human life is not sufficient; it is weak, corrupted, temporary, and it will die. We need to receive a wonderful, higher life. The divine life which we received is strong, holy, powerful, and eternal. However, we must realize that the eternal life which we receive in regeneration is the life that is in the Son of God and that is the Son of God. This divine life is a person, the Son of God Himself. The life we receive into us is not merely to help us, to supply power when we are weak, or to supply peace when we have no peace. It is true that we receive everything from Him, but we must also see that the eternal life we receive is the Son of God, the very God Himself. He is a person with a mind, emotion, and will, and He has come into us to be our Lord, our "Boss." We should not believe that once we receive the divine life through regeneration, we will have only happiness, peace, and rest. Rather, if our mind is not the same as His mind or if our emotion is not the same as His emotion, we will not have much peace within us. As we have seen, being saved in the eternal life equals reigning in life, and to reign in life is to live under the ruling of the divine life. We must not wait until we are more mature to reign in life. From the very beginning of our organic salvation, starting from regeneration, we must see that the One we have received into us as the divine life is a living person, the living God Himself, the Son of God, the pneumatic Christ. He comes into us with His mind, His emotion, and His will to be our Lord. To let Him really be our Lord is the beginning of our organic salvation. This is the process we pass through for our entire life. Life is the processed Triune God, God the Father in Christ Jesus as the Spirit, flowing into us. This life is a wonderful person to be our enjoyment, our everything, and our Lord.—B. C.
Feeding in Shepherding—the Nourishment of the Divine Life
Feeding in shepherding is the nourishment of the divine life. Feeding is the continuation of regeneration through Christ's shepherding His flock by nourishing and cherishing that His sheep may grow in the divine life unto maturity (Eph. 5:29; John 10:10-11, 14-16; 21:15-17; Heb. 13:20; 1 Pet. 5:4; 2:25). Feeding nourishes His newborn babes (new believers) that they may grow and be saved gradually through the supply of the milk in the word of God. First Peter 2:2 tells us that we grow unto salvation. We need to grow to be saved in our whole being. It is a sad situation that so many Christians do not grow after being regenerated. They remain spiritual babes waiting to go to heaven. This is not according to God's salvation. God's salvation is for us to grow. This is why the Spirit today is intensified sevenfold to intensify His organic salvation. The Triune God as the sevenfold, consummated, processed, all-inclusive, life-giving, compound Spirit, who is the all-inclusive Christ with humanity, divinity, and so many elements, is now growing and spreading in our being. Sometimes we only allow God to come into us partially. We must let Him come into every part of our being. We do not want to remain as babes. We must give Him more room.
Feeding supplies His growing believers with the solid word, which is the Spirit of life (Heb. 5:14; John 6:63), and feeding results in the believers' maturity in the divine life unto transformation and conformation to the image of Christ (2 Cor. 3:18; Rom. 12:2; 8:29). Feeding is also by the believers through the mutual shepherding for the building up of the Body of Christ for the accomplishment of God's eternal economy and the achievement of God's eternal purpose (Eph. 4:11-16; John 21:15-17; 1 Pet. 5:2-3).
God wants to save us to the extent that He makes us Himself. His organic salvation is the only way to make man God in life, in nature, and in expression. In Revelation 2—3 the Lord made a number of promises to the overcomers in the churches, such as the promises of the crown of life and of sitting with Him on His throne (2:10; 3:21). The greatest of these promises, however, is to Philadelphia: "He who overcomes, him I will make a pillar in the temple of My God" (v. 12a). This is the reward of being made something. We do not want to go to heaven with our fallen disposition, as some in Christianity teach that we will do. We want to become something; we want to change. We want to give the Lord the ground to invade our being. The sevenfold intensified life-giving Spirit is working to save us. When we were enemies, we were reconciled to God through the death of His Son, but much more we will be saved in His life so that we become like Him. We do not want to be ourselves forever. We all will be like Him, so in His recovery, we give Him the ground to change us.
Dispositional Sanctification—to Constitute the Believers with God's Divine Nature
We receive Christ as our life, but He also wants to invade our nature. Dispositional sanctification constitutes the believers with God's divine nature. No human disposition is right. Our disposition is fallen, crooked, distorted, and perverted. We need to be saved from our disposition, from what we are, by the saturation of God's very nature in our being. Brother Lee in The Experience and Growth in Life on pages 158-159 says,
The thing which most damages our usefulness in the Christian life and church life is our living according to our disposition. I have been in the Lord's work for many years, and I have found that some brothers and sisters have a strong element in their disposition which hinders them from coordinating and cooperating with others....Both the good and bad dispositions destroy our usefulness in the spiritual realm....How much the Lord can use you depends upon your capacity. But regardless of how much capacity you have, as long as you go along with your disposition, you are finished.
In the Body we need to coordinate and cooperate with others, but we can never do it in our disposition. We may say that our own disposition is good, but that of the other brothers is terrible. If we say this, we are finished. Living according to our disposition is the most damaging factor to our usefulness. Along with our disposition, we have our capacity, or ability. Being capable often leads us to have an opinion, and our opinion damages our growth in life. Therefore, the Lord must invade and take over our disposition. There is no way to deal with the disposition by man's hand alone, but in the Lord's hand, there is a way. When the disciples, who were brothers like us, heard the Lord's word, they said, "Who then can be saved?" (Matt. 19:25). The Lord responded, "With men this is impossible, but with God all things are possible" (v. 26).
Dispositional sanctification is an inward sanctifying of the believers who are growing in the divine life by the working of the Holy Spirit, the Spirit of life, in their disposition (Rom. 15:16; 8:2). The believers are sanctified with the divine, holy nature of God for them to be holy unto God and thus fulfill God's purpose in choosing them. Ephesians 1:4 says that God chose us to be holy before the foundation of the world, and 2 Peter 1:4 says that we are partakers of the divine nature. Every day we need to partake, to feed, on God's divine nature. Our nature can only be subdued and changed by God's divine nature mingling with us.
Dispositional sanctification implies transformation (Rom. 6:19, 22). Sanctification will ultimately be manifested in the New Jerusalem as the holy city (Rev. 21:2, 10; 22:19). The Lord wants to sanctify us to the degree that we become the holy city.
Renewing—the Process of God's New Creation
In His organic salvation, God not only sanctifies us by our partaking of His nature, but He also renews us. Renewing is the process of God's new creation. This new creation is something out of God's old creation, of which so many old things are renewed and become new. We may regard ourselves as quite good, but whether we are good or bad, we are of the old creation. Only God is new; we become the new creation when God is added to us. The believers are spontaneously renewed in their spiritual life when they are sanctified by the Holy Spirit (2 Cor. 5:17).
Renewing is the continuation of the washing of regeneration (Titus 3:5) and is based upon the ongoing process of sanctification, making the believers new.
