3.　We should be one with all the believers who are in the Lord's recovery throughout the world.
４　我们不该有任何信经，只该有一本用圣经本身并按圣经本身正确翻译并解释的独一圣经。
4.　We should not have any creed but only the unique Bible properly translated and interpreted by and according to the Bible itself.
５　我们该以神永远的经纶为中心线，作基督独一的见证，不教导任何与神永远的经纶无关、与基督的见证无分的道理─提前一3～4。
5.　We should take the eternal economy of God as the central line to bear the unique testimony of Christ, not teaching any doctrine that is unrelated to the eternal economy of God and has nothing to do with the testimony of Christ—1 Tim. 1:3-4.
６　我们该在一个灵里，同有一个魂，在一样的心思和一样的意见里，彼此和谐，而实行同心合意─太十八19，徒一14，腓一27，二2。
6.　We should practice the one accord by being in one spirit with one soul and by being attuned in the same mind and in the same opinion—Matt. 18:19; Acts 1:14; Phil. 1:27; 2:2.
７　我们该享受公义、和平、并圣灵中的喜乐，作神国的实际─罗十四17.
7.　We should enjoy righteousness, peace, and joy in the Holy Spirit as the reality of the kingdom of God—Rom. 14:17.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE ELEVEN
THE PRACTICE EXPRESSION OF THE CHURCH—THE BODY OF CHRIST EXPRESSED PRACTICALLY AS MANY LOCAL CHURCHES
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
In this message we will see the practical expression of the church. In the last chapter of The Divine and Mystical Realm, Brother Lee spoke concerning the unique ground of the local churches of God and the unique oneness of the universal Body of Christ. Before he spoke this message, he prayed the following, which is still applicable at this time:
Lord, how we thank You that You have brought us through all the previous fellowship. We believe You will give us a glorious conclusion. You are the Alpha and the Omega. We trust in You. Lord, thank You that all the time we depend upon Your mercy, Your blessing, Your provisions, the Word and Spirit, and Your presence. Lord, without these we are just like a dead dog. We can do nothing, we can have nothing, and we can be nothing. Lord, this is what we are. But we trust in You. You are everything to us for the purpose of making us the same as You are in life and in nature but not in Your Godhead. We thank You for this. We worship You. The main point in these days that You have unveiled to us is that You want to have a group of people to be remade through regeneration, sanctification, renewing, transformation, conformation, and glorification to be the same as You are. We thank You for Yourself. Amen.
The messages in the series, The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Ministry, began with the apostles' teaching concerning God's New Testament economy as the base for all the subsequent fellowship, and in the previous message we received a high view concerning the Body of Christ. On the occasion of Brother Lee's departure, we should consider all that the Lord has unveiled to us, all the truths which were recovered for us through our brothers faithful ministry, to bring us into the Lord's recovery and into the experience of Christ and the reality of the Body of Christ. As the Alpha and the Omega, the Lord has done so much in His recovery, and we believe that He will lead His recovery into a marvelous consummation. What our God has begun He will complete; He has brought us this far, and He will bring us all the way. Nothing can frustrate Him from His plan, His purpose, and His heart's desire.
THE CHURCH OF GOD BEING EXPRESSED PRACTICALLY AS MANY LOCAL CHURCHES WHICH EXPRESS THE ONE BODY OF CHRIST
The church of God, as the universal Body of Christ, the universal house of God, and the kingdom of God (Eph. 1:22-23; 1 Tim. 3:15-16; Matt. 16:18-19), is expressed practically as many local churches (Rev. 1:4a, 11), and all the local churches, being the one Body of Christ separated by localities for their existence, express the same one Body, not respectively but corporately. The phrase the church of God means that the church is of God; that is, the essence of the church is God. The notion that a church can be a church of certain persons is a fallen concept. The church is divine and spiritual; it is the church of God. We may illustrate this with the great wheel in Ezekiel 1, which signifies God's economy. Christ is the hub, the center of God's economy; the rim is the church, the Body of Christ, as the counterpart and enlargement of Christ the hub; and the spokes are all the believers of Christ. The church always comes out of Christ. Where there is no Christ, there is no church. This is the very nature and essence of the church.
The church is the universal Body of Christ. It is composed of all the members as the counterpart of Christ for His expression. It is also the house of God for His administration and rest. It is from His house that God administers His move, desire, and will. God has a way to move on the earth because He has the practical church. The church is also the kingdom of God for Him to fight and defeat Satan.
The church of God is expressed practically as many local churches. The practical expression of the church is crucial for the Lord's going on, and it is the base of the Lord's move in His recovery on the earth today. All the local churches are the one Body of Christ separated by localities for their existence, but they express the same one Body. Even if we strengthen and perfect the church in our locality to be full of the enjoyment of Christ, it cannot express the Body of Christ in full; no one church expresses the Body in totality. The local churches express the Body not respectively but corporately. The rim of the wheel comprises all the local churches on the earth. Even if all the members in a church are living, glorious, and wonderful, they are still only a portion of the great wheel of God's economy, and it is very difficult for only a portion of a wheel to turn. Therefore, we need to be for all the local churches. The local churches are the procedure for the expression of the Body of Christ, which is the complete rim of the wheel. To realize this should cause us to long for the blending of the Body. We cannot be only for our local church; we must be for all the local churches. It is not enough that our own locality be built up. We need to make sure that all the localities are built up, so we need much practical blending among the churches. This blending of the local churches will bring forth the reality of the Body of Christ.
THE GROUND OF THE CHURCH
Denoting the Site on Which the Foundation of the Church—Christ—Is Laid
The ground of the church denotes the site on which the foundation of the church (Christ—1 Cor. 3:11) is laid, which keeps, in practicality, the genuine oneness of the church both locally and universally, without any division or confusion. To lay any kind of foundation, we need a site. Once the site is gained, the foundation can be laid. The ground of the church is the site for the foundation of Christ to be laid for the building of the church.
According to the Divine Revelation of the New Testament, Being Constituted of Three Crucial Elements
We may have considered that the locality alone is the ground of the church, but according to the divine revelation of the New Testament, the church ground is constituted of three crucial elements. The first element is the unique oneness of the universal Body of Christ, that is, the oneness of the one Spirit as the unique essence of the Body, with the one Lord as the unique element of the Body, and with the one Father as the unique source of the Body (Eph. 4:4-6). The unique oneness of the universal Body of Christ is the oneness of the Triune God—the Spirit, the Lord, and the Father. The second element is the unique ground of locality of a local church, that is, the very locality—a city, a town, or a village—as the boundary within which a local church is established and exists, with each one locality having only one church in order to preserve the oneness and prevent division (Deut. 12:5-18). This is a crucial matter. Today we are enjoying the ministry of the New Testament, but we are enjoying it within the local churches. Some ministries are apart from any church, but the ministry of the New Testament is always in the context of the local churches. We all need to be in a practical local church on the local ground. Brother Lee testified that he loved being in the local church in Anaheim. The unique ground of locality is a marvelous preservation of the oneness of the Body of Christ. When a new believer is saved, he should gather with the Christians in the church where he lives. This seems so simple, but it is God's wisdom.
Today in a small town of two thousand people, half of them may be Christians, yet they may still have fifteen small churches of many different types. The believers in such cities do not meet together as the one expression in their city simply because the natural man wants to be distinct from others. God is one, and the element of the oneness of the Body of Christ is the oneness of God Himself. Moreover, He has a practical way to express this oneness, which is to have one church in one city. This is a marvelous way of practice for all the Christians in a locality, and it is also a real preservation for the fellowship among the believers all over the world. Today the Lord has raised up churches in so many cities, so wherever we go we know where to fellowship. It is wonderful to sing and fellowship with the dear saints in a local church in another country. To meet in this way is to practically express the Body of Christ through the many local churches.
According to the unique ground of locality, we see the church in Jerusalem, the church in Antioch, the church in Cenchrea, the church in Corinth, and the seven churches in Asia in seven respective cities (Acts 8:1; 13:1; Rom. 16:1; 1 Cor. 1:2; Rev. 1:4a, 11). The church must not be divided by different persons, doctrines, and practices as different grounds into sects and denominations (1 Cor. 1:10-13).
The third element of the ground of the church is the reality of the Spirit of oneness by whom the oneness of the Body of Christ becomes real and living and through whom the ground of locality is applied in life and not in legality (Eph. 4:3-6). Oneness is in the Spirit; we simply need to keep this oneness.
A Spiritual Fact and Practical Necessity
The church ground is therefore a spiritual fact and practical necessity, being the base of the genuine and proper fellowship of all the believers, the unique fellowship of the Body of Christ locally and universally (Acts 2:42; 1 John 1:1-3).
THE PRACTICE OF THE CHURCH
The Church of God Being the Called-out Assembly Composed of All His Children, Appearing in Many Localities on the Earth as the Local Churches
According to its practice, the church of God is the called-out assembly composed of all His children, appearing in many localities on the earth as the local churches. The local churches are for the Body of Christ, and the Body of Christ is expressed as the many local churches. If there are no local churches, there is no Body of Christ. The local churches today are the expression of the Body of Christ on the earth. This is a shame to the enemy and a glory to God.
The Body of Christ needs the local churches for its existence, expression, and practice. How can the Body exist if there are no local churches? The Body without the churches is a "phantom"; it has no expression without the local churches. The Body of Christ needs the local churches for its practice, and the local churches are the way to practice the Body of Christ in each locality. In the churches we can practice to call on the name of the Lord, to fellowship with the saints, and to be in a vital group. Wherever we go, we can practice the Body of Christ because the local church in each locality is so practical. The Body of Christ needs the local churches.
A local church is one that exists in a locality, its jurisdiction for its administration being within the boundary of the locality in which it exists. The administration of a local church is only within the boundary of a locality. The responsible brothers in a certain locality have no jurisdiction over the affairs in another locality. However, each local church should fellowship with the other local churches. Fellowship is universal, but administration is local.
The unique church of God is expressed as many local churches throughout the whole earth, yet they still express the same one universal Body of Christ, not respectively but corporately (1 Cor. 12:27). The Body of Christ is not expressed in totality in a single local church. Rather, it is expressed corporately as all the local churches on the earth. If someone is not clear about this, he should travel out of his locality and blend with the many churches all over the earth. Then the Lord will give him a vision to realize that the Body of Christ is expressed as the many local churches.
The local churches are scattered in different places by geography, yet they are not divided by any doctrine or any matter into sects or denominations (1 Cor. 1:10-13; 10:16-17). First Corinthians 1:10 says, "Now I beseech you, brothers, through the name of our Lord Jesus Christ, that you all speak the same thing and that there be no divisions among you, but that you be attuned in the same mind and in the same opinion." If we differ in doctrines and opinions, we will create a sect, a denomination, a division within the Body of Christ. We must be those who are diligent to be of the same mind and the same opinion. The local church is practical, but it is practical with a reality. In 1 Corinthians 10:17 Paul says, "Seeing that there is one bread, we who are many are one Body; for we all partake of the one bread." We are the one Body because we are partaking of the one bread, the one Christ. We all eat the same Christ, so we are the one Body of Christ expressed as the many local churches.
Among the local churches there is no head church, high church, or low church, but all the local churches are on the same level. There can be no absolute autonomy of any local church, nor can there be a federation among a group of churches. No local church should be absolutely autonomous, going on only according to the fellowship in that church. In the United States there are fifty states, yet it is one country with one federal government. Similarly, a church has a local aspect, yet it is (本段原稿多处污损，以省略号标识，下同）……absolutely local. All the churches should be open to one another……fellowship in all matters. There also should be no federal ……region…… or special grouping of churches. No churches in a region should be…… fined in their region, fellowshipping and going on only according…… churches in that region. Rather, we need to be open to the …… of Christ. We need to build up the Body in the same way through the whole wheel of God's move.—D. L.
All the Local Churches Being the Golden Lampstands, Which Are Identical in Nature, Shape, and Function to Be the One Expression of Christ
The sequence of the messages in this series is marvelous; it did not come from man but from God. The final two messages are on the local churches and the New Jerusalem. There is a great connection between these two. The local churches are the procedure, the bridge, and the New Jerusalem is the goal, the destination. We may tend to uplift the goal and belittle the procedure, saying that the procedure means nothing as long as we get to the goal. However, if we do not have the procedure, we will never get to the goal. We cannot attain to the New Jerusalem without the local churches. The local churches are the stepping stones to the New Jerusalem. The local churches with their practical expression are outward, but we may compare them to a physical body, which is needed to contain the unseen parts—the spirit and soul. All the wonderful matters that we have seen in these messages need a vessel to contain and express them. The apostles' teaching, the New Testament ministry, God's economy, the Triune God, the all-inclusive Christ, Christ's full ministry in three stages, the all-inclusive Spirit, the eternal life, God's complete salvation, and the Body of Christ are wonderful, tremendous matters, but they are found and experienced in the local churches. We must thank the Lord for the local churches and declare that we love the local churches. It is only the procedure, but in it we can enjoy all the divine riches of God.
All the local churches, composed with the believers to be the Body of Christ, are the golden lampstands, which are identical in nature, shape, and function to be the one expression of Christ (Rev. 1:11-12). The local churches are not merely the assemblies, the gathering places of Christians. This view of a local church is too low. The top view of a local church is that it is a golden lampstand. All the genuine churches on the earth must be golden lampstands; this is how they are revealed in the last book of the Bible, Revelation. A lampstand is something shining, something full of oil. The lampstand is just the expression of the Triune God—the Father, the Son, and the Spirit. Its gold signifies the nature of the Father, its shape signifies the Son, and its shining signifies the Spirit. Moreover, all the lampstands are identical in nature, shape, and function. We may have had the concept that the churches should be different, the more different the better, for the sake of variety, because we prefer things in variety. Some believe that we should make the churches different because the Body has all kinds of people. This is a corrupted concept. The more we are the same, the better it is. It is wonderful for someone to go to a foreign country, come into a meeting hall, meet the people there, and suddenly feel that he has been there before; what is there is identical to what he has seen before. We have the same God, the same Christ, the same teaching, the same expression, and to some extent, the same practice, not legally but organically. This divine sameness is a real shame to the enemy and a real glory to God. We should not feel that we are merely from our own locality. We must feel that we are in the New Jerusalem. We are one in the Lord, one in the Triune God, and we are the same in nature, shape, and function.
Although the local churches are autonomous to a certain extent in business affairs, their testimony for Christ and fellowship of the Spirit should be not only local but also universal. How each church arranges the chairs in their meetings is not important. The main thing is that we are in the same, one, universal fellowship. Hence, the local churches in certain districts should be clustered as much as possible in a blending way for the spiritual benefits in the mutual building up of the Body of Christ, as the Lord Jesus clustered the seven neighboring churches in Asia (Rev. 1—3). In these days, no church can survive without blending. Without blending we will wilt, wither, and die as a local church. We need the blending. In fact, we need at least seven times of blending a year, and the more the better. That is the purpose of jumbo jets, e-mail, and faxes. When video telephones are more available, we will blend together even more. We may be able to have morning revival with the brothers in Moscow. What a blending that would be! The days of making private fortifications and keeping national borders is over. No one should do this anymore. Technology has eliminated all kinds of borders, and the "borders" in the Lord's recovery are also disintegrating. Among us, there are no continents, nations, regions, or localities; there is only Christ. As our spiritual song says, "Blending, blending, hallelujah!"
Such a blending is not social but the blending of the very Christ whom the churches enjoy, experience, and partake of. Such clustering also stirs up the neighboring churches in mutual love, mutual care, mutual intercession, and mutual shepherding. This always happens when we come together. Sometimes a husband cannot stir up his wife, and a wife cannot stir up her husband, but when they visit the churches and see the saints, they are instantly stirred up. We should not remain where we are; we must go and blend. At this time a number of saints are going to Brazil to blend. There are hundreds of churches and thousands of saints to blend with there. We want to stir up one another with much mutuality; this is the real building up of one another.
Such blending is not an organization of any nature or a system in any way, nor is it a kind of unification in outward practices. We should never make the blending into a system or organization, and we should never care for unification in outward practices. Rather, the blending is an organic building work.
Being Administered by a Group of Elders and Ministered To by All the Gifted Saints for Its Building Up as a Living Testimony of Christ
A local church is administered by a group of elders appointed by the gifted persons who have established the church and is ministered to by all the gifted saints for its building up as a living testimony of Christ (Acts 14:14a, 23; 13:1). The administration of a local church under the leadership of the elders should be carried out in an organic way, not by any worldly, organizational way (1 Tim. 3:1-5; 5:17). No elder should sit behind a big desk, as on a throne, as the "chief executive officer." Many sisters want their husband to be an elder so that they can be the "First Lady." This is worldly and organizational. The elders should clothe themselves with humility to be slaves to the saints. May the Lord put down the thrones and raise up the slaves! Those who are slaves are qualified to be the elders.
Among the churches there are the apostles who set up the churches, and in every church there are the elders who manage the church and the deacons who serve the church. Although there is the order of these holy services, there should not be any hierarchy—religious organization or a system of rank (1 Cor. 9:1-3; 1 Tim. 3:1-13). Philippians 1:1 says, "Paul and Timothy, slaves of Christ Jesus, to all the saints in Christ Jesus who are in Philippi, with the overseers and deacons." As an orderly and beautiful church, the church in Philippi had elders and deacons and was ministered to by the apostles. The concept of hierarchy is altogether worldly and systematic. We do not care for this concept; we cast it into the lake of fire. We are here for the organic building up of the Body of Christ. There is the order in the Body, but it is not by assignment or election. It is by the organic growth in life and by the Head's tempering and placing the members in the Body as it pleases Him. We must learn to be delivered from all the things of Christianity, live in the Spirit by the divine life, and build up the Body of Christ in an organic way in the local churches.
A local church is built up directly by the functioning of all its members with the perfecting of the gifted persons, such as the apostles, prophets, evangelists, and shepherds and teachers (Eph. 4:11-12) through preaching the gospel to have sinners saved and regenerated to become the members of Christ, feeding the new believers for their growth in life and in truth (John 21:15, 17; 1 Thes. 2:7), perfecting the saints that they may mature and be built up (Eph. 4:12), and prophesying in the church meetings for the building up of the church (1 Cor. 14:1-5, 23-26, 31). These four matters are the God-ordained way to build up the church, as revealed in the apostles' teaching and unveiled to us through our brother's ministry, and this is what all the churches should practice. The above-mentioned God-ordained way to build up the church is best practiced in the vital groups day by day and from house to house (Acts 2:46; 5:42). Although the phrase vital group is not in the Bible, there is an abundance of examples and patterns in the New Testament of this organic practice for the building up of the Body.
The building up of a local church is for the building up of the entire Body of Christ. When we labor to build up the local church in our locality or the local churches in our area, we must have the consciousness deep within us that we are not merely building up something local or something in a district. When we build up a local church, we are in fact building up the Body of Christ. When we shepherd the churches in a region, we are shepherding a part of the Body of Christ. Our consciousness is not local, regional, or national. Our consciousness is of the entire Body of Christ. If we all have this feeling, we will eliminate the factors of division.
Some Crucial Practices in the Local Churches under Today's Divisive and Confusing Degradation of Christianity
Today the situation in Christianity is one of divisive and confusing degradation. This is still the environment we are living in, so we have to overcome the degradation. The last thing we have to overcome is not sin or the world; the last thing we have to overcome is degraded Christianity, and this is what we are endeavoring to do in the local churches. The following points are some crucial practices in the local churches under such a situation.
We should not participate in the Catholic heresy, the Protestant denominations, or any kind of free group of Christians. We should recognize and receive the individual believers in Christ who believe in the Lord Jesus Christ, having been redeemed by His blood and regenerated by the Holy Spirit, who are not factious, not making divisions, not worshipping idols, nor living in sin, even if they are still related to any of the above-listed divisions (Rom. 14:1—15:13; Titus 3:10; Rom. 16:17; 1 Cor. 5:11). This is according to the teaching of the apostles. The Speciality, Generality, and Practicality of the Church is helpful in these matters, especially concerning Romans 14.
Moreover, we should be one with all the believers who are in the Lord's recovery throughout the world. It is easy to read this message, but when it comes to practice, we must exercise much. We may think that we are always lovable, whether or not others realize it, and that the problems are always with others. Many believers may not seem lovable to us, so we may only love ourselves and a few others. The indication that we do not love someone is that it is easy for us to say something negative about them. We must exercise with the love of God to love every member in the Lord's recovery, especially those who are less comely, those who seem unlovable. To love in this way is the Lord's heart. Love is crucial in our practice of the local church life. It is not knowledge, gift, power, or so many other things that build up the church. Rather, it is love that builds up. Love is the very inner substance of God Himself. Therefore, we need to enjoy God and be constituted and permeated with Him to express Him and flow Him out, and this expression is love. We need love to build up the local churches.
We also should not have any creed; rather, we have only the unique Bible properly translated and interpreted by and according to the Bible itself. In the Lord's recovery we do not have creeds. If there is a "creed" among us, it is the apostles' teaching, which actually is not a creed. The proper translation and interpretation of the Bible is what we have been receiving all these years from our dear Brother Lee.
We should take the eternal economy of God as the central line to bear the unique testimony of Christ, not teaching any doctrine that is unrelated to the eternal economy of God and has nothing to do with the testimony of Christ (1 Tim. 1:3-4). By the Lord's mercy, we must hold to God's economy as our central lane, never going off on a tangent and never swerving or deviating.
We should practice the one accord by being in one spirit with one soul and by being attuned in the same mind and in the same opinion (Matt. 18:19; Acts 1:14; Phil. 1:27; 2:2). The one accord is the unique factor of God's blessing, so we must keep it in one spirit with one soul all the time. Furthermore, we should enjoy righteousness, peace, and joy in the Holy Spirit as the reality of the kingdom of God (Rom. 14:17). This is the reality of the church life and the reality of the kingdom in the local church today.
A WORD OF FELLOWSHIP CONCERNING OUR ULTIMATE RESPONSIBILITY
In light of what we have seen in these messages, and in light of Brother Lee's departure to be with the Lord, we should have much reflection and consideration concerning where we are, who we are, and where we are going. We have the ultimate vision of God's desire, the high peak of the divine revelation: God became man that man may become God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead to gain the eternal divine and human incorporation. Along with this ultimate vision, we need to have the ultimate living, which is the God-man mingling living, a living in the spirit, a living in resurrection under the cross. There is no living higher than this living; it is the heritage that our brother has left us, and it is what the Lord desires. We also have the ultimate salvation. The complete salvation of God, especially the organic aspect, is to save us to the ultimate degree, to deify us by bringing us from regeneration all the way to glorification. This is His process in us by which He saves us to the uttermost. Moreover, we have the ultimate goal: the New Jerusalem. This has been made crystal-clear to us.
Along with the ultimate vision, ultimate living, ultimate salvation, and ultimate goal, we all have the ultimate responsibility. The ultimate responsibility is to carry out all these foregoing matters for the increase and spread of the Lord's testimony throughout the whole earth. This is our ultimate responsibility, the fulfillment of which will consummate this age and bring the Lord Jesus back. It is only appropriate that after seeing all these items, we have a consecration and prayer before the Lord with a deep sense of the ultimate responsibility to carry out His divine economy to consummate this age. We, especially the young people among us, should read The World Situation and God's Move, from messages spoken in 1981, and The World Situation and the Direction of the Lord's Move, from messages given in 1991 concerning Brother Lee's burden for the move to Russia. We must see the finality of the world situation today. Some people believe that the world will end in an instant. The Lord's coming back to the earth is not only His open appearing in an instant; it is also through His parousia, His coming over a certain period of time in a hidden way. In the same way, the end of this age is not sudden; it is something which takes place over a period of time. It is a stage in which this age draws to a close. We should have the deep impression that we are living in that stage. We are at the end time. We can say this not only from the standpoint of prophecy but by looking at two things. The first is what the Lord has done in His recovery. Eyes have not seen and hearts have never dreamed of the marvelous things that have been shown to us. The angels desire to see what we have seen. There should be praise in our heart and worship in our being about this. This is a strong proof that we are in the ultimate times. The second matter is the world situation with all its wars and centuries of history. This century alone has seen the restoration of the nation of Israel and the return of Jerusalem. Communism has fallen, and the world situation today has shifted. This also points to the end times. We are living in these days. What should we do? Are we here only to have a good living? Are we even here only to have some good meetings? We are here for nothing but to work out His eternal economy, to build up the Body of Christ for the increase and spread of His testimony. Only this will build up the bride and end the age. More than ever before, to speak of the Lord's coming is full of meaning and timely. The Lord's coming is not far away; He is around the corner, and His footsteps are heard. Let us bear our responsibility until we meet Him.
We need to desperately practice the vital groups in the church life. Through our trainings and the blending with the saints from Taiwan, the Lord is burdening us to practice the way that Brother Lee spoke to us again and again. In order to carry out the final move of the Lord, we also need many full-timers. It is right for one out of twenty to serve the Lord with their full time. This means that out of about two hundred thousand saints in the Lord's recovery, ten thousand should be full-timers to be the "tape recorders" to preach the high truths, raise up golden lampstands, and practice the vital groups. This is not too much; it is possible to do this. Many, especially the young people, have the heart and the determination to be full-timers to serve the Lord to consummate this age. In the kingdom and the New Jerusalem we will all be full-time; it is better to be full-time sooner. The Lord knows those who have the heart and the burden to do this; He has seen their consecration. Many will serve the Lord lifelong with their full time because of the needs everywhere. Some already have decided to go to Russia and Europe to serve the Lord there. For this purpose, many need to go to the full-time training for two glorious years to be constituted with the Triune God and the high truths so that they can serve the Lord, build up His Body, and consummate this age. At the same time, all the senior saints who cannot join the full-time training must pray for the young saints. If many do this, then to be sure, the Lord's recovery has a bright future.—M. C.

TOP-纲目|Outline|对照-目录
　
　
第十二篇　新耶路撒冷─神永远经纶的终极完成
大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
壹　新耶路撒冷是整个神圣启示的总结，以及整个神圣启示中心并终极完成的意义─启二一2，9～10：
一　新耶路撒冷是圣经整个神圣启示的总结及总和的组成。
二　圣经的一切启示与异象都终极完成于新耶路撒冷。
贰　新耶路撒冷不是一座物质的城，乃是一个生机的构成，由救赎之经过过程并终极完成的三一神与蒙救赎、变化、并荣化之三部分人所构成，作终极完成之三一神的生机体，使祂借着得荣之三部分人，得着永远的扩大和彰显：
一　新耶路撒冷是由旧约和新约所有的圣徒组成，他们建造在一起，作神永远的建筑。
二　新耶路撒冷是所有蒙救赎、重生、变化、荣化之三部分人，与经过过程并终极完成之三一神的调和。
三　新耶路撒冷是经过过程并终极完成之三一神终极的显出，使祂得着彰显，直到永远。
叁　新耶路撒冷是一个表号─是圣经中最大并终极的表号（启一1）─表征神在旧造里、在各时代中，新造工作之结果的集大成：
一　神在列祖时代在列祖身上的工作。
二　神在律法时代在以色列人身上的工作。
三　神在恩典时代在新约信徒身上的工作。
四　神在公义时代在得救的以色列人，和其余尚未得成全的新约信徒身上的工作。
肆　新耶路撒冷是神经纶终极的目标：
一　神只有一个终极的目标─新耶路撒冷，作神的扩大、扩展和彰显。
二　根据新约的整个启示，基督徒工作的惟一目标该是新耶路撒冷：
１　新耶路撒冷是使徒们生活与工作的最高点。
２　我们必须以神永远经纶的目标─新耶路撒冷─为我们惟一并终极的目标。
伍　新耶路撒冷是照着使徒的教训建造的：
一　新耶路撒冷的十二根基上，有羔羊十二使徒的名字，代表使徒的教训─启二一14，徒二42。
二　使徒的教训是神在新约中的整个说话，论到神新约的经纶，就是要得着一个神人二性联结调和的宇宙合并。
三　新耶路撒冷是建造在使徒和申言者，以及他们从基督所领受作为磐石的启示上─太十六18，弗二20，三4～5。
四　我们必须坚定持续并紧紧跟随使徒的教训，以建造基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷─提后三10，14，二2，多一9。
陆　新耶路撒冷是神完整救恩的具体表现：
一　神完整的救恩，乃是以神的义为基础，并以神的生命为完成所组成─罗五18，八10。
二　新耶路撒冷的根基是神的义和神的信实，其完成是神的生命和神的性情。
三　整个新耶路撒冷乃是生命建造在神义之根基上的事。
柒　新耶路撒冷是在上的耶路撒冷，属天的耶路撒冷，是信徒之母─加四26，来十二22：
一　在上的耶路撒冷作信徒之母，乃是恩典的新约，由撒拉所象征。
二　新耶路撒冷是由经过过程之三一神分赐到信徒里面作恩典所产生的，好将他们生为许多儿子，组成新耶路撒冷，（启二一7，）就是他们的母。─引用经文
三　父（恩典的源头）、恩典、母、众子、城和新约，要成为一个实体─新耶路撒冷。
捌　新耶路撒冷是神圣儿子名分的总和─启二一7：
一　新耶路撒冷是神众子的组合，他们有神的生命和性情，承受了经过过程之三一神的一切所是。
二　启示录二十一章七节，是新约中关于儿子名分整个启示的总结：
１　神预定我们得儿子的名分─弗一5。
２　我们原是罪人，但我们已经被神作成众子，并被模成神长子的形像─罗八29。
３ 神正在领许多儿子进荣耀里去─来二10。
４　因此，新约启示，神的心意是要产生众子，并启示新耶路撒冷乃是神圣儿子名分的总和。
玖　新耶路撒冷是涌流之三一神的目的─约四14下：
一　约翰四章十四节下半说，“我所赐的水，要在他里面成为泉源，直涌入永远的生命”：
１　“涌入”（即罗马五章二十一节的“得”，直译，以至于）说到目的，指明永远的生命是涌流之三一神的目的。
２　永远的生命至终要成为新耶路撒冷，就是神圣生命的总和；因此，“涌入永远的生命”意思是“归入新耶路撒冷”。
二　新耶路撒冷是神在三个阶段涌流的结果：父的阶段、子的阶段、灵的阶段：
１　父是源，就是源头；子是泉，灵是涌流的河，这个涌流的结果是永远的生命，就是新耶路撒冷。
２　“源”涌现，“泉”涌出，这涌出乃是流，也就是河，涌成新耶路撒冷。
拾　新耶路撒冷是帐幕也是殿，乃是救赎之神和蒙祂救赎之人相互的居所─启二一2～3，22：
一　帐幕是神所救赎的人，殿是救赎的神:
１　帐幕主要是用神所救赎之人的人性建造的，作神的居所。
２　殿主要用神性建造的，作神所救赎之人的居所。
二　新耶路撒冷是神与蒙祂救赎之人的调和，而这调和乃是相互的居所。
三　经过过程之三一神与蒙祂救赎的人，乃是一个调和的实体，直到永远。
拾壹　新耶路撒冷是宇宙的对偶─“永世对偶”─神圣罗曼史的完成─启二二17：
一　按其人性说，新耶路撒冷是羔羊那人性的妻子（有神圣的生命和性情）─启二一2，9。
二　按其神性说，新耶路撒冷是蒙神救赎之选民那神性的丈夫（救赎的神, 在祂终极完成之具体化身基督里，有祂的人性生命和性情）。
三　启示录二十二章十七节指明，基督与作祂妻子的新耶路撒冷乃是宇宙的对偶，直到永远：
１　那是经过过程之三一神总和的那灵，与那些如今已完全成熟、作祂新妇的信徒成为一。
２　经过过程之三一神的终极完成，与蒙祂拣选、救赎、重生、变化之人的终极完成，成为宇宙的对偶，彰显三一神直到永远。
拾贰　新耶路撒冷是神与人终极的合并─经过过程并终极完成之三一神，与蒙祂救赎、重生、变化、并荣化之选民，合并成为一个合并：
一　神的心意是要所有在基督里的信徒都合并到神自己的合并里，成为一个扩大、神人二性的合并。
二　圣经向我们揭示，神的经纶是要将神与人合并成为一个合并，这个合并先是基督的身体，然后是新耶路撒冷。
三　经过过程并终极完成之三一神与重生信徒之联结、调和与合并，终极完成为新耶路撒冷。
参读　使徒的教训，第一篇、第十二篇；新耶路撒冷的解释应用于寻求的信徒；圣经中的基本启示，第八至十一章；新约总论，第二五四至二六四篇；约翰福音结晶读经，第十四篇（中文尚未出书）；长老训练第二册：主恢复的异象，第五至十三章；神人，第四至六章；神新约的经纶，下册（第二十六至四十四章）；如何作同工与长老，并如何履行同工与长老的义务，第三篇；基督为父用神圣的荣耀所荣耀的结果，第四至五章；以赛亚书生命读经，第四十七篇。

TOP-大纲|Outline|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
GENERAL SUBJECT
The Crucial Contents of God's New Testament Economy
Message Twelve
The New Jerusalem—the Consummation of God's Eternal Economy
纲目|对照-听抄-目录
I.　The New Jerusalem is the conclusion of the entire divine revelation and the central and ultimate consummated significance of the entire divine revelation—Rev. 21:2, 9-10:
A.　The New Jerusalem is the conclusion and the total composition of the entire revelation of the Bible.
B.　All the revelations and visions of the Scriptures consummate in the New Jerusalem.
II.　The New Jerusalem is not a physical city but an organic constitution constituted with the redeeming processed and consummated Triune God with the redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified tripartite man as an organism of the consummated Triune God for His eternal enlargement and expression through the glorified tripartite man:
A.　The New Jerusalem is the composition of all the Old Testament and New Testament saints built together as God's eternal building.
B.　The New Jerusalem is the mingling of all the redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified tripartite men with the processed and consummated Triune God.
C.　The New Jerusalem is the ultimate manifestation of the processed and consummated Triune God for His expression for eternity.
III.　The New Jerusalem is a sign—the greatest and ultimate sign in the Scriptures (Rev. 1:1)—of the aggregate of God's work of the new creation in all the dispensations within the old creation:
A.　God's work in the dispensation of the patriarchs on the patriarchs.
B.　God's work in the dispensation of the law on the children of Israel.
C.　God's work in the dispensation of grace on the New Testament believers.
D.　God's work in the dispensation of righteousness on the saved Israelites and on the rest of the New Testament believers not yet perfected.
IV.　The New Jerusalem is the ultimate goal of God's economy:
A.　God has only one ultimate goal—the New Jerusalem, God's enlargement, expansion, and expression.
B.　According to the entire revelation of the New Testament, the unique goal of the Christian work should be the New Jerusalem:
1.　The New Jerusalem was the highest point of the apostles' living and work.
2.　We must take the goal of God's eternal economy—the New Jerusalem—as our unique and ultimate goal.
V.　The New Jerusalem is built according to the apostles' teaching:
A.　The twelve foundations of the New Jerusalem bear the names of the twelve apostles of the Lamb, representing the apostles' teaching—Rev. 21:14; Acts 2:42.
B.　The teaching of the apostles is the entire speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament economy, which is to gain a universal incorporation of the union and mingling of divinity with humanity.
C.　The New Jerusalem is built upon the apostles and prophets with their revelation received of Christ as the rock—Matt. 16:18; Eph. 2:20; 3:4-5.
D.　We need to continue steadfastly in and closely follow the apostles' teaching to build up the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem—2 Tim. 3:10, 14; 2:2; Titus 1:9.
VI.　The New Jerusalem is the embodiment of God's complete salvation:
A.　God's complete salvation is a composition of God's righteousness as the base and God's life as the consummation—Rom. 5:18; 8:10.
B.　The foundation of the New Jerusalem is the righteousness of God with God's faithfulness, and the consummation is God's life with God's nature.
C.　The entire New Jerusalem is a matter of life built on the foundation of God's righteousness.
VII.　The New Jerusalem is the Jerusalem above, the heavenly Jerusalem, the mother of the believers—Gal. 4:26; Heb. 12:22:
A.　The Jerusalem above as the mother of the believers is the new covenant of grace symbolized by Sarah.
B.　The New Jerusalem is produced by the dispensing of the processed Triune God into the believers as grace to bring them forth as the many sons to compose the New Jerusalem (Rev. 21:7), which is their mother.
C.　The Father (the source of grace), the grace, the mother, the sons, the city, and the new covenant will become one entity—the New Jerusalem.
VIII.　The New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine sonship—Rev. 21:7:
A.　The New Jerusalem is a composition of all the sons of God, who have God's life and nature and who inherit all that the processed Triune God is.
B.　In Revelation 21:7 we have the conclusion of the entire revelation in the New Testament concerning sonship:
1.　God predestinated us unto sonship—Eph. 1:5.
2.　We were sinners, but we have been made sons by God and are being conformed to the image of God's firstborn Son—Rom. 8:29.
3.　God is leading many sons into glory—Heb. 2:10.
4.　Hence, the New Testament reveals that God's intention is to produce sons and that the New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine sonship.
IX.　The New Jerusalem is the destination of the flowing Triune God—John 4:14b:
A.　John 4:14b says, "The water that I will give him will become in him a spring of water gushing up into eternal life":
1.　Into?speaks of destination, indicating that eternal life is the destination of the flowing Triune God.
2.　The eternal life eventually will become the New Jerusalem, the totality of the divine life; hence,?into eternal life?means?into the New Jerusalem.
B.　The New Jerusalem is the issue of God's flowing in three stages: in the Father's stage, in the Son's stage, and in the Spirit's stage:
1.　The Father is the fountain as the source, the Son is the spring, the Spirit is the flowing river, and this flowing issues in the eternal life, which is the New Jerusalem.
2.　The fountain emerges, the spring gushes, and the gushing is the flowing as a river into the New Jerusalem.
X.　The New Jerusalem, which is both the tabernacle and the temple, is a mutual dwelling place for the redeeming God and His redeemed—Rev. 21:2-3, 22:
A.　The tabernacle is God's redeemed, and the temple is the redeeming God:
1.　The tabernacle is built mostly with the humanity of God's redeemed to be God's dwelling place.
2.　The temple is built mostly with divinity to be the dwelling place of God's redeemed.
B.　The New Jerusalem is the mingling of God with His redeemed, and this mingling is a mutual dwelling place.
C.　The processed Triune God and His redeemed will be one mingled entity for eternity.
XI.　The New Jerusalem is a universal couple—"a loving pair eternally"—the consummation of the divine romance—Rev. 22:17:
A.　According to its humanity the New Jerusalem is the human wife (with the divine life and nature) of the Lamb—Rev. 21:2, 9.
B.　According to its divinity the New Jerusalem is the divine Husband (the redeeming God in His consummated embodiment, Christ, with His human life and nature) of God's redeemed elect.
C.　Revelation 22:17 indicates that Christ and the New Jerusalem as His wife will be a universal couple for eternity:
1.　The Spirit, who is the totality of the processed Triune God, becomes one with the believers, who are now fully matured to be the bride.
2.　The consummation of the processed Triune God and the consummation of God's chosen, redeemed, regenerated, and transformed people will be a universal couple expressing the Triune God for eternity.
XII.　The New Jerusalem is the consummate incorporation of God and man—the processed and consummated Triune God incorporated into an incorporation with His redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified elect:
A.　God's intention is that all the believers in Christ would be incorporated into Himself as an incorporation to be an enlarged, divine and human incorporation.
B.　The Bible unveils to us that God's economy is to have God and man incorporated into an incorporation, which is first the Body of Christ and then the New Jerusalem.
C.　The union, mingling, and incorporation of the processed and consummated Triune God with the regenerated believers consummates as the New Jerusalem.

TOP-纲目|对照-听抄-目录
　
　
第十二篇　新耶路撒冷─神永远经纶的终极完成
The New Jerusalem—the Consummation of God's Eternal Economy
纲目|outline-听抄-目录
壹　新耶路撒冷是整个神圣启示的总结，以及整个神圣启示中心并终极完成的意义─启二一2，9～10：
I.　The New Jerusalem is the conclusion of the entire divine revelation and the central and ultimate consummated significance of the entire divine revelation—Rev. 21:2, 9-10:
一　新耶路撒冷是圣经整个神圣启示的总结及总和的组成。
A.　The New Jerusalem is the conclusion and the total composition of the entire revelation of the Bible.
二　圣经的一切启示与异象都终极完成于新耶路撒冷。
B.　All the revelations and visions of the Scriptures consummate in the New Jerusalem.
贰　新耶路撒冷不是一座物质的城，乃是一个生机的构成，由救赎之经过过程并终极完成的三一神与蒙救赎、变化、并荣化之三部分人所构成，作终极完成之三一神的生机体，使祂借着得荣之三部分人，得着永远的扩大和彰显：
II.　The New Jerusalem is not a physical city but an organic constitution constituted with the redeeming processed and consummated Triune God with the redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified tripartite man as an organism of the consummated Triune God for His eternal enlargement and expression through the glorified tripartite man:
一　新耶路撒冷是由旧约和新约所有的圣徒组成，他们建造在一起，作神永远的建筑。
A.　The New Jerusalem is the composition of all the Old Testament and New Testament saints built together as God's eternal building.
二　新耶路撒冷是所有蒙救赎、重生、变化、荣化之三部分人，与经过过程并终极完成之三一神的调和。
B.　The New Jerusalem is the mingling of all the redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified tripartite men with the processed and consummated Triune God.
三　新耶路撒冷是经过过程并终极完成之三一神终极的显出，使祂得着彰显，直到永远。
C.　The New Jerusalem is the ultimate manifestation of the processed and consummated Triune God for His expression for eternity.
叁　新耶路撒冷是一个表号─是圣经中最大并终极的表号（启一1）─表征神在旧造里、在各时代中，新造工作之结果的集大成：
III.　The New Jerusalem is a sign—the greatest and ultimate sign in the Scriptures (Rev. 1:1)—of the aggregate of God's work of the new creation in all the dispensations within the old creation:
一　神在列祖时代在列祖身上的工作。
A.　God's work in the dispensation of the patriarchs on the patriarchs.
二　神在律法时代在以色列人身上的工作。
B.　God's work in the dispensation of the law on the children of Israel.
三　神在恩典时代在新约信徒身上的工作。
C.　God's work in the dispensation of grace on the New Testament believers.
四　神在公义时代在得救的以色列人，和其余尚未得成全的新约信徒身上的工作。
D.　God's work in the dispensation of righteousness on the saved Israelites and on the rest of the New Testament believers not yet perfected.
肆　新耶路撒冷是神经纶终极的目标：
IV.　The New Jerusalem is the ultimate goal of God's economy:
一　神只有一个终极的目标─新耶路撒冷，作神的扩大、扩展和彰显。
A.　God has only one ultimate goal—the New Jerusalem, God's enlargement, expansion, and expression.
二　根据新约的整个启示，基督徒工作的惟一目标该是新耶路撒冷：
B.　According to the entire revelation of the New Testament, the unique goal of the Christian work should be the New Jerusalem:
１　新耶路撒冷是使徒们生活与工作的最高点。
1.　The New Jerusalem was the highest point of the apostles' living and work.
２　我们必须以神永远经纶的目标─新耶路撒冷─为我们惟一并终极的目标。
2.　We must take the goal of God's eternal economy—the New Jerusalem—as our unique and ultimate goal.
伍　新耶路撒冷是照着使徒的教训建造的：
V.　The New Jerusalem is built according to the apostles' teaching:
一　新耶路撒冷的十二根基上，有羔羊十二使徒的名字，代表使徒的教训─启二一14，徒二42。
A.　The twelve foundations of the New Jerusalem bear the names of the twelve apostles of the Lamb, representing the apostles' teaching—Rev. 21:14; Acts 2:42.
二　使徒的教训是神在新约中的整个说话，论到神新约的经纶，就是要得着一个神人二性联结调和的宇宙合并。
B.　The teaching of the apostles is the entire speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament economy, which is to gain a universal incorporation of the union and mingling of divinity with humanity.
三　新耶路撒冷是建造在使徒和申言者，以及他们从基督所领受作为磐石的启示上─太十六18，弗二20，三4～5。
C.　The New Jerusalem is built upon the apostles and prophets with their revelation received of Christ as the rock—Matt. 16:18; Eph. 2:20; 3:4-5.
四　我们必须坚定持续并紧紧跟随使徒的教训，以建造基督的身体，终极完成新耶路撒冷─提后三10，14，二2，多一9。
D.　We need to continue steadfastly in and closely follow the apostles' teaching to build up the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem—2 Tim. 3:10, 14; 2:2; Titus 1:9.
陆　新耶路撒冷是神完整救恩的具体表现：
VI.　The New Jerusalem is the embodiment of God's complete salvation:
一　神完整的救恩，乃是以神的义为基础，并以神的生命为完成所组成─罗五18，八10。
A.　God's complete salvation is a composition of God's righteousness as the base and God's life as the consummation—Rom. 5:18; 8:10.
二　新耶路撒冷的根基是神的义和神的信实，其完成是神的生命和神的性情。
B.　The foundation of the New Jerusalem is the righteousness of God with God's faithfulness, and the consummation is God's life with God's nature.
三　整个新耶路撒冷乃是生命建造在神义之根基上的事。
C.　The entire New Jerusalem is a matter of life built on the foundation of God's righteousness.
柒　新耶路撒冷是在上的耶路撒冷，属天的耶路撒冷，是信徒之母─加四26，来十二22：
VII.　The New Jerusalem is the Jerusalem above, the heavenly Jerusalem, the mother of the believers—Gal. 4:26; Heb. 12:22:
一　在上的耶路撒冷作信徒之母，乃是恩典的新约，由撒拉所象征。
A.　The Jerusalem above as the mother of the believers is the new covenant of grace symbolized by Sarah.
二　新耶路撒冷是由经过过程之三一神分赐到信徒里面作恩典所产生的，好将他们生为许多儿子，组成新耶路撒冷，（启二一7，）就是他们的母。─引用经文
B.　The New Jerusalem is produced by the dispensing of the processed Triune God into the believers as grace to bring them forth as the many sons to compose the New Jerusalem (Rev. 21:7), which is their mother.
三　父（恩典的源头）、恩典、母、众子、城和新约，要成为一个实体─新耶路撒冷。
C.　The Father (the source of grace), the grace, the mother, the sons, the city, and the new covenant will become one entity—the New Jerusalem.
捌　新耶路撒冷是神圣儿子名分的总和─启二一7：
VIII.　The New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine sonship—Rev. 21:7:
一　新耶路撒冷是神众子的组合，他们有神的生命和性情，承受了经过过程之三一神的一切所是。
A.　The New Jerusalem is a composition of all the sons of God, who have God's life and nature and who inherit all that the processed Triune God is.
二　启示录二十一章七节，是新约中关于儿子名分整个启示的总结：
B.　In Revelation 21:7 we have the conclusion of the entire revelation in the New Testament concerning sonship:
１　神预定我们得儿子的名分─弗一5。
1.　God predestinated us unto sonship—Eph. 1:5.
２　我们原是罪人，但我们已经被神作成众子，并被模成神长子的形像─罗八29。
2.　We were sinners, but we have been made sons by God and are being conformed to the image of God's firstborn Son—Rom. 8:29.
３ 神正在领许多儿子进荣耀里去─来二10。
3.　God is leading many sons into glory—Heb. 2:10.
４　因此，新约启示，神的心意是要产生众子，并启示新耶路撒冷乃是神圣儿子名分的总和。
4.　Hence, the New Testament reveals that God's intention is to produce sons and that the New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine sonship.
玖　新耶路撒冷是涌流之三一神的目的─约四14下：
IX.　The New Jerusalem is the destination of the flowing Triune God—John 4:14b:
一　约翰四章十四节下半说，“我所赐的水，要在他里面成为泉源，直涌入永远的生命”：
A.　John 4:14b says, "The water that I will give him will become in him a spring of water gushing up into eternal life":
１　“涌入”（即罗马五章二十一节的“得”，直译，以至于）说到目的，指明永远的生命是涌流之三一神的目的。
1.　Into?speaks of destination, indicating that eternal life is the destination of the flowing Triune God.
２　永远的生命至终要成为新耶路撒冷，就是神圣生命的总和；因此，“涌入永远的生命”意思是“归入新耶路撒冷”。
2.　The eternal life eventually will become the New Jerusalem, the totality of the divine life; hence,?into eternal life?means?into the New Jerusalem.
二　新耶路撒冷是神在三个阶段涌流的结果：父的阶段、子的阶段、灵的阶段：
B.　The New Jerusalem is the issue of God's flowing in three stages: in the Father's stage, in the Son's stage, and in the Spirit's stage:
１　父是源，就是源头；子是泉，灵是涌流的河，这个涌流的结果是永远的生命，就是新耶路撒冷。
1.　The Father is the fountain as the source, the Son is the spring, the Spirit is the flowing river, and this flowing issues in the eternal life, which is the New Jerusalem.
２　“源”涌现，“泉”涌出，这涌出乃是流，也就是河，涌成新耶路撒冷。
2.　The fountain emerges, the spring gushes, and the gushing is the flowing as a river into the New Jerusalem.
拾　新耶路撒冷是帐幕也是殿，乃是救赎之神和蒙祂救赎之人相互的居所─启二一2～3，22：
X.　The New Jerusalem, which is both the tabernacle and the temple, is a mutual dwelling place for the redeeming God and His redeemed—Rev. 21:2-3, 22:
一　帐幕是神所救赎的人，殿是救赎的神:
A.　The tabernacle is God's redeemed, and the temple is the redeeming God:
１　帐幕主要是用神所救赎之人的人性建造的，作神的居所。
1.　The tabernacle is built mostly with the humanity of God's redeemed to be God's dwelling place.
２　殿主要用神性建造的，作神所救赎之人的居所。
2.　The temple is built mostly with divinity to be the dwelling place of God's redeemed.
二　新耶路撒冷是神与蒙祂救赎之人的调和，而这调和乃是相互的居所。
B.　The New Jerusalem is the mingling of God with His redeemed, and this mingling is a mutual dwelling place.
三　经过过程之三一神与蒙祂救赎的人，乃是一个调和的实体，直到永远。
C.　The processed Triune God and His redeemed will be one mingled entity for eternity.
拾壹　新耶路撒冷是宇宙的对偶─“永世对偶”─神圣罗曼史的完成─启二二17：
XI.　The New Jerusalem is a universal couple—"a loving pair eternally"—the consummation of the divine romance—Rev. 22:17:
一　按其人性说，新耶路撒冷是羔羊那人性的妻子（有神圣的生命和性情）─启二一2，9。
A.　According to its humanity the New Jerusalem is the human wife (with the divine life and nature) of the Lamb—Rev. 21:2, 9.
二　按其神性说，新耶路撒冷是蒙神救赎之选民那神性的丈夫（救赎的神, 在祂终极完成之具体化身基督里，有祂的人性生命和性情）。
B.　According to its divinity the New Jerusalem is the divine Husband (the redeeming God in His consummated embodiment, Christ, with His human life and nature) of God's redeemed elect.
三　启示录二十二章十七节指明，基督与作祂妻子的新耶路撒冷乃是宇宙的对偶，直到永远：
C.　Revelation 22:17 indicates that Christ and the New Jerusalem as His wife will be a universal couple for eternity:
１　那是经过过程之三一神总和的那灵，与那些如今已完全成熟、作祂新妇的信徒成为一。
1.　The Spirit, who is the totality of the processed Triune God, becomes one with the believers, who are now fully matured to be the bride.
２　经过过程之三一神的终极完成，与蒙祂拣选、救赎、重生、变化之人的终极完成，成为宇宙的对偶，彰显三一神直到永远。
2.　The consummation of the processed Triune God and the consummation of God's chosen, redeemed, regenerated, and transformed people will be a universal couple expressing the Triune God for eternity.
拾贰　新耶路撒冷是神与人终极的合并─经过过程并终极完成之三一神，与蒙祂救赎、重生、变化、并荣化之选民，合并成为一个合并：
XII.　The New Jerusalem is the consummate incorporation of God and man—the processed and consummated Triune God incorporated into an incorporation with His redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified elect:
一　神的心意是要所有在基督里的信徒都合并到神自己的合并里，成为一个扩大、神人二性的合并。
A.　God's intention is that all the believers in Christ would be incorporated into Himself as an incorporation to be an enlarged, divine and human incorporation.
二　圣经向我们揭示，神的经纶是要将神与人合并成为一个合并，这个合并先是基督的身体，然后是新耶路撒冷。
B.　The Bible unveils to us that God's economy is to have God and man incorporated into an incorporation, which is first the Body of Christ and then the New Jerusalem.
三　经过过程并终极完成之三一神与重生信徒之联结、调和与合并，终极完成为新耶路撒冷。
C.　The union, mingling, and incorporation of the processed and consummated Triune God with the regenerated believers consummates as the New Jerusalem.

TOP-纲目|outline-听抄-目录
　
　
MESSAGE TWELVE
THE NEW JERUSALEM—THE CONSUMMATION OF GOD'S ETERNAL ECONOMY
纲目|Outline|对照-目录
（本文为英文听抄扫描所得，未经校对）
In this series of messages, the Lord has brought us step by step and level by level to the ultimate consummation of God's eternal economy, the New Jerusalem. The Lord has opened up the vision of the New Jerusalem to His recovery. Since the 1980s, Brother Lee expounded the New Jerusalem a number of times, and all the more in the last few years. He spoke much about the New Jerusalem as the Lord opened more and more light to him. We need to read the books of the ministry and study the New Jerusalem. It is a subject which has eluded the understanding of Christians for centuries. Perhaps never in history has it been opened up as it is today. We are so blessed that the New Jerusalem has been opened up to the Lord's recovery. It is no longer a mystery that we cannot understand, and we are no longer misguided by a wrong understanding of it.
THE CONCLUSION OF THE ENTIRE DIVINE REVELATION AND THE CENTRAL AND ULTIMATE CONSUMMATED SIGNIFICANCE OF THE ENTIRE DIVINE REVELATION
The New Jerusalem is the conclusion of the entire divine revelation and the central and ultimate consummated significance of the entire divine revelation (Rev. 21:2, 9-10). The conclusion is the last and deciding word. The conclusion, the last word, of the Bible tells us that the entire divine revelation relates to the New Jerusalem. Sometimes a college student changes his major several times because he does not know what he is going to be. If someone could know the future and let him know what his end will be, the student could save much time and finish school more quickly. We praise the Lord that someone has told us the end of the Bible. The end is the New Jerusalem. Knowing this should save us time and save us from unnecessary detours in useless directions.
It is never too late to be an overcomer, and it is never too early to drop what is not in the consummation. We should not wait to drop whatever does not fit in the New Jerusalem. For this purpose, we all need to be clear about what the New Jerusalem is. The New Jerusalem is the conclusion of the entire revelation of the Bible. The Bible has many significances. It is significant as history, as poetry, and as teaching, but these significances are all peripheral. The central and ultimate consummated significance of the entire divine revelation is the New Jerusalem. All the revelations and visions of the Scriptures consummate in the New Jerusalem. In this sense, the New Jerusalem defines the whole Bible. If we see the New Jerusalem, we see the whole Bible; we grasp the central and consummated significance of what the Bible is all about.
AN ORGANIC CONSTITUTION AS AN ORGANISM OF THE CONSUMMATED TRIUNE GOD
The New Jerusalem is not a physical city but an organic constitution constituted with the redeeming processed and consummated Triune God with the redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified tripartite man as an organism of the consummated Triune God for His eternal enlargement and expression through the glorified tripartite man. Even though the record in Revelation describes a city with walls, gold, and precious stones, the key to understanding the New Jerusalem is Revelation 1:1. In this verse the apostle John tells us that everything he saw in this book is a sign. A sign is a symbol with spiritual significance. Everything that the apostle spoke of in Revelation is a sign. In this book, the Lord Jesus is called the Lamb. This does not mean that He has four legs and a coat of wool. Likewise, Christ is the Lion, but He is not literally a wild animal. No one would interpret the Bible in this way. Therefore, to interpret Revelation literally and physically is ludicrous. If we would not interpret the signs of Christ in the book of Revelation in a physical sense, how can we interpret the New Jerusalem in a physical sense? We should be consistent. If Christ is not a four-legged lamb, the New Jerusalem cannot be a physical city.
Not only is the New Jerusalem not a physical city; it is also not a place to which we can go, much less a place to which we go after we die. Many religions of the world believe in a place people go to after they die. It is reputed to be a happy place. This is true of Buddhism, and the American Indians also spoke of the happy hunting ground. Unfortunately, Christians have borrowed these pagan concepts to interpret the divine Word of God. This is pitiful! The New Jerusalem is not a physical place to which we will go to be in a state of bliss after we die.　Rather, it is an organic constitution, constituted with the redeeming processed and consummated Triune God and the redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified tripartite man as an organism of the consummated Triune God for His eternal enlargement and expression through the glorified tripartite man. Organic refers to something of life. The New Jerusalem is not lifeless. It is something entirely of life, and as we have seen, this life is not the bios life or the psuche life but the zoe life. The New Jerusalem is organic in the sense that it is entirely of the divine life.
The New Jerusalem is not only organic, but it is a constitution. Constitution implies a process. The New Jerusalem is the composition of all the Old Testament and New Testament saints built together as Gods eternal building. Composition indicates that it is composed of more than one element or constituent. Moreover, it is constituted by mingling. The New Jerusalem is the mingling of all the redeemed, regenerated, transformed, and glorified tripartite men with the processed and consummated Triune God. The New Jerusalem is the ultimate manifestation of the processed and consummated Triune God for His expression for eternity. The Triune God has been seeking this.
A SIGN OF THE AGGREGATE OF GOD'S WORK OF THE NEW CREATION IN ALL THE DISPENSATIONS WITHIN THE OLD CREATION
The New Jerusalem is a sign—the greatest and ultimate sign in the Scriptures (Rev. 1:1)—of the aggregate of God's work of the new creation in all the dispensations within the old creation. Throughout the dispensations of the old creation God has been doing one work, which is to create a new creation out of the old creation. In the Bible, what is old and what is new have nothing to do with the passing of time. The old creation is old not only because it has been around for a long time, and the new creation is not new simply because it was recently created. To have this concept is to miss the meaning of old and new in the Bible. What is old is simply what is devoid of God, and what is new is God Himself. For example, the church is the new man because in it Christ is all and in all. If Christ were not all and in all, the church would be the old man. Something is new only if God is in it. Hymns, #16, a masterpiece written by Brother Lee, is for the worship of the Father for His newness. Even in our hymnbook, this is the only hymn on the subject of the Father's newness. The second stanza and the chorus say, wO Thou art God, and Thou art "new"; / Without Thee all is worn, / But all with Thee is ever fresh, / Though many years have gone. / O Father, Thou art unchanging, / Thou never hast grown old; / Thru countless ages, ever fresh, / Thy newness doth unfold." The passage of time does not make God old; it simply affords Him the opportunity to keep unfolding His newness. Because God is new, if we are without God, we are old. Out of the old creation which God created, God wants to gain a new creation. In other words, He wants to have a creation with Himself constituted, mingled, and incorporated into it.
The old creation in which God works has four dispensations, which are not only periods of time but ways in which God deals with people in those particular periods. The New Jerusalem is the result of God's work in the dispensation of the patriarchs on the patriarchs. It is also the result of God's work in the dispensation of the law on the children of Israel, which lasted from the giving of the law until the coming of Christ. It is the result of God's work in the dispensation of grace on the New Testament believers in the age of the mystery of the church. This is the period in which the greater part of the New Jerusalem is produced. It is also the result of God's work in the dispensation of righteousness on the saved Israelites and on the rest of the New Testament believers not yet perfected. Through all these dispensations God is working on the man that He created in order to gain a new creation. This new creation is the New Jerusalem.
THE ULTIMATE GOAL OF GOD'S ECONOMY
The New Jerusalem is the ultimate goal of God's economy. God has only one ultimate goal—the New Jerusalem, God's enlargement, expansion, and expression. According to the entire revelation of the New Testament, the unique goal of the Christian work should be the New Jerusalem. The New Jerusalem was the highest point of the apostles' living and work, and we must take the goal of God's eternal economy—the New Jerusalem—as our unique and ultimate goal. Concerning this, please refer to the messages entitled "The New Jerusalem—the Highest Point of the Apostles' Living and Work" (The Ministry Magazine, vol. 1, no. 1). These messages convey much light concerning the way to live out and work out the New Jerusalem. Our living today must be the living of the New Jerusalem. Because the New Jerusalem is the constitution of the processed and consummated Triune God with His elect, our living today must be a triune living of the Father, the Son, and the Spirit. If we have any other goal for our work, it is not the work of God.
BEING BUILT ACCORDING TO THE APOSTLES' TEACHING
The New Jerusalem is built according to the apostles' teaching. The apostles' teaching is the unique, divine revelation of God's New Testament economy from the incarnation of God to the consummation of the New Jerusalem carried out by the full ministry of Christ in three divine and mystical stages for the fulfillment of God's eternal economy. The twelve foundations of the New Jerusalem bear the names of the twelve apostles of the Lamb, representing the apostles' teaching (Rev. 21:14; Acts 2:42). The twelve foundations do not refer to the persons of the twelve apostles but to the grace of the New Testament, with the emphasis on the teaching of the apostles. The persons of the apostles have departed; they are no longer with us. However, the teaching of the apostles, which is the New Testament ministry, the unique divine revelation of God's New Testament economy, is very much with us. Our building today must be on the foundation of the apostles' teaching.
The teaching of the apostles is the entire speaking of God in the New Testament concerning God's New Testament economy, which is to gain a universal incorporation of the union and mingling of divinity with humanity. The New Jerusalem is built upon the apostles and prophets with their revelation received of Christ as the rock (Matt. 16:18; Eph. 2:20; 3:4-5). We need to continue steadfastly in and closely follow the apostles' teaching to build up the Body of Christ to consummate the New Jerusalem (2 Tim. 3:10, 14; 2:2; Titus 1:9). We all have benefited from the ministry of our Brother Lee, and we have much affection for this ministry. We are not opposing this ministry as some are to their own detriment. However, it is not adequate to feel an affection for the ministry; we must also be constituted with the ministry. There is a real difference between affection and constitution. It is good to love the ministry, buy the books of the ministry, and come to all the conferences and trainings, but how much is this ministry constituted into us? When we speak something for God, whether it is preaching the gospel to a new one or shepherding and ministering to the saints in need, how much of the high peak of the truth in the ministry comes out of us? Many of us are short in this regard. May the Lord turn us! Now that our brother is no longer among us, we must be all the more desperate to dive into the ministry and be constituted with it so that our whole being, thinking, concept, and living, the way we see the Word of God, and how we conduct ourselves would be adjusted to reflect the apostles' teaching. The apostles' teaching is the foundation of the New Jerusalem. If we say we mean business for the New Jerusalem but do not pay attention to being constituted with the apostles' teaching, we are fooling ourselves; to us the New Jerusalem is nothing but a dream. To be sure, if our living and work today are to result in the consummation of the New Jerusalem, we need to be constituted with the apostles' teaching. May none of us take this matter lightly; rather, may we take it to heart. We all should be constituted with the apostles' teaching and speak the apostles' teaching to one another. Those who take the lead in the churches should take the lead to follow the apostles' teaching. This will lay a very good foundation for the consummating of the New Jerusalem.
THE EMBODIMENT OF GOD'S COMPLETE SALVATION
The New Jerusalem is the embodiment of God's complete salvation. God's complete salvation is a composition of God's righteousness as the base and God's life as the consummation (Rom. 5:18; 8:10). The foundation of the New Jerusalem is the righteousness of God with God's faithfulness, and the consummation is God's life with God's nature. The entire New Jerusalem is a matter of life built on the foundation of God's righteousness. As we have seen, God's complete salvation is of two parts: His judicial redemption and His organic salvation. The totality of God's complete salvation is the New Jerusalem. The foundation of the New Jerusalem speaks of God's righteousness with His faithfulness. The foundation is composed of twelve precious stones, the colors of which are like a rainbow. In the Bible the rainbow signifies God's faithfulness, which is based on His righteousness. In our experience today we need to rely on God's judicial redemption: the forgiveness and the cleansing of our sins, positional sanctification, justification, and reconciliation to God. We will never graduate from this. It is a solid foundation for us to experience the organic part of God's salvation. Righteousness is the foundation of life, and life is the consummation of righteousness.
The entire New Jerusalem portrays something of life. As a picture of life, it shows us that God's salvation has life as its consummation. The river of life reaches every part of the city, and in the midst of and on either side of the river is the tree of life. The organic aspect of salvation begins with regeneration as the entrance into the New Jerusalem, and it continues with feeding, signified by the tree of life and the water of life. Organic salvation also includes renewing, which makes us new as the New Jerusalem, and dispositional sanctification, which is the imparting or God's divine nature into us to make us holy as the holy city. It also includes transformation, which makes us the precious stones good for the building of the wall, and it includes our building up. It includes conformation to conform us to the image of Christ. Revelation 21:11 says that the light of the city is like a jasper stone, which signifies the One who sits on the throne (4:3). Conformation is for us to fully bear the image of the One on the throne. Finally, organic salvation includes glorification as the final step of God's organic salvation to bring us fully into glory in the New Jerusalem, which has the glory of God. As we experience God's complete salvation in both the judicial and organic aspects, we are living a life which consummates the New Jerusalem.—G. C.
THE JERUSALEM ABOVE, THE HEAVENLY JERUSALEM, THE MOTHER OF THE BELIEVERS
We should consider whether we are satisfied with what we have seen concerning the New Jerusalem. Is it old knowledge to us, a "local church theology"? The New Jerusalem was an overwhelming revelation to Brother Nee and a controlling vision to Brother Lee. Is it the same to us? We are not here to teach anything new, but there is much that has already been spoken that we still need to see personally. May the Lord roll away the veils and anoint our eyes with eyesalve that we may really see the New Jerusalem!
The New Jerusalem is the Jerusalem above, the heavenly Jerusalem, the mother of the believers (Gal. 4:26; Heb. 12:22). Few believers know the New Jerusalem in this aspect. Our Father is the Triune God, and our mother is the New Jerusalem. We should honor and appreciate our mother, realizing all that she has done and is still doing to help us grow up as mature sons. In Galatians 4 Paul tells us that there are two mothers. One is typified by Hagar and the earthly Jerusalem. It is the religion of the law that brings forth sons in bondage. The other is the Jerusalem above as the mother of the believers. It is the new covenant of grace symbolized by Sarah (see The Conclusion of the New Testament, msgs. 254-255). The New Jerusalem is the new covenant, the new covenant is our mother, and the mother produces sons by grace. The law makes demands, but grace produces. Grace as a flowing river is the Triune God enjoyed by us. We have been born of the flowing river of the grace of God, and now we go on, not by struggling or by trying to intensify ourselves to be the overcomers, but by taking a daily dose of divine joy by enjoying grace from our mother.
The New Jerusalem is produced by the dispensing of the processed Triune God into the believers as grace to bring them forth as the many sons to compose the New Jerusalem (Rev. 21:7), which is their mother. As humans, we live not only because our father begot us but also because our mother gave birth to us. In the same way, the new covenant of grace brings forth living sons of God. The mother produces the sons, and the sons become the components of the mother. The church brings new ones to salvation to become the children of grace, and the children in turn become part of the very church that produced them.
The Father (the source of grace), the grace, the mother, the sons, the city, and the new covenant will become one entity—the New Jerusalem. The New Jerusalem is many millions of transformed, conformed, glorified, tripartite God-men mingled and blended together with the processed Triune God to be a single entity. As such, it is an organism and a constitution, full of glory, with no darkness, death, envy, sin, self, division, doubt, or devil. There is only God mingled with man as one entity. This will be manifested and presented to the universe, and all created beings will praise the glory of God's grace which produced such an entity.
In the New Jerusalem, we will be lost in a vast constitution of jasper to become a tiny part of redeemed humanity mingled with the Triune God. The Life-study of First and Second Samuel on page 199 says, The New Jerusalem is a composition of divinity and humanity blended and mingled together as one entity. All the components have the same life, nature, and constitution and thus are a corporate person. This is a matter of God becoming man and man becoming God in life and in nature but not in the Godhead. These two, God and man, man and God, are built up together by being blended and mingled together. This is the completion, the consummation, of God's building. We all need to see this vision.
The New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine sonship (Rev. 21:7). The New Jerusalem is a composition of all the sons of God, who have God's life and nature and who inherit all that the processed Triune God is. Strictly speaking, there will be no children of God in the New Jerusalem. Children are not mature enough to be part of the New Jerusalem. Perhaps many of us have a personal goal for our Christian life, which is to gain enough transformation to avoid outer darkness, enter into the millennial kingdom, and be assigned to rule over a small, obscure city. Accordingly, we may pray to be transformed, hope to be transformed, and sing, "Transformation is my need." However, this goal of transformation is too low and too self-centered. God's goal is not merely transformation; it is maturation. There is a practical difference between transformation and maturity. Transformation is to be changed in our natural life, while maturity is to be filled with the divine life that changes us. No parents merely have transformation as the goal for their sons or daughters, as if they could become adults without maturing. It has been our privilege to sit under a ministry that has reached a level of maturity unprecedented since the time of the apostles in the first century. Our brother became a pattern of one not only transformed but matured, filled with God as life. Hebrews 6:1 does not say, "Let us be brought on to transformation"; it says, "Let us be brought on to maturity." Everyone who participates in the New Jerusalem will be a mature, perfected son of God. If we are found immature, we will have to mature during the millennium. Now is the time to mature, and we can mature because we are in the age of intensification. By the Lord's grace in His economy, we can have more God in us when we go to bed tonight than when we rose in the morning. We do not believe in wasting our days and hours. Today is a day to be filled with God, and each day is a day to be matured with the divine life.
In Revelation 21:7 we have the conclusion of the entire revelation in the New Testament concerning sonship. God predestinated us unto sonship (Eph. 1:5). We know what we are going to become when we grow up. We are going to be sons of God. A believer may not agree at this time with the truth of deification, but eventually he will agree with it, because sooner or later he will become God in life and in nature. Sooner or later we have to be made God, so why should it not be sooner, even today? We have been predestinated for this. Why should we rebel against our destiny? Rather, we should hand ourselves over to God and say, "Give me today's growth in life unto maturity."
We were sinners, but we have been made sons by God and are being conformed to the image of God's firstborn Son (Rom. 8:29). God is leading many sons into glory (Heb. 2:10). Hence, the New Testament reveals that God's intention is to produce sons and that the New Jerusalem is the totality of the divine sonship. The New Jerusalem is the aggregate, the totality, of the many God-men. Among these God-men, the sons of God, Christ is the firstborn Son, and we are His many "twins." The New Jerusalem is God the Father with many "God the sons"; it is many millions of sons meeting around the firstborn Son. In a very real sense the New Jerusalem will be an eternal family reunion. Because we are in time and space, the sons are separated. In addition, death, the second greatest force in the universe, comes to us one by one; this also separates us. Many are now sleeping in Paradise, having gone there as overcomers. They will be resurrected and raptured, and we will join together to have a marvelous family reunion as God the Father and "God the sons" meet together for eternity. On the Saturday night before Brother Lee went to be with the Lord, a co-worker visited him in the intensive care room and was given a chance to speak to him, in hope that he was still able to hear. The co-worker repeated what a number of brothers had said to Brother Lee in his study when they had encouraged him and affirmed their commitment to the Lord's recovery: "We will speak these things, we will teach these things, we will write these things, and we will live these things until we meet the Lord." One day we will know if Brother Lee heard these parting words, because we will see him in that great and glorious family reunion.
All the millions of sons of God will be part of a tremendous totality, the New Jerusalem. In the New Jerusalem, we will still be able to recognize one another. We will not be an anonymous mass of jasper, having become God but not knowing who is who. This is too impersonal. God is expressed, but His expression in our being has its various characteristics. In the New Jerusalem our being will not be annulled; the mingling of God with us does not annul our being. Thus, we will still be what we are, and we will be able to identify one another even in eternity. Our God-created humanity will be deified and saturated with God to express God, but our being will remain forever to express God in what we are.
The New Jerusalem is the destination of the flowing Triune God (John 4:14b). Our God is a mighty flowing out! He is the source of life, divine and rich and free. He is the "river whose streams gladden the city of God" (Psa. 46:4). The New Jerusalem as the destination of the flowing Triune God is one of the most precious revelations released recently (see Crystallization-study of the Gospel of John, msg. 14), but to some degree it may remain veiled to us. John 4:14b says, "The water that I will give him will become in him a spring of water gushing up into eternal life." According to the natural concept and the natural apprehension of the Bible, the flowing Triune God and the New Jerusalem are not mentioned in this verse. It seems to only speak about water and life. However, the whole New Testament economy of God is in this half verse. Into speaks of destination, indicating that eternal life is the destination of the flowing Triune God. The eternal life eventually will become the New Jerusalem, the totality of the divine life. Hence, into eternal life means into the New Jerusalem.
